## 38:1-3 — verses 1-3 (shared commentary)

### Translation

# Tafsir of Surat Sad

[It is] Meccan.

In the name of Allah, the Most Gracious, the Most Merciful.

As for the discussion of the disconnected letters, it has already been dealt with at the beginning of Surat al-Baqarah in a manner sufficient to make repeating it here unnecessary.

His saying, {By the Qur'an, possessor of the dhikr (remembrance/mention)}, means: by the Qur'an which contains within it that which is a remembrance for the servants and a benefit for them in this life and the next.

Al-Dahhak said concerning His saying {possessor of the dhikr}: it is like His saying, {Indeed We have sent down to you a Book in which is your dhikr} [al-Anbiya: 10], meaning your being reminded. Qatadah said likewise, and Ibn Jarir preferred this view.

Ibn Abbas, Sa'id ibn Jubayr, Isma'il ibn Abi Khalid, Ibn Uyaynah, Abu Husayn, Abu Salih, and al-Suddi said: {possessor of the dhikr} means possessor of nobility, that is, possessor of standing and rank.

There is no contradiction between the two views, for it is indeed a noble Book which contains reminder, the establishment of excuse, and warning.

They differed regarding the answer (response clause) to this oath. Some said it is His saying, {None of them did other than deny the messengers, so My punishment was justly deserved} [Sad: 14]. It was also said to be His saying, {Indeed that is surely true: the dispute of the people of the Fire} [Sad: 64]. Ibn Jarir related both of these, but this second view is quite far-fetched, and Ibn Jarir weakened it.

Qatadah said: its answer is {Nay, those who disbelieve are in pride and stubborn opposition}, and Ibn Jarir preferred this.

It was also said that its answer is what the entire context of the surah contains, and Allah knows best.

Ibn Jarir then related from some of the scholars that they said: its answer is "Sad," meaning: truth, real, by the Qur'an possessor of the dhikr.

His saying, {Nay, those who disbelieve are in pride and stubborn opposition} means: indeed in this Qur'an there is a reminder for whoever takes reminder, and a lesson for whoever takes lesson. The disbelievers did not benefit from it only because they are {in pride}, meaning haughty arrogance and stubborn zeal toward it, {and stubborn opposition}, meaning defiance of it, obstinacy, and separation from it.

Then He warned them with what He had destroyed of the nations that denied before them, on account of their opposing the messengers and denying the scriptures sent down from heaven, saying: {How many a generation have We destroyed before them}, meaning how many a denying nation, {and they cried out}, meaning when the punishment came to them they sought help and cried out to Allah. But that availed them nothing, as He Most High said: {But when they perceived Our punishment, behold, they were fleeing from it} [al-Anbiya: 12], meaning they were running away, {Do not flee, and return to that in which you were given luxury, and to your dwellings, so that you may be questioned} [al-Anbiya: 13].

Abu Dawud al-Tayalisi said: Shu'bah narrated to us from Abu Ishaq from al-Tamimi, who said: I asked Ibn Abbas about the saying of Allah, {and they cried out, but it was not the time for escape}. He said: it is not a time of calling out, nor of leaping up, nor of fleeing.

Ali ibn Abi Talhah said, from Ibn Abbas: it is not a time when help can be sought.

Shabib ibn Bishr said, from Ikrimah, from Ibn Abbas: they cried out with a cry at a time when it would not benefit them, and he recited [a line of poetry]:

"Remembering Layla, but it is not the time for remembering."

Muhammad ibn Ka'b said concerning His saying, {and they cried out, but it was not the time for escape}: he means, they called out with the declaration of Divine Oneness when this world had turned away from them, and they sought help through repentance when this world had turned away from them.

Qatadah said: when they saw the punishment they wished for repentance, but not at the time when calling out could avail.

Mujahid said: {and they cried out, but it was not the time for escape} means it is not the time for fleeing nor for a response to be given.

Something similar to this has been related from Ikrimah, Sa'id ibn Jubayr, Abu Malik, al-Dahhak, Zayd ibn Aslam, al-Hasan, and Qatadah.

From Malik, from Zayd ibn Aslam: {but it was not the time for escape} means there is no calling out except at its proper time.

This word, "lata," is the negating "la" to which a "ta" has been added, just as it is added to "thumma" so that they say "thummat," and to "rubba" so that they say "rubbat." It is written separately, and the pause falls upon it. Some have related, from what [Ibn Jarir] mentioned concerning the authoritative written copy, that it is joined to "hina": "wa la ta-hina manas." But the well known form is the first. The majority then read "hina" in the accusative, the meaning being: and the time was not the time of escape. Some permitted the accusative to be governed by "lata" itself, and recited [a line of poetry]:

"Remembering the love of Layla, but there is no time for it now, while gray hair has already cut off the bond of youth."

Some permitted the genitive to be governed by it, and recited:

"They sought reconciliation with us, but it was not the time, so we answered that there is no time remaining for continuance."

Some also recited:

"but no hour of regret,"

with "sa'ah" in the genitive. The people of language say: al-naws means delay, and al-baws means advancing forward. This is why He Most High said, {but it was not the time for escape}, meaning: the time was not a time for fleeing nor for departure.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

تَفْسِيرُ سُورَةِ ص

[وَهِيَ] مَكِّيَّةٌ.

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَنِ الرَّحِيمِ

* *

أَمَّا الْكَلَامُ عَلَى الْحُرُوفِ الْمُقَطَّعَةِ فَقَدْ تَقَدَّمَ فِي أَوَّلِ سُورَةِ "الْبَقَرَةِ" بِمَا أَغْنَى عَنْ إِعَادَتِهِ هَاهُنَا.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَالْقُرْآنِ ذِي الذِّكْرِ﴾ أَيْ: وَالْقُرْآنِ الْمُشْتَمِلِ عَلَى مَا فِيهِ ذِكْرٌ لِلْعِبَادِ وَنَفْعٌ لَهُمْ فِي الْمَعَاشِ وَالْمَعَادِ.

قَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿ذِي الذِّكْرِ﴾ كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿لَقَدْ أَنزلْنَا إِلَيْكُمْ كِتَابًا فِيهِ ذِكْرُكُمْ﴾ ] الْأَنْبِيَاءِ: ١٠ [أَيْ: تَذْكِيرُكُمْ. وَكَذَا قَالَ قَتَادَةُ وَاخْتَارَهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَسَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ وَإِسْمَاعِيلُ بْنُ أَبِي خَالِدٍ، وَابْنُ عُيَيْنَةَ وَأَبُو حُصَيْنٍ وَأَبُو صَالِحٍ وَالسُّدِّيُّ ﴿ذِي الذِّكْرِ﴾ ذِي الشَّرَفِ أَيْ: ذِي الشَّأْنِ وَالْمَكَانَةِ.

وَلَا مُنَافَاةَ بَيْنَ الْقَوْلَيْنِ، فَإِنَّهُ كِتَابٌ شَرِيفٌ مُشْتَمِلٌ عَلَى التَّذْكِيرِ وَالْإِعْذَارِ وَالْإِنْذَارِ.

وَاخْتَلَفُوا فِي جَوَابِ هَذَا الْقَسْمِ فَقَالَ بَعْضُهُمْ: هُوَ قَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِنْ كُلٌّ إِلا كَذَّبَ الرُّسُلَ فَحَقَّ عِقَابِ﴾ ] ص: ١٤ [. وَقِيلَ قَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِنَّ ذَلِكَ لَحَقٌّ تَخَاصُمُ أَهْلِ النَّارِ﴾ ] ص: ٦٤ [حَكَاهُمَا ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ وَهَذَا الثَّانِي فِيهِ بُعْدٌ كَبِيرٌ، وَضَعَّفَهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: جَوَابُهُ: ﴿بَلِ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا فِي عِزَّةٍ وَشِقَاقٍ﴾ وَاخْتَارَهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ.

وَقِيلَ: جَوَابُهُ مَا تَضَمَّنَهُ سِيَاقُ السُّورَةِ بِكَمَالِهَا، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

ثُمَّ حَكَى ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ عَنْ بَعْضِ أَهْلِ الْعِلْمِ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: جَوَابُهُ "ص" بِمَعْنَى: صِدْقٌ حَقٌّ وَالْقُرْآنِ ذِي الذِّكْرِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿بَلِ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا فِي عِزَّةٍ وَشِقَاقٍ﴾ أَيْ: إِنَّ فِي هَذَا الْقُرْآنِ لَذِكْرًا لِمَنْ يَتَذَكَّرُ، وَعِبْرَةً لِمَنْ يَعْتَبِرُ. وَإِنَّمَا لَمْ يَنْتَفِعْ بِهِ الْكَافِرُونَ لِأَنَّهُمْ ﴿فِي عِزَّةٍ﴾ أَيِ: اسْتِكْبَارٍ عَنْهُ وَحَمِيَّةٍ ﴿وَشِقَاقٍ﴾ أَيْ: مُخَالَفَةٍ لَهُ وَمُعَانَدَةٍ وَمُفَارَقَةٍ.

ثُمَّ خَوَّفَهُمْ مَا أَهْلَكَ بِهِ الْأُمَمَ الْمُكَذِّبَةَ قَبْلَهُمْ بِسَبَبِ مُخَالَفَتِهِمْ لِلرُّسُلِ وَتَكْذِيبِهِمُ الكتب المنزلة من السَّمَاءِ فَقَالَ: ﴿كَمْ أَهْلَكْنَا مِنْ قَبْلِهِمْ مِنْ قَرْنٍ﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ أُمَّةٍ مُكَذِّبَةٍ، ﴿فَنَادَوْا﴾ أَيْ: حِينَ جَاءَهُمُ الْعَذَابُ اسْتَغَاثُوا وَجَأَرُوا إِلَى اللَّهِ. وَلَيْسَ ذَلِكَ بِمُجْدٍ عَنْهُمْ شَيْئًا. كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَلَمَّا أَحَسُّوا بَأْسَنَا إِذَا هُمْ مِنْهَا يَرْكُضُونَ﴾ ] الْأَنْبِيَاءِ: ١٢ [أَيْ: يَهْرَبُونَ، ﴿لَا تَرْكُضُوا وَارْجِعُوا إِلَى مَا أُتْرِفْتُمْ فِيهِ وَمَسَاكِنِكُمْ لَعَلَّكُمْ تُسْأَلُونَ﴾ ] الْأَنْبِيَاءِ: ١٣ [

قَالَ أَبُو دَاوُدَ الطَّيَالِسِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا شُعْبَةُ عَنِ أَبِي إِسْحَاقَ عَنِ التَّمِيمِيِّ قَالَ: سَأَلْتُ ابْنَ عَبَّاسٍ عَنْ قَوْلِ اللَّهِ: ﴿فَنَادَوْا وَلاتَ حِينَ مَنَاصٍ﴾ قَالَ: لَيْسَ بِحِينِ نِدَاءٍ، وَلَا نَزْوٍ وَلَا فِرَارٍ 

وَقَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: لَيْسَ بِحِينِ مِغَاثٍ.

وَقَالَ شَبِيبُ بْنُ بِشْرٍ عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: نَادَوُا النِّدَاءَ حِينَ لَا يَنْفَعُهُمْ وَأَنْشَدَ:

تَذَكَّر لَيْلَى لاتَ حِينَ تذَكّر .

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ كَعْبٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿فَنَادَوْا وَلاتَ حِينَ مَنَاصٍ﴾ يَقُولُ: نَادَوْا بِالتَّوْحِيدِ حِينَ تَوَلَّتِ الدُّنْيَا عَنْهُمْ، وَاسْتَنَاصُوا لِلتَّوْبَةِ حِينَ تَوَلَّتِ الدُّنْيَا عَنْهُمْ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: لَمَّا رَأَوُا الْعَذَابَ أَرَادُوا التَّوْبَةَ فِي غَيْرِ حِينِ النِّدَاءِ.

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: ﴿فَنَادَوْا وَلاتَ حِينَ مَنَاصٍ﴾ لَيْسَ بِحِينِ فِرَارٍ وَلَا إِجَابَةٍ.

وَقَدْ رُوِيَ نَحْوُ هَذَا عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ، وَسَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ وَأَبِي مَالِكٍ وَالضَّحَّاكِ وَزَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ وَالْحَسَنِ وَقَتَادَةَ.

وَعَنْ مَالِكٍ، عَنْ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ: ﴿وَلاتَ حِينَ مَنَاصٍ﴾ وَلَا نِدَاءَ فِي غَيْرِ حِينِ النِّدَاءِ.

وَهَذِهِ الْكَلِمَةُ وَهِيَ "لَاتَ" هِيَ "لَا" الَّتِي لِلنَّفْيِ، زِيدَتْ مَعَهَا "التَّاءُ" كَمَا تُزَادُ فِي "ثُمَّ" فَيَقُولُونَ: "ثُمَّتْ"، وَ "رُبَّ" فَيَقُولُونَ: "رُبَّتْ". وَهِيَ مَفْصُولَةٌ وَالْوَقْفُ عَلَيْهَا. وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ حَكَى عَنِ الْمُصْحَفِ الْإِمَامِ فِيمَا ذَكَرَهُ [ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ] أَنَّهَا مُتَّصِلَةٌ بِحِينَ: "وَلَا تَحِينَ مَنَاصٍ". وَالْمَشْهُورُ الْأَوَّلُ. ثُمَّ قَرَأَ الْجُمْهُورُ بِنَصْبِ "حِينَ" تَقْدِيرُهُ: وَلَيْسَ الْحِينُ حِينَ مَنَاصٍ. وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ جَوَّزَ النَّصْبَ بِهَا، وَأَنْشَدَ:

تَذَكَّر حُب لَيْلَى لاتَ حِينَا ... وأَضْحَى الشَّيْبُ قَدْ قَطَع القَرينا 

وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ جَوَّزَ الْجَرَّ بِهَا، وَأَنْشَدَ:

طَلَبُوا صُلْحَنَا ولاتَ أوانٍ ... فأجَبْنَا أن ليس حينُ بقاءِ وَأَنْشَدَ بَعْضُهُمْ أَيْضًا:

ولاتَ سَاعةَ مَنْدَم

بِخَفْضِ السَّاعَةِ، وَأَهْلُ اللُّغَةِ يَقُولُونَ: النَّوْصُ: التَّأَخُّرُ، وَالْبَوْصُ: التَّقَدُّمُ. وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلاتَ حِينَ مَنَاصٍ﴾ أَيْ: لَيْسَ الْحِينُ حِينَ فِرَارٍ وَلَا ذَهَابٍ.

---

## 38:4-11 — verses 4-11 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Exalted says, informing about the polytheists in their astonishment at the sending of a human being as messenger, as He, the Exalted, said: {Was it a wonder to the people that We revealed to a man among them, saying, "Warn mankind and give good tidings to those who believe that they will have a footing of honesty with their Lord"? The disbelievers said, "Indeed, this is an evident magician."} And He says here: {And they wonder that there has come to them a warner from among themselves}, that is, a human being like them, {and the disbelievers say, "This is a magician, a liar. Has he made the gods [into] one God?"} That is, does he claim that the object of worship is one, that there is no god but Him? The polytheists, may Allah disfigure them, denied this and marveled at abandoning association of partners with Allah, for they had received the worship of idols from their forefathers and their hearts had been steeped in it. So when the Messenger ﷺ called them to strip that out of their hearts and to single Allah out with oneness, they found that enormous and were astonished, and they said: {"Has he made the gods [into] one God? Indeed, this is a curious thing." And the eminent among them went forth}, that is, their chiefs, leaders, heads, and elders, saying: {"Walk on"}, that is, continue in your religion, {"and be patient over your gods,"} and do not respond to what Muhammad calls you to, namely monotheism.

Concerning His saying: {Indeed, this is a thing intended}, Ibn Jarir said: this thing that Muhammad ﷺ calls us to, namely monotheism, is a thing by which he intends honor and superiority over you, and that he should have followers among you, and we will not respond to him in it.

Mention of the reason for the revelation of these verses:

Al-Suddi said: a group of Quraysh gathered, among them Abu Jahl ibn Hisham, al-'As ibn Wa'il, al-Aswad ibn al-Muttalib, and al-Aswad ibn 'Abd Yaghuth, together with a company of the elders of Quraysh. Some of them said to others: let us go to Abu Talib and speak to him about him (Muhammad), so that he may be fair to us regarding him: let him restrain him from reviling our gods, and we will leave him and his god whom he worships, for we fear this old man may die and then something would come from us against him, and the Arabs would taunt us over it, saying: "They left him alone until he died, and then they attacked him." So they sent a man of theirs called al-Muttalib, who sought permission for them to see Abu Talib, saying: these are the elders of your people and their nobles, seeking permission to see you. He said: let them in. When they entered upon him, they said: O Abu Talib, you are our elder and our chief, so be fair to us regarding your nephew: order him to stop reviling our gods, and we will leave him and his god. He said: so Abu Talib sent for him. When the Messenger of Allah ﷺ entered upon him, he said: O son of my brother, these are the elders of your people and their nobles, and they have asked you to stop reviling their gods, so that they will leave you and your god. He said: "O uncle, shall I not call them to something better for them?" He said: and what do you call them to? He said: "I call them to speak a word by which the Arabs will submit to them and through which they will rule over the non-Arabs." Abu Jahl said, from among the group: what is it, by your father? We will give it and ten times its like. He said: say, "There is no god but Allah." So he recoiled and said: ask us something other than this. He said: "Even if you brought me the sun so that you placed it in my hand, I would not ask you for anything other than it." So they rose from him in anger, saying: by Allah, we will surely revile you and your god who commanded you with this. {And the eminent among them went forth, [saying], "Walk on and be patient over your gods. Indeed, this is a thing intended."}

Narrated by Ibn Abi Hatim and Ibn Jarir, with the addition: when they left, the Messenger of Allah ﷺ called his uncle to say "There is no god but Allah," but he refused and said: rather, I am upon the religion of the forefathers. And then was revealed: {Indeed, you cannot guide whom you love} [al-Qasas: 56].

Abu Ja'far ibn Jarir said: [chain] Abu Kurayb and Ibn Waki' said, Abu Usama narrated to us, al-A'mash narrated to us, 'Abbad narrated to us, from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, from Ibn 'Abbas, who said: when Abu Talib fell ill, a group of Quraysh entered upon him, among them Abu Jahl. They said: your nephew reviles our gods, and does such and such, and says such and such, so send for him and forbid him. So he sent for him, and the Prophet ﷺ came and entered the house, and between them and Abu Talib was the space of one man's sitting place. Abu Jahl feared that if he sat next to Abu Talib, it would make him (Abu Talib) more tender toward him (the Prophet), so he jumped up and sat in that place, and the Messenger of Allah ﷺ found no place near his uncle, so he sat by the door. Abu Talib said to him: O son of my brother, what is the matter with your people, that they complain of you, claiming that you revile their gods and say such and such? He said: and they spoke much against him, and the Messenger of Allah ﷺ spoke and said: "O uncle, I want from them a single word by which the Arabs will submit to them and through which the non-Arabs will pay them tribute." They were alarmed at his word and his saying, and they said: a single word! Yes, by your father, and ten [more]! They said: what is it? Abu Talib said: and what word is it, O son of my brother? He said: "There is no god but Allah." So they rose in alarm, shaking out their garments, saying: {"Has he made the gods [into] one God? Indeed, this is a curious thing."} He said: and from this point up to His saying {until they taste My punishment} was revealed. This is the wording of Abu Kurayb.

Thus it was narrated by Imam Ahmad and al-Nasa'i from the hadith of Muhammad ibn 'Abdullah ibn Numayr, both of them from Abu Usama, from al-A'mash, from 'Abbad, unattributed further, with similar wording. It was also narrated by al-Tirmidhi, al-Nasa'i, Ibn Abi Hatim, and Ibn Jarir, all of them in their tafsirs, from the hadith of Sufyan al-Thawri, from al-A'mash, from Yahya ibn 'Umara al-Kufi, from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, from Ibn 'Abbas, mentioning something similar. Al-Tirmidhi said: hasan (sound, though of lesser grade).

Concerning their saying: {We have not heard of this in the latest religion}, that is, we have not heard of this that Muhammad calls us to, namely monotheism, in the latest religion.

Mujahid, Qatada, and Ibn Zayd said: they mean the religion of Quraysh.

Others said: they mean Christianity. This was said by Muhammad ibn Ka'b and al-Suddi.

Al-'Awfi reported from Ibn 'Abbas: {We have not heard of this in the latest religion} means Christianity. They said: if this Qur'an were true, the Christians would have informed us of it.

{This is nothing but a fabrication}: Mujahid and Qatada said it means a lie, and Ibn 'Abbas said it means baseless conjecture.

Concerning their saying: {Has the message been sent down to him out of [all of] us?}, meaning that they consider it far-fetched that he should be singled out, from among all of them, for the revelation of the Qur'an, just as they said in another verse: {Why was this Qur'an not sent down upon a great man from [one of] the two cities?} [al-Zukhruf: 31]. Allah, the Exalted, said: {Do they distribute the mercy of your Lord? It is We who have apportioned among them their livelihood in the life of this world and have raised some of them above others in degrees} [al-Zukhruf: 32]. Therefore, when they said this thing which showed their ignorance and lack of understanding in considering it far-fetched that the Qur'an should be sent down upon the Messenger from among them, Allah, the Exalted, said: {But they have not yet tasted My punishment}, that is, they only say this because, up until the time of their saying it, they had not tasted the punishment of Allah and His vengeance. They will come to know the outcome of what they said and what they denied, on the day they are dragged into the fire of Hell forcibly.

Then He says, clarifying that He is the One who disposes freely in His dominion, doing what He wills, giving whom He wills what He wills, honoring whom He wills, abasing whom He wills, guiding whom He wills, misguiding whom He wills, sending down the spirit of His command upon whom He wills among His servants, and sealing the heart of whom He wills, so that none can guide him after Allah. And indeed the servants possess nothing of the matter, nor is disposal in the dominion theirs, not even the weight of a speck of dust, and they possess not even the skin of a date stone. Therefore Allah, the Exalted, said, denouncing them: {Or do they have the treasuries of the mercy of your Lord, the Exalted in Might, the Bestower?}, that is, the Exalted in Might, whose court cannot be approached, the Bestower, who gives what He wills to whom He wills.

This verse is similar to His saying: {Or have they a share of dominion? Then in that case they would not give the people [even] the speck on a date seed. Or do they envy people for what Allah has given them of His bounty? But We had already given the family of Abraham the Scripture and wisdom and conferred upon them a great kingdom. And some of them believed in it, while others of them turned away from it, and sufficient is Hell as a blazing fire} [al-Nisa: 53-55], and His saying: {Say, "If you possessed the treasuries of the mercy of my Lord, then you would withhold out of fear of spending." And ever has man been stingy} [al-Isra: 100]. That was after the account of the disbelievers denying the sending of a human messenger, just as Allah, the Exalted, informed about the people of Salih (peace be upon him) when they said: {Has the message been sent down upon him out of [all of] us? Rather, he is an insolent liar. They will know tomorrow who is the insolent liar} [al-Qamar: 25-26]. And His saying: {Or is theirs the dominion of the heavens and the earth and whatever is between them? Then let them ascend through the ways}, that is, if they have that, let them ascend through the ways.

Ibn 'Abbas, Mujahid, Sa'id ibn Jubayr, Qatada, and others said: it means the paths of heaven.

Al-Dahhak said: let them ascend to the seventh heaven.

Then He says: {[They are but] soldiers, there, defeated among the [opposing] factions}, that is, these deniers, who are in a state of pride and opposition, will be defeated, overcome, and humbled, just as those who came before them among the denying factions were humbled. This is like His saying: {Or do they say, "We are an assembled band, victorious"? [Their] assembled band will be defeated, and they will turn their backs [in retreat]}, and that occurred on the day of Badr. {But the Hour is their appointment, and the Hour is more disastrous and more bitter} [al-Qamar: 44-46].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنِ الْمُشْرِكِينَ فِي تَعَجُّبِهِمْ مِنْ بِعْثَةِ الرَّسُولِ بَشَرًا، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَكَانَ لِلنَّاسِ عَجَبًا أَنْ أَوْحَيْنَا إِلَى رَجُلٍ مِنْهُمْ أَنْ أَنْذِرِ النَّاسَ وَبَشِّرِ الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا أَنَّ لَهُمْ قَدَمَ صِدْقٍ عِنْدَ رَبِّهِمْ قَالَ الْكَافِرُونَ إِنَّ هَذَا لَسَاحِرٌ مُبِينٌ﴾ وَقَالَ هَاهُنَا: ﴿وَعَجِبُوا أَنْ جَاءَهُمْ مُنْذِرٌ مِنْهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: بَشَرٌ مِثْلُهُمْ، ﴿وَقَالَ الْكَافِرُونَ هَذَا سَاحِرٌ كَذَّابٌ أَجَعَلَ الآلِهَةَ إِلَهًا وَاحِدًا﴾ أَيْ: أَزَعَمَ أَنَّ الْمَعْبُودَ وَاحِدٌ لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا هُوَ؟! أَنْكَرَ الْمُشْرِكُونَ ذَلِكَ -قَبَّحَهُمُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى-وَتَعَجَّبُوا مِنْ تَرْكِ الشِّرْكِ بِاللَّهِ، فَإِنَّهُمْ كَانُوا قَدْ تَلَقَّوْا عَنْ آبَائِهِمْ عِبَادَةَ الْأَوْثَانِ وَأُشْرِبَتْهُ قُلُوبُهُمْ فَلَمَّا دَعَاهُمُ الرَّسُولُ ﷺ إِلَى خَلْعِ ذَلِكَ مِنْ قُلُوبِهِمْ وَإِفْرَادِ اللَّهِ بِالْوَحْدَانِيَّةِ أَعَظَمُوا ذَلِكَ وَتَعَجَّبُوا وَقَالُوا: ﴿أَجَعَلَ الآلِهَةَ إِلَهًا وَاحِدًا إِنَّ هَذَا لَشَيْءٌ عُجَابٌ وَانْطَلَقَ الْمَلأ مِنْهُمْ﴾ وَهُمْ سَادَتُهُمْ وَقَادَتُهُمْ وَرُؤَسَاؤُهُمْ وَكُبَرَاؤُهُمْ قَائِلِينَ: ﴿ [أَنِ] امْشُوا﴾ أَيِ: اسْتَمِرُّوا عَلَى دِينِكُمْ ﴿وَاصْبِرُوا عَلَى آلِهَتِكُمْ﴾ وَلَا تَسْتَجِيبُوا لِمَا يَدْعُوكُمْ إِلَيْهِ مُحَمَّدٌ مِنَ التَّوْحِيدِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِنَّ هَذَا لَشَيْءٌ يُرَادُ﴾ قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: إِنَّ هَذَا الَّذِي يَدْعُونَا إِلَيْهِ مُحَمَّدٌ ﷺ مِنَ التَّوْحِيدِ لَشَيْءٌ يُرِيدُ بِهِ الشَّرَفَ عَلَيْكُمْ وَالِاسْتِعْلَاءَ، وَأَنْ يَكُونَ لَهُ مِنْكُمْ أَتْبَاعٌ وَلَسْنَا مُجِيبِيهِ إِلَيْهِ.

ذِكْرُ سَبَبِ نُزُولِ هَذِهِ الْآيَاتِ:

قَالَ السُّدِّيُّ: إِنَّ أُنَاسًا مِنْ قُرَيْشٍ اجْتَمَعُوا فِيهِمْ: أَبُو جَهْلِ بْنُ هِشَامٍ وَالْعَاصُ بْنُ وَائِلٍ، وَالْأَسْوَدُ بْنُ الْمُطَّلِبِ وَالْأَسْوَدُ بْنُ عَبْدِ يَغُوثَ فِي نَفَرٍ مِنْ مَشْيَخَةِ قُرَيْشٍ، فَقَالَ بَعْضُهُمْ لِبَعْضٍ: انْطَلِقُوا بِنَا إِلَى أَبِي طَالِبٍ فَلْنُكَلِّمْهُ فِيهِ، فَلْيُنْصِفْنَا مِنْهُ فَلْيَكُفَّ عَنْ شَتْمِ آلِهَتِنَا وَنَدَعْهُ وَإِلَهَهُ الَّذِي يَعْبُدُهُ؛ فَإِنَّا نَخَافُ أَنْ يَمُوتَ هَذَا الشَّيْخُ فَيَكُونَ مِنَّا إِلَيْهِ شَيْءٌ. فَتُعَيِّرُنَا [بِهِ] العرب يقولون: تَرَكُوهُ حَتَّى إِذَا مَاتَ عَنْهُ تَنَاوَلُوهُ". فَبَعَثُوا رَجُلًا مِنْهُمْ يُقَالُ لَهُ الْمُطَّلِبُ" فَاسْتَأْذَنَ لَهُمْ عَلَى أَبِي طَالِبٍ فَقَالَ: هَؤُلَاءِ مَشْيَخَةُ قَوْمِكَ وَسَرَاتُهُمْ يَسْتَأْذِنُونَ عَلَيْكَ. قَالَ: أَدْخِلْهُمْ. فَلَمَّا دَخَلُوا عَلَيْهِ قَالُوا: يَا أَبَا طَالِبٍ أَنْتَ كَبِيرُنَا وَسَيِّدُنَا فَأَنْصِفْنَا مِنِ ابْنِ أَخِيكَ فَمُرْهُ فَلْيَكُفَّ عَنْ شَتْمِ آلِهَتِنَا وَنَدَعْهُ وَإِلَهَهُ. قَالَ: فَبَعَثَ إِلَيْهِ أَبُو طَالِبٍ فَلَمَّا دَخَلَ عَلَيْهِ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: يَا ابْنَ أَخِي هَؤُلَاءِ مَشْيَخَةُ قَوْمِكَ وَسَرَاتُهُمْ وَقَدْ سَأَلُوكَ أَنْ تَكُفَّ عَنْ شَتْمِ آلِهَتِهِمْ وَيَدَعُوكَ وَإِلَهَكَ. قَالَ: "يَا عَمِّ أَفَلَا أَدْعُوهُمْ إِلَى مَا هُوَ خَيْرٌ لَهُمْ؟ " قَالَ: وَإِلَامَ تَدْعُوهُمْ؟ قَالَ: "أَدْعُوهُمْ [إِلَى] أَنْ يَتَكَلَّمُوا بِكَلِمَةٍ تَدِينُ لَهُمْ بِهَا الْعَرَبُ وَيَمْلِكُونَ بِهَا الْعَجَمَ". فَقَالَ أَبُو جَهْلٍ مِنْ بَيْنِ الْقَوْمِ: مَا هِيَ وَأَبِيكَ؟ لَنُعْطِيَنَّهَا وَعَشَرَةَ أَمْثَالِهَا. قَالَ: تَقُولُونَ: "لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ". فَنَفَرَ وَقَالَ: سَلْنَا غَيْرَ هَذَا قَالَ: "لَوْ جِئْتُمُونِي بِالشَّمْسِ حَتَّى تَضَعُوهَا فِي يَدِي مَا سَأَلْتُكُمْ غَيْرَهَا" فَقَامُوا مِنْ عِنْدِهِ غِضَابًا، وَقَالُوا: وَاللَّهِ لَنَشْتُمَنَّكَ وَإِلَهَكَ الَّذِي أَمَرَكَ بِهَذَا. ﴿وَانْطَلَقَ الْمَلأ مِنْهُمْ أَنِ امْشُوا وَاصْبِرُوا عَلَى آلِهَتِكُمْ إِنَّ هَذَا لَشَيْءٌ يُرَادُ﴾

رَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ وَابْنُ جَرِيرٍ وَزَادَ: فَلَمَّا خَرَجُوا دَعَا رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ عَمَّهُ إِلَى قَوْلِ: "لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ" فَأَبَى وَقَالَ: بَلْ عَلَى دِينِ الْأَشْيَاخِ. وَنَزَلَتْ: ﴿إِنَّكَ لَا تَهْدِي مَنْ أَحْبَبْتَ﴾ [الْقَصَصِ:٥٦] 

وَقَالَ أَبُو جَعْفَرِ بْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو كُرَيْبٍ وَابْنُ وَكِيعٍ قَالَا حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو أُسَامَةَ حَدَّثَنَا الْأَعْمَشُ حَدَّثَنَا عَبَّادٌ عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قال: لما مَرِضَ أَبُو طَالِبٍ دَخَلَ عَلَيْهِ رَهْطٌ مِنْ قُرَيْشٍ فِيهِمْ أَبُو جَهْلٍ فَقَالُوا: إِنَّ ابْنَ أَخِيكَ يَشْتُمُ آلِهَتَنَا وَيَفْعَلُ وَيَفْعَلُ وَيَقُولُ وَيَقُولُ فَلَوْ بَعَثْتَ إِلَيْهِ فَنَهَيْتَهُ؟ فَبَعَثَ إِلَيْهِ فَجَاءَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ فَدَخَلَ الْبَيْتَ وَبَيْنَهُمْ وَبَيْنَ أَبِي طَالِبٍ قَدْرُ مَجْلِسِ رَجُلٍ قَالَ: فَخَشِيَ أَبُو جَهْلٍ إِنْ جَلَسَ إِلَى جَنْبِ أَبِي طَالِبٍ أَنْ يَكُونَ أَرَقَّ لَهُ عَلَيْهِ. فَوَثَبَ فَجَلَسَ فِي ذَلِكَ الْمَجْلِسِ وَلَمْ يَجِدْ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ مَجْلِسًا قُرْبَ عَمِّهِ فَجَلَسَ عِنْدَ الْبَابِ. فَقَالَ لَهُ أَبُو طَالِبٍ: أَيِ ابْنَ أَخِي مَا بَالُ قَوْمِكَ يَشُكُونَكَ، يَزْعُمُونَ أَنَّكَ تَشْتُمُ آلِهَتَهُمْ وَتَقُولُ وَتَقُولُ؟ قَالَ: وَأَكْثَرُوا عَلَيْهِ مِنَ الْقَوْلِ وَتَكَلَّمَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ فَقَالَ: " يَا عَمِّ إِنِّي أُرِيدُهُمْ عَلَى كَلِمَةٍ وَاحِدَةٍ! يَقُولُونَهَا تَدِينُ لَهُمْ بِهَا الْعَرَبُ وَتُؤَدِّي إِلَيْهِمْ بِهَا الْعَجَمُ الْجِزْيَةَ" فَفَزِعُوا لِكَلِمَتِهِ وَلِقَوْلِهِ وَقَالُوا كَلِمَةً وَاحِدَةً! نَعَمْ وَأَبِيكَ عَشْرًا فَقَالُوا: وَمَا هِيَ؟ وَقَالَ أَبُو طَالِبٍ وَأَيُّ كَلِمَةٍ هِيَ يَا ابْنَ أَخِي؟ فَقَالَ: "لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ" فَقَامُوا فَزِعِينَ يَنْفُضُونَ ثِيَابَهُمْ وَهُمْ يَقُولُونَ: ﴿أَجَعَلَ الآلِهَةَ إِلَهًا وَاحِدًا إِنَّ هَذَا لَشَيْءٌ عُجَابٌ﴾ قَالَ: وَنَزَلَتْ مِنْ هَذَا الْمَوْضِعِ إِلَى قَوْلِهِ: ﴿لَمَّا يَذُوقُوا عَذَابِ﴾ لَفْظُ أَبِي كُرَيْبٍ 

وَهَكَذَا رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ وَالنَّسَائِيُّ مِنْ حَدِيثِ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ نُمَيْرٍ، كِلَاهُمَا عَنْ أَبِي أُسَامَةَ عَنِ الْأَعْمَشِ عَنْ عَبَّادٍ غَيْرِ مَنْسُوبٍ بِهِ نَحْوَهُ وَرَوَاهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ، وَالنَّسَائِيُّ وَابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ وَابْنُ جَرِيرٍ أَيْضًا كُلُّهُمْ فِي تَفَاسِيرِهِمْ مِنْ حَدِيثِ سُفْيَانَ الثَّوْرِيِّ عن الأعمش عن يحيى بن عمارة الْكُوفِيِّ عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فَذَكَرَ نَحْوَهُ. وَقَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ حَسَنٌ 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُمْ: ﴿مَا سَمِعْنَا بِهَذَا فِي الْمِلَّةِ الآخِرَةِ﴾ أَيْ: مَا سَمِعْنَا بِهَذَا الَّذِي يَدْعُونَا إِلَيْهِ مُحَمَّدٌ مِنَ التَّوْحِيدِ فِي الْمِلَّةِ الْآخِرَةِ.

قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ وَقَتَادَةُ وَابْنُ زَيْدٍ: يَعْنُونَ دِينَ قُرَيْشٍ.

وَقَالَ غَيْرُهُمْ: يَعْنُونَ النَّصْرَانِيَّةَ، قَالَهُ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ كَعْبٍ وَالسُّدِّيُّ.

وَقَالَ الْعَوْفِيُّ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿مَا سَمِعْنَا بِهَذَا فِي الْمِلَّةِ الآخِرَةِ﴾ يَعْنِي: النَّصْرَانِيَّةَ قَالُوا: لَوْ كَانَ هَذَا الْقُرْآنُ حَقًّا أَخْبَرَتْنَا بِهِ النَّصَارَى.

﴿إِنْ هَذَا إِلا اخْتِلاقٌ﴾ قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَقَتَادَةُ كَذِبٌ وَقَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: تَخَرُّصٌ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُمْ: ﴿أَؤُنزلَ عَلَيْهِ الذِّكْرُ مِنْ بَيْنِنَا﴾ يَعْنِي: أَنَّهُمْ يَسْتَبْعِدُونَ تَخْصِيصَهُ بِإِنْزَالِ الْقُرْآنِ عَلَيْهِ مِنْ بَيْنِهِمْ كُلِّهِمْ كَمَا قَالُوا فِي الْآيَةِ الْأُخْرَى: ﴿لَوْلا نزلَ هَذَا الْقُرْآنُ عَلَى رَجُلٍ مِنَ الْقَرْيَتَيْنِ عَظِيمٍ﴾ [الزُّخْرُفِ: ٣١] قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَهُمْ يَقْسِمُونَ رَحْمَةَ رَبِّكَ نَحْنُ قَسَمْنَا بَيْنَهُمْ مَعِيشَتَهُمْ فِي الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا وَرَفَعْنَا بَعْضَهُمْ فَوْقَ بَعْضٍ دَرَجَاتٍ﴾ [الزُّخْرُفِ: ٣٢] وَلِهَذَا لَمَّا قَالُوا هَذَا الَّذِي دَلَّ عَلَى جَهْلِهِمْ وَقِلَّةِ عَقْلِهِمْ فِي اسْتِبْعَادِهِمْ إِنْزَالَ الْقُرْآنِ عَلَى الرَّسُولِ مِنْ بَيْنِهِمْ، قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿بَلْ لَمَّا يَذُوقُوا عَذَابِ﴾ أَيْ: إِنَّمَا يَقُولُونَ هَذَا لِأَنَّهُمْ مَا ذَاقُوا إِلَى حِينِ قَوْلِهِمْ ذَلِكَ عَذَابَ اللَّهِ وَنِقْمَتَهُ سَيَعْلَمُونَ غِبَّ مَا قَالُوا، وَمَا كَذَّبُوا بِهِ يَوْمَ يُدَعّون إِلَى نَارِ جَهَنَّمَ دَعّا.

ثُمَّ قَالَ مُبَيِّنًا أَنَّهُ الْمُتَصَرِّفُ فِي مُلْكِهِ الْفَعَّالُ لِمَا يَشَاءُ الَّذِي يُعْطِي مَنْ يَشَاءُ مَا يَشَاءُ وَيُعِزُّ مَنْ يَشَاءُ وَيُذِلُّ مَنْ يَشَاءُ وَيَهْدِي مَنْ يَشَاءُ وَيُضِلُّ مَنْ يَشَاءُ وَيُنَزِّلُ الرُّوحَ مِنْ أَمْرِهِ عَلَى مَنْ يَشَاءُ مِنْ عِبَادِهِ وَيَخْتِمُ عَلَى قَلْبِ مَنْ يَشَاءُ، فَلَا يَهْدِيهِ أَحَدٌ مِنْ بَعْدِ اللَّهِ وَإِنَّ الْعِبَادَ لَا يَمْلِكُونَ شَيْئًا مِنَ الْأَمْرِ وَلَيْسَ إِلَيْهِمْ مِنَ التَّصَرُّفِ فِي الْمُلْكِ وَلَا مِثْقَالَ ذَرَّةٍ وَمَا يَمْلِكُونَ مِنْ قِطْمِيرٍ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى مُنْكِرًا عَلَيْهِمْ: ﴿أَمْ عِنْدَهُمْ خَزَائِنُ رَحْمَةِ رَبِّكَ الْعَزِيزِ الْوَهَّابِ﴾ أَيِ: الْعَزِيزِ الَّذِي لَا يُرَامُ جَنَابُهُ الْوَهَّابِ الَّذِي يُعْطِي مَا يُرِيدُ لِمَنْ يُرِيدُ.

وَهَذِهِ الْآيَةُ شَبِيهَةٌ بِقَوْلِهِ: ﴿أَمْ لَهُمْ نَصِيبٌ مِنَ الْمُلْكِ فَإِذًا لَا يُؤْتُونَ النَّاسَ نَقِيرًا أَمْ يَحْسُدُونَ النَّاسَ عَلَى مَا آتَاهُمُ اللَّهُ مِنْ فَضْلِهِ فَقَدْ آتَيْنَا آلَ إِبْرَاهِيمَ الْكِتَابَ وَالْحِكْمَةَ وَآتَيْنَاهُمْ مُلْكًا عَظِيمًا فَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ آمَنَ بِهِ وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ صَدَّ عَنْهُ وَكَفَى بِجَهَنَّمَ سَعِيرًا﴾ [النِّسَاءِ: ٥٣: ٥٥] وَقَوْلُهُ ﴿قُلْ لَوْ أَنْتُمْ تَمْلِكُونَ خَزَائِنَ رَحْمَةِ رَبِّي إِذًا لأمْسَكْتُمْ خَشْيَةَ الإنْفَاقِ وَكَانَ الإنْسَانُ قَتُورًا﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ: ١٠] وَذَلِكَ بَعْدَ الْحِكَايَةِ عَنِ الْكُفَّارِ أَنَّهُمْ أَنْكَرُوا بِعْثَةَ الرَّسُولِ الْبَشَرِيِّ وَكَمَا أَخْبَرَ تَعَالَى عَنْ قَوْمِ صَالِحٍ [عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ] حِينَ قَالُوا: ﴿أَؤُلْقِيَ الذِّكْرُ عَلَيْهِ مِنْ بَيْنِنَا بَلْ هُوَ كَذَّابٌ أَشِرٌ سَيَعْلَمُونَ غَدًا مَنِ الْكَذَّابُ الأشِرُ﴾ [القمر: ٢٥: ٢٦] وقوله: ﴿أَمْ لَهُمْ مُلْكُ السَّمَوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ وَمَا بَيْنَهُمَا فَلْيَرْتَقُوا فِي الأسْبَابِ﴾ أَيْ: إِنْ كَانَ لَهُمْ ذَلِكَ فَلْيَصْعَدُوا فِي الْأَسْبَابِ.

قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَمُجَاهِدٌ وَسَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ وَقَتَادَةُ وَغَيْرُهُمْ: يَعْنِي طُرُقَ السَّمَاءِ.

وَقَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ: فَلْيَصْعَدُوا إِلَى السَّمَاءِ السَّابِعَةِ.

ثُمَّ قَالَ: ﴿جُنْدٌ مَا هُنَالِكَ مَهْزُومٌ مِنَ الأحْزَابِ﴾ أَيْ: هَؤُلَاءِ الْجُنْدُ الْمُكَذِّبُونَ الَّذِينَ هُمْ فِي عِزَّةٍ وَشِقَاقٍ سَيُهْزَمُونَ وَيُغْلَبُونَ وَيُكْبَتُونَ كَمَا كُبِتَ الَّذِينَ مِنْ قَبْلِهِمْ مِنَ الْأَحْزَابِ الْمُكَذِّبِينَ وَهَذِهِ كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿أَمْ يَقُولُونَ نَحْنُ جَمِيعٌ مُنْتَصِرٌ سَيُهْزَمُ الْجَمْعُ وَيُوَلُّونَ الدُّبُرَ﴾ وَكَانَ ذَلِكَ يَوْمَ بَدْرٍ ﴿بَلِ السَّاعَةُ مَوْعِدُهُمْ وَالسَّاعَةُ أَدْهَى وَأَمَرُّ﴾ [الْقَمَرِ: ٤٤: ٤٦] .

---

## 38:12-16 — verses 12-16 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, informing about these past generations and what befell them of punishment, retribution, and vengeance because of their opposition to the messengers and their denial of the prophets. Their stories have already been presented in detail in numerous places.

His saying, {Those are the parties} means: they were more numerous than you, stronger in power, and greater in wealth and children, yet none of that repelled from them anything of God's punishment when the command of your Lord came. For this reason He said: {Each of them only denied the messengers, so My punishment was justly deserved}. Thus He made their denial of the messengers the cause of their destruction, so let those being addressed beware of this with the utmost caution.

His saying, {And these people await nothing but a single blast, which will have no delay} Malik reported from Zayd ibn Aslam: meaning it has no repetition, that is, they await nothing but the Hour to come upon them suddenly, for its signs have already come, meaning it has drawn near, approached, and become imminent. This blast is the blast of terror which God commands Israfil to prolong, so that no one among the inhabitants of the heavens and the earth remains without being terrified, except whom God, Mighty and Majestic, excepts.

His saying, {And they said: Our Lord, hasten for us our portion before the Day of Reckoning} this is a denunciation from God of the polytheists for invoking upon themselves the hastening of the punishment. Al-qitt (the portion) means the record, and it is also said to mean the share and lot.

Ibn Abbas, Mujahid, al-Dahhak, al-Hasan, and others said: they asked for the punishment to be hastened. Qatadah added: just as they said, {O God, if this is indeed the truth from You, then rain down upon us stones from the sky or bring us a painful punishment} [al-Anfal: 32]. It is also said: they asked for their share of Paradise, if it existed, to be hastened so they could receive it in this world. This statement of theirs was only meant as an expression of denial and disbelief.

Ibn Jarir said: they asked for whatever they deserved of good or evil to be hastened in this world. This is a sound explanation, and the statements of al-Dahhak and Isma'il ibn Abi Khalid revolve around it. God knows best.

Since this statement of theirs was made in mockery and denial, God Almighty said to His Messenger ﷺ, commanding him to be patient with their harm and giving him glad tidings, for his patience, of the good outcome, victory, and triumph.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْ هَؤُلَاءِ الْقُرُونِ الْمَاضِيَةِ، وَمَا حَلَّ بِهِمْ مِنَ الْعَذَابِ وَالنَّكَالِ وَالنَّقَمَاتِ فِي مُخَالَفَةِ الرُّسُلِ وَتَكْذِيبِ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ وَقَدْ تَقَدَّمَتْ قِصَصُهُمْ مَبْسُوطَةً فِي أَمَاكِنَ مُتَعَدِّدَةٍ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿أُولَئِكَ الأحْزَابُ﴾ أَيْ: كَانُوا أَكْثَرَ مِنْكُمْ وَأَشَدَّ قُوَّةً وَأَكْثَرَ أَمْوَالًا وَأَوْلَادًا فَمَا دَافَعَ ذَلِكَ عَنْهُمْ مِنْ عَذَابِ اللَّهِ مِنْ شَيْءٍ لَمَّا جَاءَ أَمْرُ رَبِّكَ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿إِنْ كُلٌّ إِلا كَذَّبَ الرُّسُلَ فَحَقَّ عِقَابِ﴾ فَجَعَلَ عِلَّةَ هَلَاكِهِمْ هُوَ تَكْذِيبُهُمْ بِالرُّسُلِ فَلْيَحْذَرِ الْمُخَاطَبُونَ مِنْ ذَلِكَ أَشَدَّ الْحَذَرِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمَا يَنْظُرُ هَؤُلاءِ إِلا صَيْحَةً وَاحِدَةً مَا لَهَا مِنْ فَوَاقٍ﴾ قَالَ مَالِكٌ عَنْ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ: أَيْ لَيْسَ لَهَا مَثْنَوِيَّةٌ أَيْ: مَا يَنْظُرُونَ إِلَّا السَّاعَةَ أَنْ تَأْتِيَهُمْ بَغْتَةً فَقَدْ جَاءَ أَشْرَاطُهَا أَيْ: فَقَدِ اقْتَرَبَتْ وَدَنَتْ وَأَزِفَتْ وَهَذِهِ الصَّيْحَةُ هِيَ نَفْخَةُ الْفَزَعِ الَّتِي يَأْمُرُ اللَّهُ إِسْرَافِيلَ أَنْ يُطَوِّلَهَا، فَلَا يَبْقَى أَحَدٌ مِنْ أَهْلِ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضِ إِلَّا فَزِعَ إِلَّا مَنِ اسْتَثْنَى اللَّهُ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَقَالُوا رَبَّنَا عَجِّلْ لَنَا قِطَّنَا قَبْلَ يَوْمِ الْحِسَابِ﴾ هَذَا إِنْكَارٌ مِنَ اللَّهِ عَلَى الْمُشْرِكِينَ فِي دُعَائِهِمْ عَلَى أَنْفُسِهِمْ بِتَعْجِيلِ الْعَذَابِ، فَإِنَّ الْقِطَّ هُوَ الْكِتَابُ وَقِيلَ: هُوَ الْحَظُّ وَالنَّصِيبُ.

قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ وَمُجَاهِدٌ وَالضَّحَّاكُ وَالْحَسَنُ وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ: سَأَلُوا تَعْجِيلَ الْعَذَابِ -زَادَ قَتَادَةُ كَمَا قَالُوا: ﴿اللَّهُمَّ إِنْ كَانَ هَذَا هُوَ الْحَقَّ مِنْ عِنْدِكَ فَأَمْطِرْ عَلَيْنَا حِجَارَةً مِنَ السَّمَاءِ أَوِ ائْتِنَا بِعَذَابٍ أَلِيمٍ﴾ [الأنفال: ٣٢] وَقِيلَ: سَأَلُوا تَعْجِيلَ نَصِيبِهِمْ مِنَ الْجَنَّةِ إِنْ كَانَتْ مَوْجُودَةً أَنْ يَلْقَوْا ذَاكَ فِي الدُّنْيَا. وَإِنَّمَا خَرَجَ هَذَا مِنْهُمْ مَخْرَجَ الِاسْتِبْعَادِ وَالتَّكْذِيبِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: سَأَلُوا تَعْجِيلَ مَا يَسْتَحِقُّونَهُ مِنَ الْخَيْرِ أَوِ الشَّرِّ فِي الدُّنْيَا وَهَذَا الَّذِي قَالَهُ جَيِّدٌ، وَعَلَيْهِ يَدُورُ كَلَامُ الضَّحَّاكِ وَإِسْمَاعِيلَ بْنِ أَبِي خَالِدٍ وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَلَمَّا كَانَ هَذَا الْكَلَامُ مِنْهُمْ عَلَى وَجْهِ الِاسْتِهْزَاءِ وَالِاسْتِبْعَادِ قَالَ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى لِرَسُولِهِ ﷺ آمِرًا لَهُ بِالصَّبْرِ عَلَى أَذَاهُمْ وَمُبَشِّرًا لَهُ عَلَى صَبْرِهِ بِالْعَاقِبَةِ وَالنَّصْرِ وَالظَّفَرِ.

---

## 38:17-20 — verses 17-20 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty mentions concerning His servant and messenger David (peace be upon him) that he possessed al-ayd (strength), and al-ayd means strength in knowledge and in action.

[Ibn Abbas], Ibn Zayd, and al-Suddi said: al-ayd means strength. Ibn Zayd recited: {And the heaven We built with ayd (power), and indeed We are the Expanders} [al-Dhariyat: 47].

Mujahid said: al-ayd means strength in obedience.

Qatadah said: David (peace be upon him) was given strength in worship and understanding in Islam. It has been mentioned to us that he (peace be upon him) used to stand in prayer a third of the night and fast half of his lifetime.

This is established in the two Sahihs from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, that he said: "The prayer most beloved to Allah is the prayer of David, and the fasting most beloved to Allah is the fasting of David. He would sleep half the night, stand a third of it, and sleep a sixth of it, and he would fast one day and break his fast the next day, and he would not flee when he met the enemy." And indeed he was awwab, meaning one who constantly turns back to Allah, Mighty and Majestic, in all his affairs and matters.

Concerning His words: {Indeed, We subjected the mountains to glorify with him in the evening and at sunrise}, meaning that the Almighty subjected the mountains so that they would glorify Allah along with him at sunrise and at the end of the day, as the Almighty said: {O mountains, echo his praises, and the birds as well} [Saba: 10]. Likewise the birds used to glorify along with his glorification and echo his refrain: when a bird passed by him while soaring in the air and heard him chanting his recitation of the Psalms, it would be unable to continue flying and would instead stop in the air and glorify along with him, and the towering mountains would answer him, echoing along with him and glorifying in accordance with him.

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] Abu Kurayb told us, Muhammad ibn Bishr told us, from Mis'ar, from Abd al-Karim, from Musa ibn Abi Kathir, from Ibn Abbas, that it reached him that Umm Hani mentioned that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, on the day of the conquest of Makkah, prayed the mid-morning prayer (duha) of eight units (rak'at). Ibn Abbas said: I had thought that this hour had a prayer, for Allah the Almighty says: {They glorify in the evening and at sunrise}.

He then related it through the hadith of Sa'id ibn Abi Arubah, from Abu al-Mutawakkil, from Ayyub ibn Safwan, from his client Abdullah ibn al-Harith ibn Nawfal, that Ibn Abbas used not to pray the duha prayer. He said: So I brought him in to Umm Hani and said: Tell him what you told me. Umm Hani said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ entered upon me in my house on the day of the conquest, then he ordered water to be poured into a basin, then he ordered a cloth to be brought and it was held between me and him, and he washed himself, then he sprinkled a corner of the house and prayed eight units, and that was from the duha prayer: their standing, their bowing, their prostration, and their sitting were all equal, close to one another. Ibn Abbas then went out saying: I have read what is between the two covers [of the Qur'an] and I did not know the duha prayer until now: {They glorify in the evening and at sunrise}. And I used to say: where is the prayer of ishraq (sunrise)? And after that he used to say: it is the prayer of ishraq.

For this reason He said: {And the birds gathered}, meaning held fast in the air, {each one turning back to Him}, meaning obedient, glorifying in accordance with him.

Sa'id ibn Jubayr, Qatadah, and Malik, from Zayd ibn Aslam and Ibn Zayd, said: {each one turning back to Him} means obedient.

Concerning His words: {And We strengthened his kingdom}, meaning We granted him a complete kingdom, comprising everything that kings need.

Ibn Abi Najih said, from Mujahid: he was the most powerful ruler among the people of the world.

Al-Suddi said: four thousand guards would guard him every day.

Some of the early scholars (salaf) said: it has reached me that his guards numbered thirty-three thousand each night, and the rotation would not come back around to the same men until the following year.

Others said: forty thousand, fully armed. Ibn Jarir and Ibn Abi Hatim mentioned, through the report of Ilba ibn Ahmar, from Ikrimah, from Ibn Abbas: that two men among the Children of Israel came before David (peace be upon him), one of them bringing a complaint against the other, claiming that the other had seized his cattle by force. The other denied it, and the claimant had no proof, so David deferred the matter between them. When night came, David (peace be upon him) was commanded in a dream to kill the claimant. When day came, he summoned them both and ordered the claimant to be killed. The man said: O Prophet of Allah, why do you kill me, when this man has seized my cattle by force? David said: Allah, Mighty and Majestic, has commanded me to kill you, so I will kill you without doubt. The man said: By Allah, O Prophet of Allah, Allah has not commanded you to kill me for the sake of this claim I brought against him, and indeed I am truthful in what I claimed, but I had once treacherously killed this man's father, and no one was aware of that. So David (peace be upon him) ordered him to be killed, and he was killed.

Ibn Abbas said: so the awe of him grew intense among the Children of Israel, and this is what Allah, Mighty and Majestic, refers to when He says: {And We strengthened his kingdom}.

Concerning His words: {And We gave him wisdom (al-hikmah)}, Mujahid said: it means understanding, intellect, and perceptiveness. On another occasion he said: wisdom and justice. On another occasion he said: correctness.

Qatadah said: it means the Book of Allah and following what is in it.

Al-Suddi said: {wisdom} means prophethood.

Concerning His words: {And decisive speech (fasl al-khitab)}, Shurayh the judge and al-Sha'bi said: decisive speech means witnesses and oaths.

Qatadah said: two witnesses against the claimant, or the oath of the defendant, this is the decisive speech by which the prophets and messengers, or he said the believers and the righteous, rendered judgment, and it is the ruling method of this nation (ummah) until the Day of Resurrection. Abu Abd al-Rahman al-Sulami said likewise.

Mujahid and al-Suddi said: it means arriving at the correct judgment and understanding it.

Mujahid also said: it means decisiveness in speech and in judgment.

This encompasses all of the above, and that is what is meant, and this is what Ibn Jarir chose.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Umar ibn Shabbah al-Numayri told us, Ibrahim ibn al-Mundhir told us, Abd al-Aziz ibn Abi Thabit told me, from Abd al-Rahman ibn Abi al-Zinad, from his father, from Bilal ibn Abi Burdah, from his father, from Abu Musa, may Allah be pleased with him, who said: the first to say "amma ba'd" (now then) was David (peace be upon him), and that is fasl al-khitab.

Al-Sha'bi said likewise: decisive speech is the phrase "amma ba'd".

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَذْكُرُ تَعَالَى عَنْ عَبْدِهِ وَرَسُولِهِ دَاوُدَ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ: أَنَّهُ كَانَ ذَا أَيْدٍ وَالْأَيْدُ: الْقُوَّةُ فِي الْعِلْمِ وَالْعَمَلِ.

قَالَ [ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ] وَابْنُ زَيْدٍ وَالسُّدِّيُّ: الْأَيْدُ: الْقُوَّةُ وَقَرَأَ ابْنُ زَيْدٍ: ﴿وَالسَّمَاءَ بَنَيْنَاهَا بِأَيْدٍ وَإِنَّا لَمُوسِعُونَ﴾ [الذَّارِيَاتِ: ٤٧]

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: الْأَيْدُ: الْقُوَّةُ فِي الطَّاعَةِ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: أُعْطِيَ دَاوُدُ [عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ] قُوَّةً فِي الْعِبَادَةِ وَفِقْهًا فِي الْإِسْلَامِ، وَقَدْ ذُكِرَ لَنَا أَنَّهُ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ كَانَ يَقُومُ ثُلُثَ اللَّيْلِ وَيَصُومُ نِصْفَ الدَّهْرِ.

وَهَذَا ثَابِتٌ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "أَحَبُّ الصَّلَاةِ إِلَى اللَّهِ صَلَاةُ دَاوُدَ وَأَحَبُّ الصِّيَامِ إِلَى اللَّهِ صِيَامُ دَاوُدَ كَانَ يَنَامُ نِصْفَ اللَّيْلِ وَيَقُومُ ثُلُثَهُ وَيَنَامُ سُدُسَهُ وَكَانَ يَصُومُ يَوْمًا وَيُفْطِرُ يَوْمًا وَلَا يَفِرُّ إِذَا لَاقَى" وَإِنَّهُ كَانَ أَوَّابًا، وَهُوَ الرَّجَّاعُ إِلَى اللَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ فِي جَمِيعِ أُمُورِهِ وَشُئُونِهِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِنَّا سَخَّرْنَا الْجِبَالَ مَعَهُ يُسَبِّحْنَ بِالْعَشِيِّ وَالإشْرَاقِ﴾ أَيْ: إِنَّهُ تَعَالَى سَخَّرَ الْجِبَالَ تُسَبِّحُ مَعَهُ عِنْدَ إِشْرَاقِ الشَّمْسِ وَآخِرِ النَّهَارِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَا جِبَالُ أَوِّبِي مَعَهُ وَالطَّيْرَ﴾ [سَبَأٍ: ١٠] وَكَذَلِكَ كَانَتِ الطَّيْرُ تُسَبِّحُ بِتَسْبِيحِهِ وَتُرَجِّعُ بِتَرْجِيعِهِ إِذَا مَرَّ بِهِ الطَّيْرُ وَهُوَ سَابِحٌ فِي الْهَوَاءِ فَسَمِعَهُ وَهُوَ يَتَرَنَّمُ بِقِرَاءَةِ الزَّبُورِ لَا تَسْتَطِيعُ الذَّهَابَ بَلْ تَقِفُ فِي الْهَوَاءِ وَتُسَبِّحُ مَعَهُ وَتُجِيبُهُ الْجِبَالُ الشَّامِخَاتُ تُرَجِّعُ مَعَهُ وَتُسَبِّحُ تَبَعًا لَهُ.

قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو كُرَيْب حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ بِشْرٍ عَنْ مِسْعَر عَنْ عبد الكريم عن مُوسَى بْنِ أَبِي كَثِيرٍ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ أَنَّهُ بَلَغَهُ: أَنَّ أُمَّ هَانِئٍ ذَكَرَتْ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ وسلم يوم فَتْحِ مَكَّةَ صَلَّى الضُّحَى ثَمَانِ رَكَعَاتٍ، قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: قَدْ ظَنَنْتُ أَنَّ لِهَذِهِ السَّاعَةِ صَلَاةً يَقُولُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿يُسَبِّحْنَ بِالْعَشِيِّ وَالإشْرَاقِ﴾ 

ثُمَّ رَوَاهُ مِنْ حَدِيثِ سَعِيدِ بْنِ أَبِي عَرُوبَةَ، عَنْ أَبِي الْمُتَوَكِّلِ عَنْ أَيُّوبَ بْنِ صَفْوَانَ عَنْ مَوْلَاهُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ الْحَارِثِ بْنِ نَوْفَلٍ أَنَّ ابْنَ عَبَّاسٍ كَانَ لَا يُصَلِّي الضُّحَى قَالَ: فَأَدْخَلْتُهُ عَلَى أُمِّ هَانِئٍ فَقُلْتُ: أَخْبِرِي هَذَا مَا أَخْبَرْتِنِي بِهِ. فَقَالَتْ أُمُّ هَانِئٍ: دَخَلَ عَلَيَّ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَوْمَ الْفَتْحِ فِي بَيْتِي ثُمَّ أَمَرَ بِمَاءٍ صُبَّ فِي قَصْعَةٍ ثُمَّ أَمَرَ بِثَوْبٍ فَأَخَذَ بَيْنِي وَبَيْنَهُ فَاغْتَسَلَ ثُمَّ رَشَّ نَاحِيَةَ الْبَيْتِ فَصَلَّى ثَمَانِ رَكَعَاتٍ، وَذَلِكَ مِنَ الضُّحَى قِيَامُهُنَّ وَرُكُوعُهُنَّ وَسُجُودُهُنَّ وَجُلُوسُهُنَّ سَوَاءٌ قَرِيبٌ بِعَضُهُنَّ مِنْ بَعْضٍ فَخَرَجَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ وَهُوَ يَقُولُ: لَقَدْ قَرَأْتُ مَا بَيْنَ اللَّوْحَيْنِ مَا عَرَفْتُ صَلَاةَ الضُّحَى إِلَّا الْآنَ: ﴿يُسَبِّحْنَ بِالْعَشِيِّ وَالإشْرَاقِ﴾ وَكُنْتُ أَقُولُ: أَيْنَ صَلَاةُ الْإِشْرَاقِ وَكَانَ بَعْدُ يَقُولُ: صَلَاةُ الْإِشْرَاقِ. 

وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَالطَّيْرَ مَحْشُورَةً﴾ أَيْ: مَحْبُوسَةً فِي الْهَوَاءِ، ﴿كُلٌّ لَهُ أَوَّابٌ﴾ أَيْ: مُطِيعٌ يُسَبِّحُ تَبَعًا لَهُ.

قَالَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ وَقَتَادَةُ وَمَالِكٌ عَنْ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ وَابْنِ زَيْدٍ: ﴿كُلٌّ لَهُ أَوَّابٌ﴾ أَيْ: مُطِيعٌ.

[وَقَوْلُهُ] ﴿وَشَدَدْنَا مُلْكَهُ﴾ أَيْ: جَعَلْنَا لَهُ مُلْكًا كَامِلًا مِنْ جَمِيعِ مَا يَحْتَاجُ إِلَيْهِ الْمُلُوكُ.

قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي نَجِيحٍ عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ: كَانَ أَشَدَّ أَهْلِ الدُّنْيَا سُلْطَانًا.

وَقَالَ السُّدِّيُّ: كَانَ يَحْرُسُهُ فِي كُلِّ يَوْمٍ أَرْبَعَةُ آلَافٍ.

وَقَالَ بَعْضُ السَّلَفِ: بَلَغَنِي أَنَّهُ كَانَ حَرَسُه فِي كُلِّ لَيْلَةٍ ثَلَاثَةً وَثَلَاثِينَ أَلْفًا لَا تَدُورُ عَلَيْهِمُ النَّوْبَةُ إِلَى مِثْلِهَا مِنَ الْعَامِ الْقَابِلِ.

وَقَالَ غَيْرُهُ: أَرْبَعُونَ أَلْفًا مُشْتَمِلُونَ بِالسِّلَاحِ. وَقَدْ ذَكَرَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ وَابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ مِنْ رِوَايَةِ عِلْباء بْنُ أَحْمَرَ عَنْ عِكْرِمة عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: أَنَّ نَفَرَيْنِ مِنْ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ اسْتَعْدَى أَحَدُهُمَا عَلَى الْآخَرِ إِلَى دَاوُدَ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ أَنَّهُ اغْتَصَبَهُ بَقَرًا فَأَنْكَرَ الْآخَرُ، وَلَمْ يَكُنْ لِلْمُدَّعِي بَيِّنَةٌ فَأَرْجَأَ أَمْرَهُمَا فَلَمَّا كَانَ اللَّيْلُ أُمِرَ دَاوُدُ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، فِي الْمَنَامِ بِقَتْلِ الْمُدَّعِي فَلَمَّا كَانَ النَّهَارُ طَلَبَهُمَا وَأَمَرَ بِقَتْلِ الْمُدَّعِي فَقَالَ: يَا نَبِيَّ اللَّهِ عَلَامَ تَقْتُلُنِي وَقَدِ اغْتَصَبَنِي هَذَا بَقَرِي؟ فَقَالَ: إِنِ اللَّهَ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ أَمَرَنِي بِقَتْلِكَ فَأَنَا قَاتِلُكَ لَا مَحَالَةَ. فَقَالَ: وَاللَّهِ يا نبي اللَّهِ إِنَّ اللَّهَ لَمْ يَأْمُرْكَ بِقَتْلِي لِأَجْلِ هَذَا الَّذِي ادَّعَيْتُ عَلَيْهِ، وَإِنِّي لَصَادِقٌ فِيمَا ادَّعَيْتُ وَلَكِنِّي كُنْتُ قَدِ اغْتَلْتُ أَبَاهُ وَقَتَلْتُهُ، وَلَمْ يَشْعُرْ بِذَلِكَ أَحَدٌ فَأَمَرَ بِهِ دَاوُدُ [عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ] فَقُتِلَ.

قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: فَاشْتَدَّتْ هَيْبَتُهُ فِي بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ وَهُوَ الَّذِي يَقُولُ اللَّهُ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ: ﴿وَشَدَدْنَا مُلْكَهُ﴾

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَآتَيْنَاهُ الْحِكْمَةَ﴾ قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: يَعْنِي: الْفَهْمَ وَالْعَقْلَ وَالْفِطْنَةَ. وَقَالَ مَرَّةً: الْحِكْمَةَ وَالْعَدْلَ. وَقَالَ مَرَّةً: الصَّوَابَ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: كِتَابَ اللَّهِ وَاتِّبَاعَ مَا فِيهِ.

وَقَالَ السُّدِّيُّ: ﴿الْحِكْمَةَ﴾ النُّبُوَّةُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَفَصْلَ الْخِطَابِ﴾ قَالَ شُرَيْحٌ الْقَاضِي وَالشَّعْبِيُّ فَصْلُ الْخِطَابِ: الشُّهُودُ وَالْأَيْمَانُ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: شَاهِدَانِ عَلَى الْمُدَّعِي أَوْ يَمِينُ الْمُدَّعَى عَلَيْهِ هُوَ فَصْلُ الْخِطَابِ الَّذِي فَصَلَ بِهِ الْأَنْبِيَاءُ وَالرُّسُلُ -أَوْ قَالَ: الْمُؤْمِنُونَ وَالصَّالِحُونَ-وَهُوَ قَضَاءُ هَذِهِ الْأُمَّةِ إِلَى يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ وَكَذَا قَالَ أَبُو عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ السُّلَمِيُّ.

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ وَالسُّدِّيُّ: هُوَ إِصَابَةُ الْقَضَاءِ وَفَهْمِهِ.

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ أَيْضًا: هُوَ الْفَصْلُ فِي الْكَلَامِ وَفِي الْحُكْمِ 

وَهَذَا يَشْمَلُ هَذَا كُلَّهُ وَهُوَ الْمُرَادُ وَاخْتَارَهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا عُمَرُ بْنُ شَبَّةَ النُّمَيْرِيُّ حَدَّثَنَا إِبْرَاهِيمُ بْنُ الْمُنْذِرِ حَدَّثَنِي عَبْدُ الْعَزِيزِ بْنُ أَبِي ثَابِتٍ عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ أَبِي الزِّنَادِ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ عَنْ بِلَالِ بْنِ أَبِي بُرْدَةَ عَنْ أَبِيهِ عَنْ أَبِي مُوسَى رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ قَالَ: أَوَّلُ مَنْ قَالَ: "أَمَّا بَعْدُ" دَاوُدُ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ وَهُوَ فَصْلُ الْخِطَابِ.

وَكَذَا قَالَ الشَّعْبِيُّ: فَصْلُ الْخِطَابِ: "أَمَّا بَعْدُ".

---

## 38:21-25 — verses 21-25 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The commentators have mentioned here a story, most of which is taken from Isra'iliyyat (Israelite narrations), and no hadith has been established from the infallible one [the Prophet ﷺ] concerning it that must be followed. However, Ibn Abi Hatim has related here a hadith whose chain of transmission is not sound, because it comes through the narration of Yazid al-Raqashi from Anas. Yazid, although he was among the righteous, is weak in hadith according to the leading scholars. Therefore it is more fitting to limit oneself to simply reciting this story and to refer knowledge of it back to God, mighty and exalted, for the Qur'an is truth, and whatever it contains is likewise truth.

As for His statement, {[when they entered upon David] and he was frightened by them}, this was because he was in his mihrab, which was the noblest place in his house, and he had commanded that no one enter upon him that day. He became aware only of two persons who had climbed over the wall into the mihrab upon him, that is, they surrounded him, asking him about their matter.

As for His statement, {and he overpowered me in speech}, it means: he overcame me. One says "azza ya'izzu" when someone subdues and overcomes.

As for His statement, {and David realized that We had only tried him}, Ali ibn Abi Talha reported from Ibn Abbas: meaning, We tested him.

As for His statement, {and he fell down bowing}, meaning: prostrating, {and turned in repentance}. It is possible that he first bowed and then prostrated afterward. It has been mentioned that he remained prostrate for forty mornings. {So We forgave him that}, meaning what had occurred from him, concerning which it is said: the good deeds of the righteous are the sins of those brought near [to God].

The leading scholars, may God be pleased with them, differed concerning the prostration in Surah Sad, as to whether it is among the obligatory prostrations of recitation, on two views. The newer position of the school of al-Shafi'i, may God have mercy on him, is that it is not among the obligatory prostrations but rather a prostration of gratitude. The evidence for this is what Imam Ahmad related, where he said:

[chain] Isma'il, that is Ibn Ulayyah, from Ayyub, from Ibn Abbas, that he said concerning the prostration in Surah Sad: it is not among the obligatory prostrations, but I saw the Messenger of God ﷺ prostrate during it.

Al-Bukhari, Abu Dawud, al-Tirmidhi, and al-Nasa'i in his tafsir related it from the hadith of Ayyub with this wording, and al-Tirmidhi said: hasan sahih (good and sound).

Al-Nasa'i also said, in his commentary on this verse: [chain] Ibrahim ibn al-Hasan, that is al-Miqsami, told us, Hajjaj ibn Muhammad told us, from Amr ibn Dharr, from his father, from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, from Ibn Abbas, may God be pleased with both of them, that the Prophet ﷺ prostrated in Surah Sad and said: "David (peace be upon him) prostrated it as repentance, and we prostrate it as gratitude."

Al-Nasa'i alone related this, and the men of its chain are all trustworthy. My shaykh, the hafiz Abu al-Hajjaj al-Mizzi, informed me, reading it to him while I listened: [chain] Abu Ishaq al-Mudarraji informed us, Zahir ibn Abi Tahir al-Thaqafi informed us, Zahir ibn Tahir al-Shahhami informed us, Abu Sa'id al-Kanjarudhi informed us, al-Hakim Abu Ahmad Muhammad ibn Muhammad al-Hafiz informed us, Abu al-Abbas al-Sarraj informed us, Harun ibn Abdullah told us, Muhammad ibn Yazid ibn Khunays told us, from al-Hasan ibn Muhammad ibn Ubaydullah ibn Abi Yazid, who said: Ibn Jurayj said to me: O Hasan, your grandfather Ubaydullah ibn Abi Yazid told me, from Ibn Abbas, who said: A man came to the Prophet ﷺ and said: O Messenger of God, I saw in a dream, as a sleeper sees, that I was praying behind a tree, and I recited the verse of prostration and prostrated, and the tree prostrated for my prostration, and I heard it say while it was prostrating: O God, record for me thereby a reward with You, and make it for me a treasure with You, and remove from me thereby a burden, and accept it from me as You accepted it from Your servant David.

Ibn Abbas said: Then I saw the Prophet ﷺ stand up and recite the verse of prostration, then prostrate, and I heard him say while prostrating what the man had related of the tree's words.

Al-Tirmidhi related it from Qutaybah, and Ibn Majah from Abu Bakr ibn Khallad, both of them from Muhammad ibn Yazid ibn Khunays, similarly, and al-Tirmidhi said: gharib (singular), we do not know it except from this route.

Al-Bukhari also said, in his commentary on it: [chain] Muhammad ibn Abdullah told us, Muhammad ibn Ubayd al-Tanafisi told us, from al-Awwam, who said: I asked Mujahid about the prostration in Surah Sad, and he said: I asked Ibn Abbas: on what basis did you prostrate? He said: Do you not recite: {And of his descendants, David and Solomon} [al-An'am: 84], {Those are the ones whom God has guided, so follow their guidance} [al-An'am: 90]. David (peace be upon him) was among those whom your Prophet ﷺ was commanded to follow. So David (peace be upon him) prostrated it, and the Messenger of God ﷺ prostrated it.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Affan told us, Yazid ibn Zurayi told us, Humayd told us, Bakr, that is Ibn Abdullah al-Muzani, told us, that Abu Sa'id al-Khudri saw a dream in which he was writing Surah Sad, and when he reached the verse where prostration occurs, he saw the inkwell and the pen and everything present with him turn over in prostration. He said: he related it to the Prophet ﷺ, and he continued to prostrate at it afterward. Ahmad alone related this.

Abu Dawud said: [chain] Ahmad ibn Salih told us, Ibn Wahb told us, Amr ibn al-Harith informed me, from Sa'id ibn Abi Hilal, from Iyad ibn Abdullah ibn Sa'd ibn Abi Sarh, from Abu Sa'id al-Khudri, may God be pleased with him, who said: The Messenger of God ﷺ recited Surah Sad while on the pulpit, and when he reached the verse of prostration, he came down and prostrated, and the people prostrated with him. Then on another day he recited it, and when he reached the verse of prostration, the people prepared themselves for prostration, so he said: "It is only the repentance of a prophet, but I saw you preparing yourselves." Then he came down and prostrated, and they prostrated. Abu Dawud alone related this, and its chain meets the standard of sound hadith.

As for His statement, {and indeed for him is nearness with Us, and a good place of return}, meaning: on the Day of Resurrection he will have a nearness by which God, mighty and exalted, will bring him close, and a good return, which is the elevated ranks in Paradise, on account of his repentance and his complete justice in his kingdom. As has come in the sound hadith: "Those who act justly will be upon pulpits of light, on the right hand of the Most Merciful, both of whose hands are right hands, those who act justly toward their families and whatever they are entrusted with."

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Yahya ibn Adam told us, Fudayl told us, from Atiyyah, from Abu Sa'id al-Khudri, who said: The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "Indeed the most beloved of people to God on the Day of Resurrection, and the nearest of them to Him in seating, is a just leader. And indeed the most hateful of people to God on the Day of Resurrection, and the most severe of them in punishment, is an unjust leader." Al-Tirmidhi related it from the hadith of Fudayl, that is Ibn Marzuq al-Aghar, from Atiyyah, with this wording, and he said: we do not know it as a marfu (elevated) report except from this route.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Abu Zur'ah told us, Abdullah ibn Abi Ziyad told us, Sayyar told us, Ja'far ibn Sulayman told us: I heard Malik ibn Dinar say concerning His statement, {and indeed for him is nearness with Us, and a good place of return}: David will be made to stand on the Day of Resurrection at the foot of the Throne, then it will be said: O David, glorify Me today with that beautiful, mellow voice with which you used to glorify Me in the world. He will say: How, when it has been taken from me? It will be said: I am returning it to you today. He said: Then David will raise his voice in a way that will exhaust the bliss of the people of the gardens of Paradise.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَدْ ذَكَرَ الْمُفَسِّرُونَ هَاهُنَا قِصَّةً أَكْثَرُهَا مَأْخُوذٌ مِنَ الْإِسْرَائِيلِيَّاتِ وَلَمْ يَثْبُتْ فِيهَا عَنِ الْمَعْصُومِ حَدِيثٌ يَجِبُ اتِّبَاعُهُ وَلَكِنْ رَوَى ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ هُنَا حَدِيثًا لَا يَصِحُّ سَنَدُهُ؛ لِأَنَّهُ مِنْ رِوَايَةِ يَزِيدَ الرَّقَاشِيِّ عَنْ أَنَسٍ -وَيَزِيدُ وَإِنْ كَانَ مِنَ الصَّالِحِينَ-لَكِنَّهُ ضَعِيفُ الْحَدِيثِ عِنْدَ الْأَئِمَّةِ فَالْأُولَى أَنْ يُقْتَصَرَ عَلَى مُجَرَّدِ تِلَاوَةِ هَذِهِ الْقِصَّةِ وَأَنْ يُرَدَّ عِلْمُهَا إِلَى اللَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ فَإِنَّ الْقُرْآنَ حَقٌّ وَمَا تَضَمَّنَ فَهُوَ حَقٌّ أَيْضًا.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿ [إِذْ دَخَلُوا عَلَى دَاوُدَ] فَفَزِعَ مِنْهُمْ﴾ إِنَّمَا كَانَ ذَلِكَ لِأَنَّهُ كَانَ فِي مِحْرَابِهِ، وَهُوَ أَشْرَفُ مَكَانٍ فِي دَارِهِ وَكَانَ قَدْ أَمَرَ أَلَّا يَدْخُلَ عَلَيْهِ أَحَدٌ ذَلِكَ الْيَوْمَ فَلَمْ يَشْعُرْ إِلَّا بِشَخْصَيْنِ قَدْ تَسَوَّرا عَلَيْهِ الْمِحْرَابَ أَيِ: احْتَاطَا بِهِ يَسْأَلَانِهِ عَنْ شَأْنِهِمَا.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَعَزَّنِي فِي الْخِطَابِ﴾ أَيْ: غَلَبَنِي يُقَالُ: عَزَّ يَعِزُّ: إِذَا قَهَرَ وَغَلَبَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَظَنَّ دَاوُدُ أَنَّمَا فَتَنَّاهُ﴾ قَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: أَيِ اخْتَبَرْنَاهُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَخَرَّ رَاكِعًا﴾ أَيْ: سَاجِدًا ﴿وَأَنَابَ﴾ وَيُحْتَمَلُ أَنَّهُ رَكَعَ أَوَّلًا ثُمَّ سَجَدَ بَعْدَ ذَلِكَ وَقَدْ ذَكَرَ أَنَّهُ اسْتَمَرَّ سَاجِدًا أَرْبَعِينَ صَبَاحًا، ﴿فَغَفَرْنَا لَهُ ذَلِكَ﴾ أَيْ: مَا كَانَ مِنْهُ مِمَّا يُقَالُ فِيهِ: إِنَّ حَسَنَاتِ الْأَبْرَارِ سَيِّئَاتُ الْمُقَرَّبِينَ.

وَقَدِ اخْتَلَفَ الْأَئِمَّةُ رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمْ فِي سَجْدَةِ "ص" هَلْ هِيَ مِنْ عَزَائِمِ السُّجُودِ؟ عَلَى قَوْلَيْنِ الْجَدِيدُ مِنْ مَذْهَبِ الشَّافِعِيِّ رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ أَنَّهَا لَيْسَتْ مِنْ عَزَائِمِ السُّجُودِ بَلْ هِيَ سَجْدَةُ شُكْرٍ. وَالدَّلِيلُ عَلَى ذَلِكَ مَا رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ حَيْثُ قَالَ:

حَدَّثَنَا إِسْمَاعِيلُ -وَهُوَ ابْنُ عُلَيَّةَ-عَنْ أَيُّوبَ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ أَنَّهُ قَالَ فِي السُّجُودِ فِي "ص": لَيْسَتْ مِنْ عَزَائِمِ السُّجُودِ وَقَدْ رَأَيْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَسْجُدُ فِيهَا.

وَرَوَاهُ الْبُخَارِيُّ وَأَبُو دَاوُدَ وَالتِّرْمِذِيُّ وَالنَّسَائِيُّ فِي تَفْسِيرِهِ مِنْ حَدِيثِ أَيُّوبَ بِهِ وَقَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: حَسَنٌ صَحِيحٌ.

وَقَالَ النَّسَائِيُّ أَيْضًا عِنْدَ تَفْسِيرِ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: أَخْبَرَنِي إِبْرَاهِيمُ بْنُ الْحَسَنِ -هُوَ الْمِقْسَمِيُّ-حَدَّثَنَا حَجَّاجُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنُ ذَرٍّ عَنْ أَبِيهِ عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا أن النَّبِيَّ ﷺ سَجَدَ فِي "ص" وَقَالَ: "سَجَدَهَا دَاوُدُ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ تَوْبَةً وَنَسْجُدُهَا شُكْرًا".

تَفَرَّدَ بِرِوَايَتِهِ النَّسَائِيُّ وَرِجَالُ إِسْنَادِهِ كُلُّهُمْ ثِقَاتٌ وَقَدْ أَخْبَرَنِي شَيْخُنَا الْحَافِظُ أَبُو الحجاج المزي قراءة عليه وأنا أسمع: أَخْبَرَنَا أَبُو إِسْحَاقَ الْمُدَرَّجِيُّ أَخْبَرَنَا زَاهِرُ بْنُ أَبِي طَاهِرٍ الثَّقَفِيُّ أَخْبَرَنَا زَاهِرُ بْنُ طَاهِرٍ الشَّحَامِيُّ، أَخْبَرَنَا أَبُو سَعِيدٍ الكَنْجَرُوذي أَخْبَرَنَا الْحَاكِمُ أَبُو أَحْمَدَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ الْحَافِظُ أَخْبَرَنَا أَبُو الْعَبَّاسِ السَّرَّاجُ حَدَّثَنَا هَارُونُ بْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ حَدَّثَنَا محمد بن يزيد ابن خُنَيْس عَنِ الْحَسَنِ بْنِ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ عَبِيدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ أَبِي يَزِيدَ قَالَ: قَالَ لِيَ ابْنُ جُرَيْجٍ: يَا حَسَنُ حَدَّثَنِي جَدُّكَ عُبَيْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ أَبِي يَزِيدَ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: جَاءَ رَجُلٌ إِلَى النَّبِيِّ ﷺ فَقَالَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ إِنِّي رَأَيْتُ فِيمَا يَرَى النَّائِمُ كَأَنِّي أُصَلِّي خَلْفَ شَجَرَةٍ فَقَرَأْتُ السَّجْدَةَ فَسَجَدْتُ فَسَجَدَتِ الشَّجَرَةُ لِسُجُودِي فَسَمِعْتُهَا تَقُولُ وَهِيَ سَاجِدَةٌ: اللَّهُمَّ اكْتُبْ لِي بِهَا عِنْدَكَ أَجْرًا وَاجْعَلْهَا لِي عِنْدَكَ ذُخْرًا وَضَعْ عَنِّي بِهَا وِزْرًا وَاقْبَلْهَا مِنِّي كَمَا قَبِلْتَهَا مِنْ عَبْدِكَ دَاوُدَ.

قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: فَرَأَيْتُ النَّبِيَّ ﷺ قَامَ فَقَرَأَ السَّجْدَةَ ثُمَّ سَجَدَ فَسَمِعْتُهُ يَقُولُ وَهُوَ سَاجِدٌ كَمَا حَكَى الرَّجُلُ مِنْ كَلَامِ الشَّجَرَةِ 

رَوَاهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ عَنْ قُتَيْبَةَ وَابْنِ مَاجَهْ عَنْ أَبِي بَكْرِ بْنِ خَلَّادٍ كِلَاهُمَا عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ يَزِيدَ بْنِ خُنَيْسٍ نَحْوَهُ وَقَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: غَرِيبٌ لَا نَعْرِفُهُ إِلَّا مِنْ هَذَا الْوَجْهِ 

وَقَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ عِنْدَ تَفْسِيرِهَا أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَبِيدِ الطَّنَافِسِيُّ عَنِ الْعَوَامِّ قَالَ: سَأَلْتُ مُجَاهِدًا عَنْ سَجْدَةِ "ص" فَقَالَ: سَأَلْتُ ابْنَ عَبَّاسٍ: مِنْ أين سجدت؟ فقال: أو ما تَقْرَأُ: ﴿وَمِنْ ذُرِّيَّتِهِ دَاوُدَ وَسُلَيْمَانَ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ:٨٤] ﴿أُولَئِكَ الَّذِينَ هَدَى اللَّهُ فَبِهُدَاهُمُ اقْتَدِهِ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ:٩٠] فَكَانَ دَاوُدُ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ مِمَّنْ أُمِرَ نَبِيُّكُمْ ﷺ أَنْ يَقْتَدِيَ بِهِ فَسَجَدَهَا دَاوُدُ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ فَسَجَدَهَا رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ 

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَفَّانُ حَدَّثَنَا يَزِيدُ بْنُ زُرَيْعٍ حَدَّثَنَا حُمَيْدٍ حَدَّثَنَا بَكْرٌ -هُوَ ابْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ الْمُزَنِيُّ-أَنَّهُ أَخْبَرَهُ أَنَّ أَبَا سَعِيدٍ الْخُدْرِيَّ رَأَى رُؤْيَا أَنَّهُ يَكْتُبُ "ص" فَلَمَّا بَلَغَ إِلَى الَّتِي يَسْجُدُ بِهَا رَأَى الدَّوَاةَ وَالْقَلَمَ وَكُلَّ شَيْءٍ بِحَضْرَتِهِ انْقَلَبَ سَاجِدًا قَالَ: فَقَصَّهَا عَلَى النَّبِيِّ ﷺ فَلَمْ يَزَلْ يَسْجُدُ بِهَا بَعْدُ. تَفَرَّدَ بِهِ [الْإِمَامُ] أَحْمَدُ 

وَقَالَ أَبُو دَاوُدَ: حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ صَالِحٍ حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ وَهْبٍ أَخْبَرَنِي عَمْرُو بْنُ الْحَارِثِ عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ أَبِي هِلَالٍ عَنْ عِيَاضِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ سَعْدِ بْنِ أَبِي سَرْحٍ عن أبي سعيد الخدري رضي اللَّهُ عَنْهُ قَالَ: قَرَأَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ وَهُوَ عَلَى الْمِنْبَرِ "ص" فَلَمَّا بَلَغَ السَّجْدَةَ نَزَلَ فَسَجَدَ وَسَجَدَ النَّاسُ مَعَهُ، فَلَمَّا كَانَ يَوْمٌ آخَرُ قَرَأَهَا فَلَمَّا بَلَغَ السَّجْدَةَ تَشَزّن النَّاسُ لِلسُّجُودِ، فَقَالَ: "إِنَّمَا هِيَ تَوْبَةُ نَبِيٍّ وَلَكِنِّي رَأَيْتُكُمْ تَشَزّنْتُم". فَنَزَلَ وَسَجَدَ وَسَجَدُوا. تَفَرَّدَ بِهِ أَبُو دَاوُدَ وَإِسْنَادُهُ عَلَى شَرْطِ الصَّحِيحِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَإِنَّ لَهُ عِنْدَنَا لَزُلْفَى وَحُسْنَ مَآبٍ﴾ أَيْ: وَإِنَّ لَهُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ لَقُرْبَةً يُقَرِّبُهُ اللَّهُ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ بِهَا وَحُسْنَ مَرْجِعٍ وَهُوَ الدَّرَجَاتُ الْعَالِيَاتُ فِي الْجَنَّةِ لِتَوْبَتِهِ وَعَدْلِهِ التَّامِّ فِي مُلْكِهِ كَمَا جَاءَ فِي الصَّحِيحِ: "الْمُقْسِطُونَ عَلَى مَنَابِرَ مِنْ نُورٍ عَنْ يَمِينِ الرَّحْمَنِ وَكِلْتَا يَدَيْهِ يَمِينٌ الَّذِينَ يُقْسِطُونَ فِي أَهْلِيهِمْ وَمَا وُلُّوا" 

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ آدَمَ، حَدَّثَنَا فُضَيْلٌ عَنْ عَطِيَّةَ عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ الْخُدْرِيِّ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنَّ أَحَبَّ النَّاسِ إِلَى اللَّهِ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ وَأَقْرَبَهُمْ مِنْهُ مَجْلِسًا إِمَامٌ عَادِلٌ وَإِنَّ أَبْغَضَ النَّاسِ إِلَى اللَّهِ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ وَأَشَدَّهُمْ عَذَابًا إِمَامٌ جَائِرٌ". وَرَوَاهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ مِنْ حَدِيثِ فُضَيْلٍ -وَهُوَ ابْنُ مَرْزُوقٍ الْأَغَرُّ-عَنْ عَطِيَّةَ بِهِ وَقَالَ: لَا نَعْرِفُهُ مَرْفُوعًا إِلَّا مِنْ هَذَا الْوَجْهِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو زُرْعَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ أَبِي زِيَادٍ حَدَّثَنَا سَيَّارٌ، حَدَّثَنَا جَعْفَرُ بْنُ سُلَيْمَانَ: سَمِعْتُ مَالِكَ بْنَ دِينَارٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَإِنَّ لَهُ عِنْدَنَا لَزُلْفَى وَحُسْنَ مَآبٍ﴾ قَالَ: يُقَامُ دَاوُدُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ عِنْدَ سَاقِ الْعَرْشِ ثُمَّ يَقُولُ: يَا دَاوُدُ مَجِّدْنِي الْيَوْمَ بِذَلِكَ الصَّوْتِ الْحَسَنِ الرَّخِيمِ الَّذِي كُنْتَ تُمَجِّدُنِي بِهِ فِي الدُّنْيَا. فَيَقُولُ: وَكَيْفَ وَقَدْ سُلِبْتُهُ؟ فَيَقُولُ: إِنِّي أَرُدُّهُ عَلَيْكَ الْيَوْمَ. قَالَ: فَيَرْفَعُ دَاوُدُ بِصَوْتٍ يَسْتَفْرِغُ نعيم أهل الجنان.

---

## 38:26 — verse 26

### Translation

This is a directive from Allah, Mighty and Majestic, to those in charge of affairs, that they should judge among people by the truth revealed from Him, Blessed and Exalted is He, and not turn away from it, thereby straying from His path. And Allah, Exalted is He, has threatened whoever strays from His path and forgets the Day of Reckoning with a firm warning and severe punishment.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: My father narrated to us, Hisham ibn Khalid narrated to us, al-Walid narrated to us, Marwan ibn Jannah narrated to us, Ibrahim Abu Zur'ah, who had read the Scripture, narrated to me, that al-Walid ibn Abd al-Malik said to him: "Will the caliph be held to account? For you have read the earlier Scripture, and you have read the Qur'an and gained understanding." So I said: "O Commander of the Faithful, may I speak?" He said: "Speak, you are safe." I said: "O Commander of the Faithful, are you more honored before Allah, or David? Allah, Mighty and Majestic, combined for him prophethood and caliphate, and yet He threatened him in His Book, saying: {O David, indeed We have made you a successor upon the earth, so judge between the people in truth and do not follow desire, for it will lead you astray from the way of Allah. Indeed, those who go astray}" the verse.

Ikrimah said concerning {For them is a severe punishment because they forgot the Day of Reckoning}: this is an instance of taqdim and ta'khir (transposition of word order), meaning: for them is a severe punishment on the Day of Reckoning because they forgot.

Al-Suddi said: for them is a severe punishment because they neglected to work for the Day of Reckoning.

This latter view follows more closely the apparent sense of the verse, and Allah knows best.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

هَذِهِ وَصِيَّةٌ مِنَ اللَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ لِوُلَاةِ الْأُمُورِ أَنْ يَحْكُمُوا بَيْنَ النَّاسِ بِالْحَقِّ الْمُنَزَّلِ مِنْ عِنْدِهِ تَبَارَكَ وَتَعَالَى وَلَا يَعْدِلُوا عَنْهُ فَيَضِلُّوا عَنْ سَبِيلِهِ وَقَدْ تَوَعَّدَ [اللَّهُ] تَعَالَى مَنْ ضَلَّ عَنْ سَبِيلِهِ، وَتَنَاسَى يَوْمَ الْحِسَابِ، بِالْوَعِيدِ الْأَكِيدِ وَالْعَذَابِ الشَّدِيدِ.

قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي حَدَّثَنَا هِشَامُ بْنُ خَالِدٍ حَدَّثَنَا الْوَلِيدُ، حَدَّثَنَا مَرْوَانُ بْنُ جَنَاحٍ، حَدَّثَنِي إِبْرَاهِيمُ أَبُو زُرْعَةَ -وَكَانَ قَدْ قَرَأَ الْكِتَابَ-أَنَّ الْوَلِيدَ بْنَ عَبْدِ الْمَلِكِ قَالَ لَهُ: أَيُحَاسَبُ الْخَلِيفَةُ فَإِنَّكَ قَدْ قَرَأْتَ الْكِتَابَ الْأَوَّلَ، وَقَرَأْتَ الْقُرْآنَ وَفَقِهْتَ؟ فَقُلْتُ: يَا أَمِيرَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ أَقُولُ؟ قَالَ: قُلْ فِي أَمَانٍ. قَلْتُ يَا أَمِيرَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ أَنْتَ أَكْرَمُ عَلَى اللَّهِ أَوْ دَاوُدُ؟ إِنِ اللَّهَ -عَزَّ وَجَلَّ-جَمَعَ لَهُ النُّبُوَّةَ وَالْخِلَافَةَ ثُمَّ تَوَعَّدَهُ فِي كِتَابِهِ فَقَالَ: ﴿يَا دَاوُدُ إِنَّا جَعَلْنَاكَ خَلِيفَةً فِي الأرْضِ فَاحْكُمْ بَيْنَ النَّاسِ بِالْحَقِّ وَلا تَتَّبِعِ الْهَوَى فَيُضِلَّكَ عَنْ سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ إِنَّ الَّذِينَ يَضِلُّونَ﴾ الْآيَةَ.

وَقَالَ عِكْرِمَةُ: ﴿لَهُمْ عَذَابٌ شَدِيدٌ بِمَا نَسُوا يَوْمَ الْحِسَابِ﴾ هَذَا مِنَ الْمُقَدَّمِ وَالْمُؤَخَّرِ لَهُمْ عَذَابٌ شَدِيدٌ يَوْمَ الْحِسَابِ بِمَا نَسُوا.

وَقَالَ السُّدِّيُّ: لَهُمْ عَذَابٌ شَدِيدٌ بِمَا تَرَكُوا أَنْ يَعْمَلُوا لِيَوْمِ الْحِسَابِ.

وَهَذَا الْقَوْلُ أَمَشَى عَلَى ظَاهِرِ الْآيَةِ فَاللَّهُ أعلم.

---

## 38:27-29 — verses 27-29 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty informs that He did not create the creation in vain, but rather created them so that they might worship Him and affirm His oneness. Then He gathers them for the Day of Gathering, rewarding the obedient and punishing the disbeliever. For this reason, the Almighty said: {And We did not create the heaven and the earth and what is between them in vain. That is the assumption of those who disbelieve} that is, those who do not believe in resurrection or return, and who hold only this worldly abode to be real. {So woe to those who disbelieve, from the Fire}, that is, woe to them on the day of their return and their resurrection, from the Fire prepared for them.

Then the Almighty explains that it is part of His justice and wisdom that He does not equate the believer with the disbeliever, so He said: {Or shall We treat those who believe and do righteous deeds like those who cause corruption in the earth? Or shall We treat the righteous like the wicked?} that is, We do not do that, and they are not equal in God's sight. Since this is so, there must necessarily be another abode in which this obedient one is rewarded and this wicked one is punished. This guidance shows sound minds and upright natural dispositions that there must be a return and a recompense, for we see the wrongdoing oppressor increase in wealth, children, and comfort, and die in that same state, while we see the obedient one who is wronged die in his grief. So it must follow, within the wisdom of the All-Wise, All-Knowing, Just One who does not wrong anyone by even the weight of a speck of dust, that there be fairness rendered between these two. And since this does not occur in this worldly abode, it is thereby established that there is another abode for this recompense and this redress. Since the Qur'an guides toward sound aims and clear rational proofs, He said: {A Book which We have sent down to you, blessed, that they may reflect upon its verses and that those of understanding may take heed} that is, those possessed of intellects, which are the albab (plural of lubb), meaning the intellect.

Al-Hasan al-Basri said: By God, reflecting upon it (tadabbur) does not consist in memorizing its letters while neglecting its limits, to the point that one of them says: "I have recited the entire Qur'an," yet no trace of the Qur'an is to be seen in his character or his deeds. Narrated by Ibn Abi Hatim.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى أَنَّهُ مَا خَلَقَ الْخَلْقَ عَبَثًا وَإِنَّمَا خَلَقَهُمْ لِيَعْبُدُوهُ وَيُوَحِّدُوهُ ثُمَّ يَجْمَعُهُمْ لِيَوْمِ الْجَمْعِ فَيُثِيبُ الْمُطِيعَ وَيُعَذِّبُ الْكَافِرَ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَا خَلَقْنَا السَّمَاءَ وَالأرْضَ وَمَا بَيْنَهُمَا بَاطِلا ذَلِكَ ظَنُّ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا﴾ أَيِ: الَّذِينَ لَا يَرَوْنَ بَعْثًا وَلَا مَعَادًا وَإِنَّمَا يَعْتَقِدُونَ هَذِهِ الدَّارَ فَقَطْ، ﴿فَوَيْلٌ لِلَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا مِنَ النَّارِ﴾ أَيْ: وَيْلٌ لَهُمْ يَوْمَ مَعَادِهِمْ وَنَشُورِهِمْ مِنَ النَّارِ الْمُعَدَّةِ لَهُمْ.

ثُمَّ بَيَّنَ تَعَالَى أَنَّهُ مِنْ عَدْلِهِ وَحِكْمَتِهِ لَا يُسَاوِي بَيْنَ الْمُؤْمِنِ وَالْكَافِرِ فَقَالَ: ﴿أَمْ نَجْعَلُ الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا وَعَمِلُوا الصَّالِحَاتِ كَالْمُفْسِدِينَ فِي الأرْضِ أَمْ نَجْعَلُ الْمُتَّقِينَ كَالْفُجَّارِ﴾ أَيْ: لَا نَفْعَلُ ذَلِكَ وَلَا يَسْتَوُونَ عِنْدَ اللَّهِ، وَإِذَا كَانَ الْأَمْرُ كَذَلِكَ فَلَا بُدَّ مِنْ دَارٍ أُخْرَى يُثَابُ فِيهَا هَذَا الْمُطِيعُ وَيُعَاقَبُ فِيهَا هَذَا الْفَاجِرُ. وَهَذَا الْإِرْشَادُ يَدُلُّ الْعُقُولَ السَّلِيمَةَ وَالْفِطَرَ الْمُسْتَقِيمَةَ عَلَى أَنَّهُ لَا بُدَّ مِنْ مَعَادٍ وَجَزَاءٍ فَإِنَّا نَرَى الظَّالِمَ الْبَاغِيَ يَزْدَادُ مَالُهُ وَوَلَدُهُ وَنَعِيمُهُ وَيَمُوتُ كَذَلِكَ وَنَرَى الْمُطِيعَ الْمَظْلُومَ يَمُوتُ بِكَمَدِهِ فَلَا بُدَّ فِي حِكْمَةِ الْحَكِيمِ الْعَلِيمِ الْعَادِلِ الَّذِي لَا يَظْلِمُ مِثْقَالَ ذَرَّةٍ مِنْ إِنْصَافِ هَذَا مِنْ هَذَا. وَإِذَا لَمْ يَقَعْ هَذَا فِي هَذِهِ الدَّارِ فَتَعَيَّنَ أَنَّ هُنَاكَ دَارًا أُخْرَى لِهَذَا الْجَزَاءِ وَالْمُوَاسَاةِ. وَلَمَّا كَانَ الْقُرْآنُ يُرْشِدُ إِلَى الْمَقَاصِدِ الصَّحِيحَةِ وَالْمَآخِذِ الْعَقْلِيَّةِ الصَّرِيحَةِ، قَالَ: ﴿كِتَابٌ أَنزلْنَاهُ إِلَيْكَ مُبَارَكٌ لِيَدَّبَّرُوا آيَاتِهِ وَلِيَتَذَكَّرَ أُولُو الألْبَابِ﴾ أَيْ: ذَوُو الْعُقُولِ وَهِيَ الْأَلْبَابُ، جَمْعُ لُبٍّ، وَهُوَ العقل.

قَالَ الْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ: وَاللَّهِ مَا تَدَبُّره بِحِفْظِ حُرُوفِهِ وَإِضَاعَةِ حُدُودِهِ، حَتَّى إِنَّ أَحَدَهُمْ لَيَقُولُ: قَرَأْتُ الْقُرْآنَ [كُلَّهُ] مَا يُرَى لَهُ القرآنُ فِي خُلُقٍ وَلَا عَمَلٍ. رَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ.

---

## 38:30-33 — verses 30-33 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, informing us that He granted David Solomon, that is, as a prophet, just as He said: {And Solomon inherited from David} meaning, in prophethood, otherwise David had other sons besides him, for he had a hundred free wives.

His saying: {An excellent servant, indeed he was one who often turned back (in repentance)} is praise of Solomon, peace be upon him, indicating that he was abundant in obedience, worship, and turning back to Allah, Mighty and Majestic.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: my father narrated to us, Mahmud ibn Khalid narrated to us, al-Walid narrated to us, Makhul narrated to us, saying: When Allah granted David Solomon, peace be upon him, David said to him: "O my son, what is most beautiful?" He said: "The tranquility of Allah and faith." He said: "What is most ugly?" He said: "Disbelief after faith." He said: "What is sweetest?" He said: "The mercy of Allah among His servants." He said: "What is coolest?" He said: "The pardon of Allah toward people, and the pardon of people toward one another." David, peace be upon him, said: "Then you are a prophet."

His saying: {When there were displayed before him in the evening the standing, swift horses} means, when there were displayed before Solomon, during the time of his kingship and dominion, the standing horses.

Mujahid said: these are the horses that stand on three legs with the tip of the fourth hoof, and al-jiyad (the swift ones) means the fast ones. Others among the early generations said the same.

Ibn Jarir said: Muhammad ibn Bashshar narrated to us, Muammal narrated to us, Sufyan narrated to us from his father Sa'id ibn Masruq, from Ibrahim al-Taymi, regarding His saying: {When there were displayed before him in the evening the standing, swift horses}, he said: they were twenty horses possessing wings. This is how Ibn Jarir related it.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: Abu Zur'ah narrated to us, Ibrahim ibn Musa narrated to us, Ibn Abi Za'idah narrated to us, Isra'il informed me from Sa'id ibn Masruq, from Ibrahim al-Taymi, who said: the horses that occupied Solomon, upon him be prayer and peace, were twenty thousand horses, and he slaughtered them. This is more plausible, and Allah knows best.

Abu Dawud said: Muhammad ibn Awf narrated to us, Sa'id ibn Abi Maryam narrated to us, Yahya ibn Ayyub informed us, Umarah ibn Ghaziyyah narrated to me: that Muhammad ibn Ibrahim narrated to him from Abu Salamah ibn Abd al-Rahman, from Aisha, may Allah be pleased with her, who said: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ returned from the expedition of Tabuk, or Khaybar, and in her alcove there was a curtain. A wind blew and lifted one side of the curtain, revealing some dolls belonging to Aisha, which were toys. He said: "What is this, O Aisha?" She said: "My dolls." And he saw among them a horse with two wings made of patches, and he said: "What is this that I see among them?" She said: "A horse." He said: "And what is this upon it?" She said: "Two wings." He said: "A horse with two wings?!" She said: "Have you not heard that Solomon had horses with wings?" She said: he laughed until I saw his molars, ﷺ.

His saying: {And he said: Indeed, I have preferred the love of good things over the remembrance of my Lord, until it disappeared behind the veil} several among the early generations and the exegetes mentioned that he became occupied with reviewing them until the time of the Asr prayer had passed. What is certain is that he did not abandon it deliberately but out of forgetfulness, just as the Prophet ﷺ was occupied on the day of the Trench and missed the Asr prayer until he prayed it after sunset. This is established in the two Sahihs through more than one route. Among them, from Jabir, who said: Umar, may Allah be pleased with him, came on the day of the Trench after the sun had set, and he began cursing the disbelievers of Quraysh, saying: "O Messenger of Allah, by Allah I nearly did not pray Asr until the sun was about to set." The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "By Allah, I have not prayed it either." He said: so we got up and went to Buthan, and he performed ablution for the prayer and we performed ablution with him, and he prayed Asr after the sun had set, then he prayed Maghrib after it.

It is also possible that in their religious law it was permissible to delay the prayer for the excuse of raiding and fighting, and horses were sought for battle. A group of scholars has claimed that this was legislated and then abrogated by the prayer of fear (salat al-khawf), while others held that this applied specifically to the state of close combat and pressing engagement, where prayer, bowing, and prostration were not possible, as the companions, may Allah be pleased with them, did at the conquest of Tustar. This is reported from Makhul, al-Awza'i, and others. The first view is closer to the truth, because after this He says: {Return them to me}, so he began to stroke their legs and necks.

Al-Hasan al-Basri said: he said: "No, by Allah, you will not distract me from the worship of my Lord any longer than you already have." Then he ordered them, and they were slaughtered. Qatadah said the same.

Al-Suddi said: he struck their necks and hamstrings with swords.

Ali ibn Abi Talhah reported from Ibn Abbas: he began to stroke the manes of the horses, and their "araqib" (hamstrings) means their ropes (i.e., he was untying them). Ibn Jarir chose this view, saying: because he would not torment an animal by hamstringing it and destroy some of his own wealth without cause, merely because he had been distracted from his prayer by looking at them, when the horses bore no blame for that. This preference of Ibn Jarir's is open to question, because it may be that in their religious law such an act was permissible, especially if it was done in anger for the sake of Allah, Mighty and Majestic, on account of having been occupied with them until the time of prayer had passed. This is why, when he gave them up for the sake of Allah, the Almighty compensated him with something better than them, namely the wind that ran by His command gently, such that its morning course covered a month's journey and its evening course covered a month's journey. This is faster and better than horses.
