Imam Ahmad said: Isma'il narrated to us, Sulayman ibn al-Mughirah narrated to us, from Humayd ibn Hilal, from Abu Qatadah and Abu al-Dahma, who used to travel frequently toward the House, and they said: we came upon a man from the people of the desert, and the Bedouin said: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ took my hand and began teaching me from what Allah, the Almighty, had taught him, and he said: "You do not give up anything for fear of Allah, Mighty and Majestic, except that Allah gives you something better than it."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا أَنَّهُ وَهَبَ لِدَاوُدَ سُلَيْمَانَ، أَيْ: نَبِيًّا كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿وَوَرِثَ سُلَيْمَانُ دَاوُدَ﴾ أَيْ: فِي النُّبُوَّةِ وَإِلَّا فَقَدَ كَانَ لَهُ بَنُونَ غَيْرُهُ، فَإِنَّهُ قَدْ كَانَ عِنْدَهُ مِائَةُ امْرَأَةٍ حَرَائِرَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿نِعْمَ الْعَبْدُ إِنَّهُ أَوَّابٌ﴾ ثَنَاءٌ عَلَى سُلَيْمَانَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، بِأَنَّهُ كَثِيرُ الطَّاعَةِ وَالْعِبَادَةِ وَالْإِنَابَةِ إِلَى اللَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ.

قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي حَدَّثَنَا مَحْمُودُ بْنُ خَالِدٍ حَدَّثَنَا الْوَلِيدُ حَدَّثَنَا مَكْحُولٌ قَالَ: لَمَّا وَهَبَ اللَّهُ لِدَاوُدَ سُلَيْمَانَ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ قَالَ لَهُ: يَا بُنَيَّ مَا أَحْسَنُ؟ قَالَ: سَكِينَةُ اللَّهِ وَإِيمَانٌ. قَالَ: فَمَا أَقْبَحُ؟ قَالَ: كَفْرٌ بَعْدَ إِيمَانٍ. قَالَ: فَمَا أَحْلَى؟ قَالَ: رَوْحُ اللَّهِ بَيْنَ عِبَادِهِ. قَالَ: فَمَا أَبْرَدُ؟ قَالَ: عَفْوُ اللَّهِ عَنِ النَّاسِ وَعَفْوُ النَّاسِ بَعْضِهِمْ عَنْ بَعْضٍ. قَالَ دَاوُدُ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ: فَأَنْتَ نَبِيٌّ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِذْ عُرِضَ عَلَيْهِ بِالْعَشِيِّ الصَّافِنَاتُ الْجِيَادُ﴾ أَيْ: إِذْ عُرِضَ عَلَى سُلَيْمَانَ فِي حَالِ مَمْلَكَتِهِ وَسُلْطَانِهِ الْخَيْلُ الصَّافِنَاتُ.

قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: وَهِيَ الَّتِي تَقِفُ عَلَى ثَلَاثٍ وَطَرَفِ حَافِرِ الرَّابِعَةِ، وَالْجِيَادُ: السِّرَاعُ. وَكَذَا قَالَ غَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ مِنَ السَّلَفِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ بَشَّارٍ حَدَّثَنَا مُؤمَّل حَدَّثَنَا سُفْيَانُ عَنْ أَبِيهِ سَعِيدِ بْنِ مَسْرُوقٍ عَنْ إِبْرَاهِيمَ التَّيْمِيِّ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿إِذْ عُرِضَ عَلَيْهِ بِالْعَشِيِّ الصَّافِنَاتُ الْجِيَادُ﴾ قَالَ: كَانَتْ عِشْرِينَ فَرَسًا ذَاتَ أَجْنِحَةٍ. كَذَا رَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو زُرْعَةَ حَدَّثَنَا إِبْرَاهِيمُ بْنُ مُوسَى حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ أَبِي زَائِدَةَ أَخْبَرَنِي إِسْرَائِيلُ عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ مَسْرُوقٍ عَنْ إِبْرَاهِيمَ التَّيْمِيِّ قَالَ: كَانَتِ الْخَيْلُ الَّتِي شَغَلَتْ سُلَيْمَانَ، عَلَيْهِ الصَّلَاةُ وَالسَّلَامُ عِشْرِينَ أَلْفَ فَرَسٍ، فَعَقَرَهَا وَهَذَا أَشْبَهُ وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَقَالَ أَبُو دَاوُدَ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَوْفٍ، حَدَّثَنَا سَعِيدُ بْنُ أَبِي مَرْيَمَ أَخْبَرَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ أَيُّوبَ حَدَّثَنِي عُمَارة بْنُ غَزيَّة: أَنَّ مُحَمَّدَ بْنَ إِبْرَاهِيمَ حَدَّثَهُ عَنْ أَبِي سَلَمَةَ بْنِ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ عَنْ عائشة رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا قَالَتْ: قَدِمَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ مِنْ غَزْوَةِ تَبُوكَ -أَوْ خَيْبَرَ-وَفِي سَهْوَتِهَا سَتْرٌ فَهَبَّتِ الرِّيحُ فَكَشَفَتْ نَاحِيَةَ السَّتْرِ عَنْ بَنَاتٍ لِعَائِشَةَ -لُعَب-فَقَالَ: "مَا هَذَا يَا عَائِشَةُ؟ " قَالَتْ: بَنَاتِي. وَرَأَى بَيْنَهُنَّ فَرَسًا لَهُ جَنَاحَانِ مِنْ رِقَاعٍ فَقَالَ: "مَا هَذَا الَّذِي أَرَى وَسَطَهُنَّ؟ " قَالَتْ: فَرَسٌ. قَالَ: "وَمَا هَذَا الَّذِي عَلَيْهِ؟ " قَالَتْ: جَنَاحَانِ قَالَ: "فَرَسٌ لَهُ جَنَاحَانِ؟! " قَالَتْ: أَمَا سَمِعْتَ أَنَّ لِسُلَيْمَانَ خَيْلٌ لَهَا أَجْنِحَةٌ؟ قَالَتْ: فَضَحِكَ حَتَّى رَأَيْتُ نَوَاجِذَهُ ﷺ 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَقَالَ إِنِّي أَحْبَبْتُ حُبَّ الْخَيْرِ عَنْ ذِكْرِ رَبِّي حَتَّى تَوَارَتْ بِالْحِجَابِ﴾ ذَكَرَ غَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ مِنَ السَّلَفِ وَالْمُفَسِّرِينَ أَنَّهُ اشْتَغَلَ بِعَرْضِهَا حَتَّى فَاتَ وَقْتُ صَلَاةِ الْعَصْرِ وَالَّذِي يُقْطَعُ بِهِ أَنَّهُ لَمْ يَتْرُكْهَا عَمْدًا بَلْ نِسْيَانًا كَمَا شُغِلَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ يَوْمَ الْخَنْدَقِ عَنْ صَلَاةِ الْعَصْرِ حَتَّى صَلَّاهَا بَعْدَ الْغُرُوبِ وَذَلِكَ ثَابِتٌ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ مِنْ غَيْرِ وَجْهٍ، مِنْ ذَلِكَ عَنْ جَابِرٍ قَالَ: جَاءَ عُمَرُ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ يَوْمَ الْخَنْدَقِ بَعْدَ مَا غَرَبَتِ الشَّمْسُ فَجَعَلَ يَسُبُّ كُفَّارَ قُرَيْشٍ، وَيَقُولُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، وَاللَّهِ مَا كِدْتُ أُصَلِّي الْعَصْرَ حَتَّى كَادَتِ الشَّمْسُ تَغْرُبُ. فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "وَاللَّهِ مَا صَلَّيْتُهَا" فَقَالَ: فَقُمْنَا إِلَى بُطْحَان فَتَوَضَّأَ لِلصَّلَاةِ وَتَوَضَّأْنَا لَهَا فَصَلَّى الْعَصْرَ بَعْدَ مَا غَرَبَتِ الشَّمْسُ ثُمَّ صَلَّى بَعْدَهَا الْمَغْرِبَ 

وَيُحْتَمَلُ أَنَّهُ كَانَ سَائِغًا فِي مِلَّتِهِمْ تَأْخِيرُ الصَّلَاةِ لِعُذْرِ الْغَزْوِ وَالْقِتَالِ. وَالْخَيْلُ تُرَادُ لِلْقِتَالِ. وَقَدِ ادَّعَى طَائِفَةٌ مِنَ الْعُلَمَاءِ أَنَّ هَذَا كَانَ مَشْرُوعًا فَنُسِخَ ذَلِكَ بِصَلَاةِ الْخَوْفِ وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ ذَهَبَ إِلَى ذَلِكَ فِي حَالِ الْمُسَايَفَةِ وَالْمُضَايَقَةِ، حَيْثُ لَا يُمْكِنُ صَلَاةٌ وَلَا رُكُوعٌ وَلَا سُجُودٌ كَمَا فَعَلَ الصَّحَابَةُ رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمْ فِي فَتْحِ تُسْتَرَ، وَهُوَ مَنْقُولٌ عَنْ مَكْحُولٍ وَالْأَوْزَاعِيِّ وَغَيْرِهِمَا وَالْأَوَّلُ أُقَرَبُ؛ لِأَنَّهُ قَالَ بَعْدَهَا: ﴿رُدُّوهَا عَلَيَّ فَطَفِقَ مَسْحًا بِالسُّوقِ وَالأعْنَاقِ﴾

قَالَ الْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ. قَالَ: لَا وَاللَّهِ لَا تَشْغَلِينِي عَنْ عِبَادَةِ رَبِّي آخِرَ مَا عَلَيْكِ. ثُمَّ أَمَرَ بِهَا فَعُقِرَتْ. وَكَذَا قَالَ قَتَادَةُ.

وَقَالَ السُّدِّيُّ: ضَرَبَ أَعْنَاقَهَا وَعَرَاقِيبَهَا بِالسُّيُوفِ.

وَقَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: جَعَلَ يَمْسَحُ أَعْرَافَ الْخَيْلِ، وَعَرَاقِيبُهَا حِبَالُهَا. وَهَذَا الْقَوْلُ اخْتَارَهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ قَالَ: لِأَنَّهُ لَمْ يَكُنْ لِيُعَذِّبَ حَيَوَانًا بِالْعَرْقَبَةِ وَيُهْلِكَ مَالًا مِنْ مَالِهِ بِلَا سَبَبٍ سِوَى أَنَّهُ اشْتَغَلَ عَنْ صِلَاتِهِ بِالنَّظَرِ إِلَيْهَا وَلَا ذَنْبَ لَهَا. وَهَذَا الَّذِي رَجَّحَ بِهِ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ فِيهِ نَظَرٌ؛ لِأَنَّهُ قَدْ يَكُونُ فِي شَرْعِهِمْ جَوَازُ مِثْلِ هَذَا وَلَا سِيَّمَا إِذَا كَانَ غَضَبًا لله عز وجل بسبب أنه اشْتَغَلَ بِهَا حَتَّى خَرَجَ وَقْتُ الصَّلَاةِ؛ وَلِهَذَا لَمَّا خَرَجَ عَنْهَا لِلَّهِ تَعَالَى عَوَّضَهُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى مَا هُوَ خَيْرٌ مِنْهَا وَهِيَ الرِّيحُ الَّتِي تَجْرِي بِأَمْرِهِ رُخَاءً حَيْثُ أَصَابَ غُدُوُّهَا شَهْرٌ وَرَوَاحُهَا شَهْرٌ فَهَذَا أَسْرَعُ وَخَيْرٌ مِنَ الْخَيْلِ 

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا إِسْمَاعِيلُ حَدَّثَنَا سُلَيْمَانُ بْنُ الْمُغِيرَةِ عَنْ حُمَيْدِ بْنِ هِلَالٍ عَنْ أَبِي قَتَادَةَ وَأَبِي الدَّهْمَاءِ -وَكَانَا يُكْثِرَانِ السَّفَرَ نَحْوَ الْبَيْتِ-قَالَا أَتَيْنَا عَلَى رَجُلٍ مِنْ أَهْلِ الْبَادِيَةِ، فَقَالَ الْبَدَوِيُّ: أَخَذَ بِيَدِي رَسُولُ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ وسلم فجعل يُعَلِّمُنِي مِمَّا عَلَّمَهُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى وَقَالَ: "إِنَّكَ لَا تَدَعُ شَيْئًا اتِّقَاءَ اللَّهِ -عَزَّ وَجَلَّ-إِلَّا أَعْطَاكَ اللَّهُ خَيْرًا مِنْهُ"

---

## 38:34-40 — verses 34-40 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Allah, exalted is He, says: {And indeed We tried Solomon} that is: We tested him by stripping him of his kingdom for a time, {and We cast upon his throne a body}. Ibn 'Abbas, Mujahid, Sa'id ibn Jubayr, al-Hasan, Qatadah and others said: meaning a devil (shaytan). {Then he turned in repentance} that is: he returned to his kingdom, his authority, and his majesty.

Ibn Jarir said: that devil's name was Sakhr. This was said by Ibn 'Abbas and Qatadah. It was also said: Asif, said by Mujahid. And it was said: Asirun, also said by Mujahid. And it was said: Habaqiq, said by al-Suddi. They have related this story at length and in brief.

Sa'id ibn Abi 'Arubah reported from Qatadah, who said: Solomon, peace be upon him, was commanded to build the Sacred House (Bayt al-Maqdis), and it was said to him: build it, and let no sound of iron be heard in it. He sought a means to do this but could not manage it. Then it was said to him: there is a devil in the sea called "Sakhr," resembling a rebellious jinn. So he sought him out. There was a spring in the sea which the devil would visit once every seven days. Its water was drained out and wine was put in its place. He came on the day of his visit and found the wine there, and said: "You are indeed a good drink, except that you make the forbearing man foolish and increase the ignorant man in ignorance." Then he went away until he became extremely thirsty, and returned to it and said the same words again. Then he drank it until it overcame his reason. Then, it is said, he was shown the seal, or the seal was placed between his shoulders, and he became subdued. His kingdom, it is said, resided in his seal ring. He was brought to Solomon, who said: "We have been commanded to build this House, and it has been said to us that no sound of iron should be heard in it." So the devil brought a hoopoe's egg and placed a piece of glass over it. The hoopoe came and circled around it, seeing its egg but unable to reach it. It went away and brought back diamond and placed it upon the glass, cutting through it until it reached its egg. So the diamond was taken, and they began to cut stones with it.

Now Solomon, peace be upon him, when he wished to enter the privy, or the bathhouse, would not take his seal ring in with him. One day he went to the bathhouse, and that devil Sakhr was with him, at a time when he had had relations with one of his wives. He entered the bathhouse and gave the devil his seal ring to hold. The devil then cast it into the sea, where a fish swallowed it. Solomon's kingdom was stripped from him, and the devil's appearance was made to resemble Solomon's. The devil came and sat upon his throne and his seat, and was given power over the whole of Solomon's kingdom except his wives. He began to judge among the people, and they began to notice things amiss in him, until they said: "The Prophet of Allah has indeed been afflicted with madness." Among them was a man they likened to 'Umar ibn al-Khattab in strength, who said: "By Allah, I shall test him." He said: "O Prophet of Allah," believing him truly to be the Prophet of Allah, "if one of us is in a state of ritual impurity on a cold night and deliberately delays the ritual washing until sunrise, do you see any blame upon him?" He said: "No." This continued for forty nights, until the Prophet of Allah found his seal ring in the belly of a fish. He returned, and no jinn or bird encountered him without prostrating to him, until he reached them. {And We cast upon his throne a body}: he said, this refers to the devil Sakhr.

Al-Suddi said: {And indeed We tried Solomon}, that is, We tested Solomon. {And We cast upon his throne a body}: he said, the devil sat upon his throne for forty days. Solomon, peace be upon him, had a hundred wives, one of whom was called "Jaradah," who was the most favored of his wives and the one he trusted most. When he was in a state of ritual impurity or had some need, he would remove his seal ring, entrusting it to no one but her. One day he gave her his seal ring and entered the privy. The devil came out in his form and said to her: "Give me the seal ring." She gave it to him. He came and sat in Solomon's place of judgment. When Solomon came out afterward, he asked her for his seal ring. She said: "Did you not take it earlier?" He said: "No," and went out in that state, bewildered. The devil remained ruling among the people for forty days. The people came to disapprove of his judgments, so the reciters and scholars of the Children of Israel gathered and went to his wives and said: "We have found this objectionable. If this is Solomon, then his reason has left him, and we reject his judgments." The women wept at this. Then the people came and surrounded him, and unrolled the Torah and read from it. He flew away from before them until he landed upon a parapet, still with the ring, then flew on until he went to the sea, where the ring fell from him into the sea and was swallowed by one of the sea's fish. Solomon meanwhile continued in the state he was in, until he came to a fisherman of the sea, being hungry, indeed extremely hungry. He asked them for food from their catch and said: "I am Solomon." One of them rose up and struck him with a stick, wounding his head, and he began to wash away the blood while on the shore. The other fishermen blamed their companion who had struck him, saying: "How wretched was what you did in striking him." He said: "He claimed to be Solomon." They gave him two fish that had gone bad among their catch. Despite the pain of the blow, he went to the seashore and slit open their bellies, and while washing away his blood he found his ring in the belly of one of them. He took it, put it on, and Allah restored to him his splendor and his kingdom. The birds came and hovered over him, and the people recognized that he was Solomon, peace be upon him. They came forward apologizing for what they had done to him, but he said: "I neither commend you for your excuse nor blame you for what happened, for this matter was destined to occur." He returned to his kingdom and sent for the devil, who was brought to him. He ordered him placed in a chest of iron, which was then sealed shut, locked with a lock, and stamped with his seal ring. Then he ordered it cast into the sea, where it remains until the Hour comes. His name was Habaqiq. Solomon said: "And He subjected the wind to him," which had not been subjected to him before that, and this is referred to in His words: {Grant me a kingdom such as will not befit anyone after me. Indeed, You are the Bestower.}

Ibn Abi Najih reported from Mujahid concerning His words {And We cast upon his throne a body}: he said, a devil called Asif. Solomon said to him: "How is it that you tempt people?" He said: "Show me your seal ring, and I will tell you." When Solomon gave it to him, Asif cast it into the sea, and Solomon wandered off and his kingdom departed from him. Asif sat upon his throne, and Allah prevented him from approaching Solomon's wives, and they refused him and rejected him. Solomon would ask for food, saying: "Do you know me? Feed me, I am Solomon," but they would deny him, until one day a woman gave him a fish, and as he was cleaning its belly, he found his ring inside it. His kingdom then returned to him, and Asif fled, entering the sea in flight.

All of these are from the Isra'iliyyat (narrations of Israelite origin), and among the most objectionable of them is what Ibn Abi Hatim reported:

[chain] ... from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, from Ibn 'Abbas, may Allah be pleased with them both, concerning {And We cast upon his throne a body, then he turned in repentance}: he said, Solomon wished to enter the privy, so he gave his seal ring to Jaradah, who was his wife and the most beloved of his wives to him. The devil then came in the form of Solomon and said to her: "Give me my seal ring." She gave it to him. When he put it on, mankind, the jinn, and the devils submitted to him. When Solomon came out of the privy, he said to her: "Give me my seal ring." She said: "I have already given it to Solomon." He said: "I am Solomon." She said: "You lie, you are not Solomon." Wherever he went afterward, saying "I am Solomon," he was disbelieved, until children began throwing stones at him. When he saw this, he recognized that it was from the decree of Allah, Mighty and Majestic. The devil arose to judge among the people. When Allah wished to restore Solomon's authority to him, He cast into people's hearts a rejection of that devil. They sent to Solomon's wives and said to them: "Do you find anything objectionable in Solomon?" They said: "Yes, he comes to us while we are menstruating, which he never did before." When the devil saw that he had been discovered, he thought that his time was over. So they wrote documents containing sorcery and disbelief, and buried them beneath Solomon's throne, then dug them up again and read them out to the people.

They said: it was by means of this that Sulayman used to prevail over people [and overcome them]. So the people declared Sulayman (peace be upon him) to be a disbeliever, and they kept declaring him so. That devil then took the ring and threw it into the sea, and a fish met it and swallowed it. Sulayman had been working as a porter on the shore of the sea for wages. A man came and bought fish, among which was that fish which had the ring in its belly. Sulayman called out to him and said: "Will you let me carry this fish for you?" He said: "Yes." He said: "For what payment?" He said: "For one fish from these fish." Sulayman (peace be upon him) then carried the fish and set off with it to the man's house. When the man reached his door, he gave him that fish which had the ring in its belly. Sulayman took it and split open its belly, and there was the ring inside it. He took it and put it on.

He said: when he put it on, the jinn, mankind, and the devils submitted to him, and he returned to his former state. The devil fled until he entered one of the islands of the sea. Sulayman sent people in search of him, for he was a rebellious devil. They kept searching for him and could not overpower him, until one day they found him asleep. They came and built a structure of lead around him. He woke up and leapt up, but wherever he leapt in the house he found lead matting with him. He said: they seized him, bound him fast, and brought him to Sulayman. He ordered that a chest be hollowed out of marble, and he was placed inside it, then it was sealed with copper, and then he ordered it thrown into the sea. That is the meaning of His saying: {And indeed We tried Sulayman and placed upon his throne a body, then he turned in repentance}. He said: meaning the devil who had been given power over him.

Its chain of transmission back to Ibn Abbas is strong, but it appears that Ibn Abbas, if it is indeed authentically attributed to him, received it from the People of the Book, among whom there is a group who do not believe in the prophethood of Sulayman (peace be upon him). It therefore appears that they lied about him. For this reason the account contains objectionable elements, the most serious of which is the mention of the women, for it is well known that that jinn was not given power over the wives of Sulayman. Rather, God protected them from him, as an honor and a mark of dignity for His prophet ﷺ. This story has been narrated at length from a group of the early generations, such as Sa'id ibn al-Musayyab, Zayd ibn Aslam, and others, but all of it is received from the tales of the People of the Book. And God knows best what is correct.

Yahya ibn Abi Amr al-Saybani said: Sulayman found his ring in Ascalon, and he walked in a piece of cloth to Bayt al-Maqdis out of humility before God, Mighty and Majestic. This was narrated by Ibn Abi Hatim.

Ibn Abi Hatim narrated from Ka'b al-Ahbar, concerning the description of the throne of Sulayman (peace and blessings be upon him), an astonishing report. He said: [chain] Abu Ishaq al-Misri narrated to me from Ka'b al-Ahbar, that when he had finished the account of "Iram of the Pillars," Mu'awiya said to him: "O Abu Ishaq, tell me about the throne of Sulayman ibn Dawud, what was upon it, and of what it was made." He said: "The throne of Sulayman was made of elephant tusks, inlaid with pearls, rubies, chrysolite, and pearls. A step was made for it, likewise inlaid with pearls, rubies, and chrysolite. Then he ordered that the throne be surrounded on both sides with palm trees, palm trees of gold whose clusters were of ruby, chrysolite, and pearl. On the tops of the palm trees to the right of the throne were placed peacocks of gold, and on the tops of the palm trees to the left of the throne were placed eagles of gold, facing the peacocks. To the right of the first step were placed two pine trees of gold, and to its left two lions of gold, and on the heads of the two lions were two pillars of chrysolite. On both sides of the throne were placed two grapevines of gold that shaded the throne, and their clusters were made of pearl and red ruby. Then above the steps of the throne were placed two great lions of gold, hollow and filled with musk and ambergris.

"When Sulayman wished to ascend his throne, the two lions would rotate for a moment and then settle, spraying out what was in their bellies of musk and ambergris around the throne of Sulayman (peace be upon him). Then two pulpits of gold would be set out, one for his deputy and the other for the chief of the rabbis of the Children of Israel of that time. Then in front of his throne would be placed seventy pulpits of gold, upon which would sit seventy judges from the Children of Israel, their scholars, and their people of nobility and standing. Behind all these pulpits were thirty-five pulpits of gold with no one upon them.

"When he wished to ascend his throne, he would place his feet on the lowest step, and the whole throne, with everything in it and upon it, would rotate. The lion would extend its right paw and the eagle would spread its left wing. Then Sulayman would ascend to the second step, and the lion would extend its left paw and the eagle would spread its right wing. When Sulayman settled onto the third step and sat upon the throne, a great eagle from among those eagles would take Sulayman's crown and place it upon his head. When it placed it upon his head, the throne would rotate with everything in it, as a fast-turning millstone rotates."

Mu'awiya, may God be pleased with him, said: "And what is it that makes it rotate, O Abu Ishaq?" He said: "A great dragon of gold belonging to that throne, which was made by Sakhr the jinni. When the eagles, lions, and peacocks that were at the base of the throne sensed its rotation, they would turn toward its top, and when it stopped, they would all stop, with their heads bowed down toward the head of Sulayman ibn Dawud (peace be upon him) as he sat, and then they would all spray out what was in their bellies of musk and ambergris upon the head of Sulayman (peace be upon him). Then a dove of gold standing upon a pillar of jewels would take the Torah and place it in his hand, and Sulayman would read it to the people."

He mentioned the rest of the report, and it is gharib (singular) in the extreme.

{He said: My Lord, forgive me and grant me a kingdom that will not belong to anyone after me. Indeed You are the Bestower.} Some of them said: its meaning is "that will not belong to anyone after me," that is, it is not fitting for anyone to strip it from me, as happened in the matter of the body that was cast upon his throne, not that it forbids anyone after him among people from having such a kingdom. But the correct view is that he asked God, exalted is He, for a kingdom the like of which would not belong to anyone among mankind after him. This is the apparent meaning of the passage of the verse, and it is what is reported in the authentic hadiths transmitted through several chains from the Messenger of God ﷺ.

Al-Bukhari said, in the commentary on this verse: [chain] Abu Hurayrah, may God be pleased with him, from the Prophet ﷺ, said: "A rebellious jinn attacked me last night, or words to that effect, to interrupt my prayer, but God enabled me to overpower him. I wanted to tie him to one of the pillars of the mosque so that you could all wake up in the morning and look at him, but then I remembered the saying of my brother Sulayman: {My Lord, forgive me and grant me a kingdom that will not belong to anyone after me}"

Rawh said: "So he sent him away, rebuffed and disgraced."

This was likewise narrated by Muslim and al-Nasa'i through the hadith of Shu'bah, with the same content.

Muslim said in his Sahih: [chain] Abu al-Darda said: The Messenger of God ﷺ stood up to pray, and we heard him say: "I seek refuge in God from you." Then he said: "I curse you with the curse of God," three times, and he stretched out his hand as though he were taking hold of something. When he finished the prayer, we said: "O Messenger of God, we heard you say something in the prayer that we had not heard you say before, and we saw you stretch out your hand." He said: "The enemy of God, Iblis, came with a flame of fire to place it on my face. I said: 'I seek refuge in God from you,' three times. Then I said: 'I curse you with the complete curse of God.'"

It did not delay for three times, and then I wanted to seize it. By Allah, had it not been for the supplication of our brother Sulayman, it would have woken up bound, with the children of the city's people playing with it."

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Abu Ubayd, chamberlain of Sulayman, said: I saw Ata' ibn Yazid al-Layth standing in prayer, and I went to pass in front of him, but he stopped me. Then he said: Abu Sa'id al-Khudri narrated to me that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ stood to pray the dawn prayer while he was behind him, and he recited, but the recitation became confused for him. When he finished his prayer he said: "Had you seen me and Iblis, I reached out with my hand and did not stop strangling him until I felt the coolness of his saliva between these two fingers of mine, the thumb and the one next to it. Had it not been for the supplication of my brother Sulayman, he would have woken up tied to one of the pillars of the mosque, with the children of Madinah playing with him. So whoever among you is able to prevent anyone from coming between him and the qibla, let him do so."

Abu Dawud narrated from this: "Whoever among you is able to prevent anyone from coming between him and the qibla, let him do so," from Ahmad ibn Abi Surayj, from Abu Ahmad al-Zubayri, with the same chain.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Abdullah al-Daylami said: I entered upon Abdullah ibn Amr while he was in an orchard of his in Ta'if called "al-Wahat," and he was walking arm in arm with a young man from Quraysh who was suspected of drinking wine. I said: A hadith has reached me from you that "whoever drinks a draught of wine, Allah, mighty and majestic, will not accept his repentance for forty mornings, and the wretched one is he who was made wretched in his mother's womb, and whoever comes to Bayt al-Maqdis intending nothing but prayer in it will emerge from his sin as on the day his mother bore him." When the young man heard the mention of wine, he pulled his hand away from his and left. Abdullah ibn Amr said: I do not permit anyone to attribute to me what I did not say. I heard the Messenger of Allah ﷺ say: "Whoever drinks a draught of wine, his prayer will not be accepted for forty mornings. If he repents, Allah will accept his repentance. If he returns to it, his prayer will not be accepted for forty mornings. If he repents, Allah will accept his repentance. If he returns to it," he said, I do not know whether this was the third or fourth time, "if he returns to it, it becomes incumbent upon Allah to give him to drink from Radghat al-Khabal (the mire of corruption) on the Day of Resurrection." He said: And I heard the Messenger of Allah ﷺ say: "Allah created His creation in darkness, then cast upon them some of His light. Whoever was touched by His light on that day was guided, and whoever missed it went astray. That is why I say the pen has dried upon the knowledge of Allah, mighty and majestic." And I heard the Messenger of Allah ﷺ say: "Sulayman asked Allah, exalted is He, for three things, and He gave him two, and we hope that the third will be ours. He asked Him for a judgment that would match His judgment, and He gave it to him. He asked Him for a dominion that would not be fitting for anyone after him, and He gave it to him. And he asked that whichever man leaves his house intending nothing but prayer in this mosque should emerge from his sin as on the day his mother bore him. So we hope that Allah, exalted is He, has given us this one."

This last portion of this hadith was narrated by al-Nasa'i and Ibn Majah through several chains from Abdullah ibn Fayruz al-Daylami, from Abdullah ibn Amr, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "When Sulayman built Bayt al-Maqdis, he asked his Lord, mighty and majestic, for three qualities..." and he mentioned it.

It has also been narrated from the hadith of Rafi' ibn Umayr, may Allah be pleased with him, with a gharib (singular) chain and wording. Al-Tabarani said:

[chain] Rafi' ibn Umayr said: I heard the Messenger of Allah ﷺ say: "Allah, mighty and majestic, said to Dawud (peace be upon him): Build for Me a house on the earth. So Dawud built a house for himself before the house he had been commanded to build. Allah revealed to him: O Dawud, you erected your house before My house? He said: O Lord, thus have You decreed, whoever holds dominion claims priority for himself. Then he began building the mosque, and when the wall was completed, it collapsed three times. He complained of this to Allah, mighty and majestic, and He said: O Dawud, you are not fit to build a house for Me. He said: Why, O Lord? He said: Because of the blood that has been shed by your hands. He said: O Lord, was that not in accordance with Your will and Your love? He said: Yes, but they are My servants, and I have mercy upon them. This grieved him greatly, so Allah revealed to him: Do not grieve, for I shall accomplish its building at the hands of your son Sulayman. When Dawud died, Sulayman began its construction, and when it was completed, he offered sacrifices, slaughtered offerings, and gathered the Children of Israel. Allah revealed to him: I have seen your joy at the building of My house, so ask of Me and I shall give you. He said: I ask You for three qualities: a judgment that matches Your judgment, a dominion that would not be fitting for anyone after me, and that whoever comes to this house intending nothing but prayer in it should emerge from his sins as on the day his mother bore him." The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "As for two of them, he was given them, and I hope that he was given the third as well."

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Iyas ibn Salama ibn al-Akwa', from his father, said: You never heard the Messenger of Allah ﷺ make any supplication without opening it with "Glory be to Allah, my Lord, the Most High, the Exalted, the Bestower."

Abu Ubayd said: [chain] Salih ibn Mismar said: When the Prophet of Allah Dawud died, Allah revealed to his son Sulayman (peace be upon them both): Ask Me for your need. He said: I ask You to give me a heart that fears You as my father's heart feared You, and to make my heart love You as my father's heart loved You. Allah said: I sent to My servant and asked him his need, and his need was that I make his heart fear Me and that I make his heart love Me. I shall surely grant him a dominion that would not be fitting for anyone after him. Allah, exalted is He, said: {So We subjected to him the wind, blowing gently by his command wherever he directed} and what follows it. He said: So Allah gave him what He gave him, and in the Hereafter there will be no reckoning against him.

This is how Abu al-Qasim ibn Asakir related it in the biography of Sulayman (peace be upon him) in his history.

It has been narrated from some of the predecessors that he said: It has reached me about Dawud (peace be upon him) that he said: "My God, be to Sulayman as You were to me." So Allah revealed to him: Say to Sulayman: If he is to Me as you were to Me, I shall be to him as I was to you.

His saying: {So We subjected to him the wind, blowing gently by his command wherever he directed}. Al-Hasan al-Basri, may Allah have mercy on him, said: When Sulayman slaughtered the horses out of anger for the sake of Allah, mighty and majestic, Allah compensated him with something better than them, namely the wind, whose morning journey covered a month's distance and whose evening journey covered a month's distance.

His saying: {wherever he directed}, meaning wherever he wished among the lands.

His saying: {And the devils, every builder and diver}, meaning that among them were those employed in massive constructions such as sanctuaries, statues, basins like great cisterns, and fixed cooking pots, along with other arduous tasks that human beings are not capable of. And a group of them were divers in the seas, extracting from what is in them of pearls, gems, and precious things that are found nowhere else. {And others bound together in shackles}, meaning bound in chains and fetters, from among those who had rebelled, disobeyed, refused to work and declined, or had acted wrongfully and transgressed in their conduct.

His saying: {This is Our gift, so grant or withhold without account}, meaning: this complete dominion and perfect authority that We have given you, just as you asked Us, so give to whomever you wish and withhold from whomever you wish, there is no reckoning against you, meaning: whatever you do is permissible for you, judge as you wish, for it will be correct.

It is established in the two Sahihs that when the Messenger of Allah ﷺ was given the choice between being a servant-messenger, that is, one who does what he is commanded to do and is merely a distributor who divides among the people what Allah has commanded him to give, and being a king-prophet who gives to whomever he wishes and withholds from whomever he wishes without account and without blame, he chose the first station after consulting Jibril, who said to him: "Be humble." So he chose the first station because it is higher in rank with Allah and loftier in station in the return to Him, even though the second station, namely prophethood combined with kingship, is also great in this world and the next.

For this reason, when Allah, Blessed and Exalted, mentioned what He had given Sulayman (peace be upon him) in this world, He drew attention to the fact that he also has a great portion with Allah on the Day of Resurrection, saying: {And indeed, for him is nearness to Us and an excellent return}, meaning: in the Hereafter.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَقَدْ فَتَنَّا سُلَيْمَانَ﴾ أَيِ: اخْتَبَرْنَاهُ بِأَنْ سَلَبْنَاهُ الْمُلْكَ مَرَّةً، ﴿وَأَلْقَيْنَا عَلَى كُرْسِيِّهِ جَسَدًا﴾ قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَمُجَاهِدٌ وَسَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ وَالْحَسَنُ وَقَتَادَةُ وَغَيْرُهُمْ: يَعْنِي شَيْطَانًا. ﴿ثُمَّ أَنَابَ﴾ أَيْ: رَجَعَ إِلَى مُلْكِهِ وَسُلْطَانِهِ وَأُبَّهَتِهِ.

قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: وَكَانَ اسْمُ ذَلِكَ الشَّيْطَانِ صَخْرًا. قَالَهُ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَقَتَادَةُ. وَقِيلَ: آصِفُ. قَالَهُ مُجَاهِدٌ وَقِيلَ: آصِرُوا. قَالَهُ مُجَاهِدٌ أَيْضًا. وَقِيلَ: حبقيقُ. قَالَهُ السُّدِّيُّ. وَقَدْ ذَكَرُوا هَذِهِ الْقِصَّةَ مَبْسُوطَةً وَمُخْتَصَرَةً.

وَقَدْ قَالَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ أَبِي عَرُوبة عَنْ قَتَادَةَ: قَالَ أَمَرَ سُلَيْمَانُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ بِبِنَاءِ بَيْتِ الْمَقْدِسِ فَقِيلَ لَهُ: ابْنِهِ وَلَا يُسمَعُ فِيهِ صَوْتُ حَدِيدٍ. فَقَالَ: فَطَلَبَ ذَلِكَ فَلَمْ يَقْدِرْ عَلَيْهِ. فَقِيلَ لَهُ: إِنَّ شَيْطَانًا فِي الْبَحْرِ يُقَالُ لَهُ: "صَخْرٌ" شِبْهُ الْمَارِدِ. قَالَ: فَطَلَبَهُ وَكَانَتْ عَيْنٌ فِي الْبَحْرِ يَردهُا فِي كُلِّ سَبْعَةِ أَيَّامٍ مَرَّةً فَنُزِحَ مَاؤُهَا وَجُعِلَ فِيهَا خَمْرٌ، فَجَاءَ يَوْمَ ورْده فَإِذَا هُوَ بِالْخَمْرِ فَقَالَ: إِنَّكِ لَشَرَابٌ طَيِّبٌ إِلَّا أَنَّكِ تُصْبِينَ الْحَلِيمَ، وَتَزِيدِينَ الْجَاهِلَ جَهْلًا. ثُمَّ رَجَعَ حَتَّى عَطِشَ عَطَشًا شَدِيدًا ثُمَّ أَتَاهَا فَقَالَ: إِنَّكِ لَشَرَابٌ طَيِّبٌ إِلَّا أَنَّكِ تُصْبِينَ الْحَلِيمَ، وَتَزِيدِينَ الْجَاهِلَ جَهْلًا. ثُمَّ شَرِبَهَا حَتَّى غَلَبَتْ عَلَى عَقْلِهِ، قَالَ: فَأُرِيَ الْخَاتَمَ أَوْ خُتِمَ بِهِ بَيْنَ كَتِفَيْهِ فَذَلَّ. قَالَ: وَكَانَ مُلْكُهُ فِي خَاتَمِهِ فأتي به سليمان فقال: إنه قَدْ أُمِرْنَا بِبِنَاءِ هَذَا الْبَيْتِ وَقِيلَ لَنَا: لَا يُسْمَعَنَّ فِيهِ صَوْتُ حَدِيدٍ. قَالَ: فَأَتَى بِبَيْضِ الْهُدْهُدِ فَجَعَلَ عَلَيْهِ زُجَاجَةً فَجَاءَ الْهُدْهُدُ فَدَارَ حَوْلَهَا، فَجَعَلَ يَرَى بَيْضَهُ وَلَا يَقْدِرُ عَلَيْهِ فَذَهَبَ فَجَاءَ بِالْمَاسِ فَوَضَعَهُ عَلَيْهِ فَقَطَعَهَا بِهِ حَتَّى أَفْضَى إِلَى بَيْضِهِ. فَأَخَذَ الْمَاسَ فَجَعَلُوا يَقْطَعُونَ بِهِ الْحِجَارَةَ. وَكَانَ سُلَيْمَانُ [عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ] إِذَا أَرَادَ أَنْ يَدْخُلَ الْخَلَاءَ -أَوِ: الْحَمَّامَ-لَمْ يَدْخُلْ بِخَاتَمِهِ فَانْطَلَقَ يَوْمًا إِلَى الْحَمَّامِ وَذَلِكَ الشَّيْطَانُ صَخْرٌ مَعَهُ، وَذَلِكَ عِنْدَ مُقَارَفَةٍ قَارَفَ فِيهِ بَعْضَ نِسَائِهِ. قَالَ: فَدَخَلَ الْحَمَّامَ وَأَعْطَى الشَّيْطَانَ خَاتَمَهُ فَأَلْقَاهُ فِي الْبَحْرِ فَالْتَقَمَتْهُ سَمَكَةٌ، وَنُزِعَ مُلك سُلَيْمَانَ مِنْهُ وَأُلْقِيَ عَلَى الشَّيْطَانِ شَبَه سُلَيْمَانَ. قَالَ: فَجَاءَ فَقَعَدَ عَلَى كُرْسِيِّهِ وَسَرِيرِهِ وسُلِّط عَلَى مُلْكِ سُلَيْمَانَ كُلِّهِ غَيْرَ نِسَائِهِ. قَالَ: فَجَعَلَ يَقْضِي بَيْنَهُمْ، وَجَعَلُوا يُنْكِرُونَ مِنْهُ أَشْيَاءَ حَتَّى قَالُوا: لَقَدْ فُتِنَ نَبِيُّ اللَّهِ. وَكَانَ فِيهِمْ رَجُلٌ يُشَبِّهُونَهُ بِعُمَرَ بْنِ الْخَطَّابِ فِي الْقُوَّةِ فَقَالَ: وَاللَّهُ لَأُجَرِّبَنَّهُ. قَالَ: فَقَالَ: يَا نَبِيَّ اللَّهِ -وَهُوَ لَا يَرَى إِلَّا أَنَّهُ نَبِيُّ اللَّهِ-أَحَدُنَا تُصِيبُهُ الْجَنَابَةُ فِي اللَّيْلَةِ الْبَارِدَةِ فَيَدَعُ الْغُسْلَ عَمْدًا حَتَّى تَطْلُعَ الشَّمْسُ أَتُرَى عَلَيْهِ بَأْسًا؟ فَقَالَ: لَا. قَالَ: فَبَيْنَا هُوَ كَذَلِكَ أَرْبَعِينَ لَيْلَةً حَتَّى وَجَدَ نَبِيُّ اللَّهِ خَاتَمَهُ فِي بَطْنِ سَمَكَةٍ فَأَقْبَلَ فَجَعَلَ لَا يَسْتَقْبِلُهُ جِنِّيٌّ وَلَا طَيْرٌ إِلَّا سَجَدَ لَهُ حَتَّى انْتَهَى إِلَيْهِمْ، ﴿وَأَلْقَيْنَا عَلَى كُرْسِيِّهِ جَسَدًا﴾ قَالَ: هُوَ الشَّيْطَانُ صَخْرٌ 

وَقَالَ السُّدِّيُّ: ﴿وَلَقَدْ فَتَنَّا سُلَيْمَانَ﴾ أَيِ: ابْتَلَيْنَا سُلَيْمَانَ، ﴿وَأَلْقَيْنَا عَلَى كُرْسِيِّهِ جَسَدًا﴾ قَالَ: جَلَسَ الشَّيْطَانُ عَلَى كُرْسِيِّهِ أَرْبَعِينَ يَوْمًا. قَالَ: وَكَانَ لِسُلَيْمَانَ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ مِائَةُ امْرَأَةٍ وَكَانَتِ امْرَأَةٌ مِنْهُنَّ يُقَالُ لَهَا: "جَرَادَةُ"، وَهِيَ آثَرُ نِسَائِهِ وَآمَنُهُنَّ عِنْدَهُ وَكَانَ إِذَا أَجْنَبَ أَوْ أَتَى حَاجَةً نَزَعَ خَاتَمَهُ وَلَمْ يَأْتَمِنْ عَلَيْهِ أَحَدًا مِنَ النَّاسِ غَيْرَهَا فَأَعْطَاهَا يَوْمًا خَاتَمَهُ وَدَخَلَ الْخَلَاءَ فَخَرَجَ الشَّيْطَانُ فِي صُورَتِهِ فَقَالَ: هَاتِي الْخَاتَمَ. فَأَعْطَتْهُ فَجَاءَ حَتَّى جَلَسَ عَلَى مَجْلِسِ سُلَيْمَانَ وَخَرَجَ سُلَيْمَانُ بَعْدَ ذَلِكَ فَسَأَلَهَا أَنْ تُعْطِيَهِ خَاتَمَهُ، فَقَالَتْ: أَلَمْ تَأْخُذْهُ قَبْلُ؟ قَالَ: لَا. وَخَرَجَ مَكَانَهُ تَائِهًا. قَالَ: وَمَكَثَ الشَّيْطَانُ يُحْكُمُ بَيْنَ النَّاسِ أَرْبَعِينَ يَوْمًا، قَالَ: فَأَنْكَرَ النَّاسُ أَحْكَامَهُ فَاجْتَمَعَ قُرَّاءُ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ وَعُلَمَاؤُهُمْ فَجَاءُوا حَتَّى دَخَلُوا عَلَى نِسَائِهِ فَقَالُوا: إِنَّا قَدْ أَنْكَرْنَا هَذَا فَإِنْ كَانَ سُلَيْمَانَ فَقَدْ ذَهَبَ عَقْلُهُ وَأَنْكَرْنَا أَحْكَامَهُ. قَالَ: فَبَكَى النِّسَاءُ عِنْدَ ذَلِكَ قَالَ: فَأَقْبَلُوا يَمْشُونَ حَتَّى أَتَوْا فَأَحْدَقُوا بِهِ ثُمَّ نَشَرُوا التَّوْرَاةَ فَقَرَءُوا. قَالَ: فَطَارَ مِنْ بَيْنِ أَيْدِيهِمْ حَتَّى وَقَعَ عَلَى شُرْفَةٍ وَالْخَاتَمُ مَعَهُ. ثُمَّ طَارَ حَتَّى ذَهَبَ إِلَى الْبَحْرِ فَوَقَعَ الْخَاتَمُ مِنْهُ فِي الْبَحْرِ فَابْتَلَعَهُ حُوتٌ مِنْ حِيتَانِ الْبَحْرِ. قَالَ: وَأَقْبَلَ سُلَيْمَانُ فِي حَالِهِ الَّتِي كَانَ فِيهَا حَتَّى انْتَهَى إِلَى صَيَّادٍ مِنْ صَيَّادِي الْبَحْرِ وَهُوَ جَائِعٌ وَقَدِ اشْتَدَّ جُوعُهُ. فَاسْتَطْعَمَهُمْ مِنْ صَيْدِهِمْ وَقَالَ: إِنِّي أَنَا سُلَيْمَانُ. فَقَامَ إِلَيْهِ بَعْضُهُمْ فَضَرَبَهُ بِعَصًا فَشَجَّهُ فَجَعَلَ يَغْسِلُ دَمَهُ وَهُوَ عَلَى شَاطِئِ الْبَحْرِ فَلَامَ الصَّيَّادُونَ صَاحِبَهُمُ الَّذِي ضَرَبَهُ فَقَالُوا بِئْسَ مَا صَنَعْتَ حيث ضربته. قال: إنه زَعَمَ أَنَّهُ سُلَيْمَانُ. قَالَ: فَأَعْطَوْهُ سَمَكَتَيْنِ مِمَّا قَدْ مَذِرَ عِنْدَهُمْ فَلَمْ يَشْغَلْهُ مَا كَانَ بِهِ مِنَ الضَّرْبِ حَتَّى قَامَ إِلَى شَطِّ الْبَحْرِ فَشَقَّ بُطُونَهُمَا فَجَعَلَ يَغْسِلُ [دَمَهُ] فَوَجَدَ خَاتَمَهُ فِي بَطْنِ إِحْدَاهُمَا فَأَخَذَهُ فَلَبِسَهُ فَرَدَّ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ بَهَاءَهُ وَمُلْكَهُ، وَجَاءَتِ الطَّيْرُ حَتَّى حَامَتْ عَلَيْهِ فَعَرَفَ الْقَوْمُ أَنَّهُ سُلَيْمَانُ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ فَقَامَ الْقَوْمُ يَعْتَذِرُونَ مِمَّا صَنَعُوا [بِهِ] فَقَالَ: مَا أَحْمَدُكُمْ عَلَى عُذْرِكُمْ وَلَا أَلُومُكُمْ عَلَى مَا كَانَ مِنْكُمْ، كَانَ هَذَا الْأَمْرُ لَا بُدَّ مِنْهُ. قَالَ: فَجَاءَ حَتَّى أَتَى مُلْكَهُ وَأَرْسَلَ إِلَى الشَّيْطَانِ فَجِيءَ بِهِ فَأَمَرَ بِهِ فَجُعِلَ فِي صُنْدُوقٍ مِنْ حَدِيدٍ، ثُمَّ أَطْبَقَ عَلَيْهِ وَقَفَلَ عَلَيْهِ بِقُفْلٍ وَخَتَمَ عَلَيْهِ بِخَاتَمِهِ ثُمَّ أَمَرَ بِهِ فَأُلْقِي فِي الْبَحْرِ فَهُوَ فِيهِ حَتَّى تَقُومَ السَّاعَةُ. وَكَانَ اسْمُهُ حبقيقُ قَالَ: وَسَخَّرَ لَهُ الرِّيحَ وَلَمْ تَكُنْ سُخِّرَتْ لَهُ قَبْلَ ذَلِكَ وَهُوَ قَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَهَبْ لِي مُلْكًا لَا يَنْبَغِي لأحَدٍ مِنْ بَعْدِي إِنَّكَ أَنْتَ الْوَهَّابُ﴾ 

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي نَجِيحٍ، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ قَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَأَلْقَيْنَا عَلَى كُرْسِيِّهِ جَسَدًا﴾ قَالَ: شَيْطَانًا يُقَالُ لَهُ: آصِفُ. فَقَالَ لَهُ سُلَيْمَانُ: كَيْفَ تَفْتِنُونَ النَّاسَ؟ قَالَ: أَرِنِي خَاتَمَكَ أُخْبِرْكَ. فَلَمَّا أَعْطَاهُ إِيَّاهُ نَبَذَهُ آصِفُ فِي الْبَحْرِ فَسَاحَ سُلَيْمَانُ وَذَهَبَ مُلْكُهُ، وَقَعَدَ آصِفُ عَلَى كُرْسِيِّهِ وَمَنَعَهُ اللَّهُ نِسَاءَ سُلَيْمَانَ فَلَمْ يَقْرَبْهُنَّ -وَلَمْ يَقْرَبْنَهُ وَأَنْكَرْنَهُ. قَالَ: فَكَانَ سُلَيْمَانُ يَسْتَطْعِمُ فَيَقُولُ: أَتَعْرِفُونِي؟ أَطْعِمُونِي أَنَا سُلَيْمَانُ فَيُكَذِّبُونَهُ، حَتَّى أَعْطَتْهُ امْرَأَةٌ يَوْمًا حُوتًا فَجَعَلَ يُطَيِّبُ بَطْنَهُ، فَوَجَدَ خَاتَمَهُ فِي بَطْنِهِ فَرَجَعَ إِلَيْهِ مُلْكُهُ وَفَرَّ آصِفُ فَدَخَلَ الْبَحْرَ فَارًّا.

وَهَذِهِ كُلُّهَا مِنَ الْإِسْرَائِيلِيَّاتِ وَمِنْ أَنْكَرِهَا مَا قَالَهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ:

حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ الْحُسَيْنِ حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ الْعَلَاءِ وَعُثْمَانُ بْنُ أَبِي شَيْبَةَ وَعَلِيُّ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ قَالُوا: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو مُعَاوِيَةَ أَخْبَرَنَا الْأَعْمَشِ عَنِ الْمِنْهَالِ بْنِ عَمْرٍو عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ [رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا] ﴿وَأَلْقَيْنَا عَلَى كُرْسِيِّهِ جَسَدًا ثُمَّ أَنَابَ﴾ قَالَ: أَرَادَ سُلَيْمَانُ أَنْ يَدْخُلَ الْخَلَاءَ فَأَعْطَى الْجَرَادَةَ خَاتَمَهُ -وَكَانَتِ الْجَرَادَةُ امْرَأَتَهُ وَكَانَتْ أَحَبَّ نِسَائِهِ إِلَيْهِ-فَجَاءَ الشَّيْطَانُ فِي صُورَةِ سُلَيْمَانَ فَقَالَ لَهَا: هَاتِي خَاتَمِي. فَأَعْطَتْهُ إِيَّاهُ. فَلَمَّا لَبِسَهُ دَانَتْ لَهُ الْإِنْسُ وَالْجِنُّ وَالشَّيَاطِينُ فَلَمَّا خَرَجَ سُلَيْمَانُ مِنَ الْخَلَاءِ قَالَ لَهَا: هَاتِي خَاتَمِي. قَالَتْ: قَدْ أَعْطَيْتُهُ سُلَيْمَانَ. قَالَ: أَنَا سُلَيْمَانُ. قَالَتْ: كَذَبْتَ لَسْتَ سُلَيْمَانَ فَجَعَلَ لَا يَأْتِي أَحَدًا يَقُولُ لَهُ: "أَنَا سُلَيْمَانُ"، إِلَّا كَذَّبَهُ حَتَّى جَعَلَ الصِّبْيَانُ يَرْمُونَهُ بِالْحِجَارَةِ. فَلَمَّا رَأَى ذَلِكَ عَرَف أَنَّهُ مِنْ أَمْرِ اللَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ. قَالَ: وَقَامَ الشَّيْطَانُ يَحْكُمُ بَيْنَ النَّاسِ فَلَمَّا أَرَادَ اللَّهُ أَنْ يَرُدَّ عَلَى سُلَيْمَانَ سُلْطَانَهُ أَلْقَى فِي قُلُوبِ النَّاسِ إِنْكَارَ ذَلِكَ الشَّيْطَانِ. قَالَ: فَأَرْسَلُوا إِلَى نِسَاءِ سُلَيْمَانَ فَقَالُوا لَهُنَّ: أَتُنْكِرْنَ مِنْ سُلَيْمَانَ شَيْئًا؟ قُلْنَ: نَعَمْ إِنَّهُ يَأْتِينَا وَنَحْنُ حُيَّضٌ وَمَا كَانَ يَأْتِينَا قَبْلَ ذَلِكَ. فَلَمَّا رَأَى الشَّيْطَانُ أَنَّهُ قَدْ فَطِنَ لَهُ ظَنَّ أَنَّ أَمْرَهُ قَدِ انْقَطَعَ فَكَتَبُوا كُتُبًا فِيهَا سِحْرٌ وَكُفْرٌ، فَدَفَنُوهَا تَحْتَ كُرْسِيِّ سُلَيْمَانَ ثُمَّ أَثَارُوهَا وقرءوها على الناس. وقالوا: بِهَذَا كَانَ يَظْهَرُ سُلَيْمَانُ عَلَى النَّاسِ [وَيَغْلِبُهُمْ] فَأَكْفَرَ النَّاسُ سُلَيْمَانَ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ فَلَمْ يَزَالُوا يُكَفِّرُونَهُ وَبَعَثَ ذَلِكَ الشيطانُ بِالْخَاتَمِ فَطَرَحَهُ فِي الْبَحْرِ فَتَلَقَّتْهُ سَمَكَةٌ فَأَخَذَتْهُ. وَكَانَ سُلَيْمَانُ يَحْمِلُ عَلَى شَطِّ الْبَحْرِ بِالْأَجْرِ فَجَاءَ رَجُلٌ فَاشْتَرَى سَمَكًا فِيهِ تِلْكَ السَّمَكَةُ الَّتِي فِي بَطْنِهَا الْخَاتَمُ فَدَعَا سُلَيْمَانُ فَقَالَ: تَحْمِلُ لِي هَذَا السَّمَكَ؟ فَقَالَ: نَعَمْ. قَالَ: بِكَمْ؟ قَالَ بِسَمَكَةٍ مِنْ هَذَا السَّمَكِ. قَالَ: فَحَمَلَ سُلَيْمَانُ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ السَّمَكَ ثُمَّ انْطَلَقَ بِهِ إِلَى مَنْزِلِهِ فَلَمَّا انْتَهَى الرَّجُلُ إِلَى بَابِهِ أَعْطَاهُ تِلْكَ السَّمَكَةَ الَّتِي فِي بَطْنِهَا الْخَاتَمُ فَأَخَذَهَا سُلَيْمَانُ فَشَقَّ بَطْنَهَا، فَإِذَا الْخَاتَمُ فِي جَوْفِهَا فَأَخَذَهُ فَلَبِسَهُ. قَالَ: فَلَمَّا لَبِسَهُ دَانَتْ لَهُ الْجِنُّ وَالْإِنْسُ وَالشَّيَاطِينُ وَعَادَ إِلَى حَالِهِ وَهَرب الشَّيْطَانُ حَتَّى دَخَلَ جَزِيرَةً مِنْ جَزَائِرِ الْبَحْرِ فَأَرْسَلَ سُلَيْمَانُ فِي طَلَبِهِ وَكَانَ شَيْطَانًا مَرِيدًا فَجَعَلُوا يَطْلُبُونَهُ وَلَا يَقْدِرُونَ عَلَيْهِ حَتَّى وَجَدُوهُ يَوْمًا نَائِمًا فَجَاءُوا فَبَنَوْا عَلَيْهِ بُنْيَانًا مِنْ رَصَاصٍ فَاسْتَيْقَظَ فَوَثَبَ فَجَعَلَ لَا يَثِبُ فِي مَكَانٍ من البيت إلا أنماط معه من الرَّصَاصُ قَالَ: فَأَخَذُوهُ فَأَوْثَقُوهُ وَجَاءُوا بِهِ إِلَى سُلَيْمَانَ، فَأَمَرَ بِهِ فَنُقِرَ لَهُ تَخْتٌ مِنْ رُخَامٍ ثُمَّ أُدْخِلَ فِي جَوْفِهِ ثُمَّ سُدَّ بِالنُّحَاسِ ثُمَّ أُمِرَ بِهِ فَطُرِحَ فِي الْبَحْرِ فَذَلِكَ قَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلَقَدْ فَتَنَّا سُلَيْمَانَ وَأَلْقَيْنَا عَلَى كُرْسِيِّهِ جَسَدًا ثُمَّ أَنَابَ﴾ قَالَ: يَعْنِي الشَّيْطَانَ الَّذِي كَانَ سُلِّطَ عَلَيْهِ.

إِسْنَادُهُ إِلَى ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَوِيٌّ وَلَكِنَّ الظَّاهِرَ أَنَّهُ إِنَّمَا تَلَقَّاهُ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ -إِنْ صَحَّ عَنْهُ-مِنْ أَهْلِ الْكِتَابِ، وَفِيهِمْ طَائِفَةٌ لَا يَعْتَقِدُونَ نُبُوَّةَ سُلَيْمَانَ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ فَالظَّاهِرُ أَنَّهُمْ يَكْذِبُونَ عَلَيْهِ وَلِهَذَا كَانَ فِي السِّيَاقِ مُنْكَرَاتٌ مِنْ أَشَدِّهَا ذِكْرُ النِّسَاءِ فَإِنَّ الْمَشْهُورَ أَنَّ ذَلِكَ الْجِنِّيَّ لَمْ يُسَلَّطْ عَلَى نِسَاءِ سُلَيْمَانَ بَلْ عَصَمَهُنَّ اللَّهُ مِنْهُ تَشْرِيفًا وَتَكْرِيمًا لِنَبِيِّهِ ﷺ، وَقَدْ رُوِيَتْ هَذِهِ الْقِصَّةُ مُطَوَّلَةً عَنْ جَمَاعَةٍ مِنَ السَّلَفِ، كَسَعِيدِ بْنِ الْمُسَيَّبِ وَزَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ وَجَمَاعَةٍ آخَرِينَ وَكُلُّهَا متُلقًّاة مِنْ قَصَصِ أَهْلِ الْكِتَابِ وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ بِالصَّوَابِ.

وَقَالَ يَحْيَى بْنُ أَبِي عَمْرٍو السَّيْبَانِيُّ: وَجَدَ سُلَيْمَانُ خَاتَمَهُ فِي عَسْقَلَانَ، فَمَشَى فِي خِرْقَةٍ إِلَى بَيْتِ الْمَقْدِسِ تَوَاضُعًا لِلَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، رَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ.

وَقَدْ رَوَى ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ عَنْ كَعْبِ الْأَحْبَارِ فِي صِفَةِ كُرْسِيِّ سُلَيْمَانَ عَلَيْهِ الصَّلَاةُ وَالسَّلَامُ خَبَرًا عَجِيبًا فَقَالَ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو صَالِحٍ كَاتِبُ اللَّيْثِ أَخْبَرَنِي أَبُو إِسْحَاقَ الْمِصْرِيُّ عَنْ كَعْبِ الْأَحْبَارِ؛ أَنَّهُ لَمَّا فَرَغَ مِنْ حَدِيثِ "إِرَمَ ذَاتِ الْعِمَادِ" قَالَ لَهُ مُعَاوِيَةُ: يَا أَبَا إِسْحَاقَ أَخْبِرْنِي عَنْ كُرْسِيِّ سُلَيْمَانَ بْنِ دَاوُدَ وَمَا كَانَ عَلَيْهِ؛ وَمِنْ أَيِّ شَيْءٍ هُوَ؟ فَقَالَ: كَانَ كُرْسِيُّ سُلَيْمَانَ مِنْ أَنْيَابِ الْفِيَلَةِ مُفَصّصاً بِالدُّرِّ وَالْيَاقُوتِ وَالزَّبَرْجَدِ وَاللُّؤْلُؤِ. وَقَدْ جُعل لَهُ دَرَجَةً مِنْهَا مُفَصّصة بِالدُّرِّ وَالْيَاقُوتِ وَالزَّبَرْجَدِ ثُمَّ أَمَرَ بِالْكُرْسِيِّ فحُفّ مِنْ جَانِبَيْهِ بِالنَّخْلِ، نَخْلٌ مِنْ ذَهَبٍ شَمَارِيخُهَا مِنْ يَاقُوتٍ وَزَبَرْجَدٍ وَلُؤْلُؤٍ. وَجُعِلَ عَلَى رُءُوسِ النَّخْلِ الَّتِي عَنْ يَمِينِ الْكُرْسِيِّ طَوَاوِيسُ مَنْ ذَهَبٍ، ثُمَّ جُعِلَ عَلَى رُءُوسِ النَّخْلِ الَّتِي عَلَى يَسَارِ الْكُرْسِيِّ نُسُورٌ مَنْ ذَهَبٍ مُقَابَلَةَ الطَّوَاوِيسِ، وَجُعِلَ على يمين الدرجة الأولى شَجَرَتَا صَنَوْبَرٍ مَنْ ذَهَبٍ، وَعَنْ يَسَارِهَا أَسَدَانِ مَنْ ذَهَبٍ وَعَلَى رُءُوسِ الْأَسَدَيْنِ عَمُودَانِ مِنْ زَبَرْجَدٍ وَجُعِلَ مِنْ جَانِبَيِ الْكُرْسِيِّ شَجَرَتَا كَرْمٍ مَنْ ذَهَبٍ قَدْ أَظَلَّتَا الْكُرْسِيَّ وَجُعِلَ عَنَاقِيدُهُمَا دُرًّا وَيَاقُوتًا أَحْمَرَ. ثُمَّ جُعل فَوْقَ دَرَج الْكُرْسِيِّ أسَدَان عَظِيمَانِ مِنْ ذَهَبٍ مُجَوَّفَانِ مَحْشُوَّانِ مِسْكًا وَعَنْبَرًا. فَإِذَا أَرَادَ سُلَيْمَانُ أَنْ يَصْعَدَ عَلَى كُرْسِيِّهِ اسْتَدَارَ الْأَسَدَانِ سَاعَةً ثُمَّ يَقَعَانِ فَيَنْضَحَانِ مَا فِي أَجْوَافِهِمَا مِنَ الْمِسْكِ وَالْعَنْبَرِ حَوْلَ كُرْسِيِّ سُلَيْمَانَ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، ثُمَّ يُوضَعُ مِنْبَرَانِ مِنْ ذَهَبٍ وَاحِدٌ لِخَلِيفَتِهِ وَالْآخِرُ لِرَئِيسِ أَحْبَارِ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ ذَلِكَ الزَّمَانِ. ثُمَّ يُوضَعُ أَمَامَ كُرْسِيِّهِ سَبْعُونَ مِنْبَرًا مِنْ ذَهَبٍ يَقْعُدُ عَلَيْهَا سَبْعُونَ قَاضِيًا مِنْ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ وَعُلَمَائِهِمْ وَأَهْلِ الشَّرَفِ مِنْهُمْ وَالطَوْلِ وَمِنْ خَلْفِ تِلْكَ الْمَنَابِرِ كُلِّهَا خَمْسَةٌ وَثَلَاثُونَ مِنْبَرًا مِنْ ذَهَبٍ لَيْسَ عَلَيْهَا أَحَدٌ، فَإِذَا أَرَادَ أَنْ يَصْعَدَ عَلَى كُرْسِيِّهِ وَضَعَ قَدَمَيْهِ عَلَى الدَّرَجَةِ السُّفْلَى فَاسْتَدَارَ الْكُرْسِيُّ كُلُّهُ بِمَا فِيهِ وَمَا عَلَيْهِ، وَيَبْسُطُ الْأَسَدُ يَدَهُ الْيُمْنَى وَيَنْشُرُ النَّسْرُ جَنَاحَهُ الْأَيْسَرَ ثُمَّ يَصْعَدُ [سُلَيْمَانُ] عَلَى الدَّرَجَةِ الثَّانِيَةِ فَيَبْسُطُ الْأَسَدُ يَدَهُ الْيُسْرَى وَيَنْشُرُ النَّسْرُ جَنَاحَهُ الْأَيْمَنَ فَإِذَا اسْتَوَى سُلَيْمَانُ عَلَى الدَّرَجَةِ الثَّالِثَةِ وَقَعَدَ عَلَى الْكُرْسِيِّ أَخَذَ نَسْرٌ مِنْ تِلْكَ النُّسُورِ عَظِيمٌ تَاجَ سُلَيْمَانَ فَوَضَعَهُ عَلَى رَأْسِهِ فَإِذَا وَضَعَهُ عَلَى رَأْسِهِ اسْتَدَارَ الْكُرْسِيُّ بِمَا فِيهِ كَمَا تَدُورُ الرَّحَى الْمُسْرِعَةُ. فَقَالَ مُعَاوِيَةُ رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ: وَمَا الَّذِي يُدِيرُهُ يَا أَبَا إِسْحَاقَ؟ قَالَ: تِنِّينٌ مِنْ ذَهَبِ ذَلِكَ الْكُرْسِيِّ عَلَيْهِ وَهُوَ عَظِيمٌ مِمَّا عَمِلَهُ صَخْرٌ الْجِنِّيُّ فَإِذَا أَحَسَّتْ بِدَوَرَانِهِ تِلْكَ النُّسُورُ والأسْدُ وَالطَّوَاوِيسُ الَّتِي فِي أَسْفَلِ الْكُرْسِيِّ دُرْنَ إِلَى أَعْلَاهُ فَإِذَا وَقَفَ وَقَفْنَ كُلُّهُنَّ مُنَكِّسَاتٍ رُءُوسَهُنَّ عَلَى رَأْسِ سُلَيْمَانَ [ابْنِ دَاوُدَ] عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ وَهُوَ جَالِسٌ ثُمَّ يَنْضَحْنَ جَمِيعًا مَا فِي أَجْوَافِهِنَّ مِنَ الْمِسْكِ وَالْعَنْبَرِ عَلَى رَأْسِ سُلَيْمَانَ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ. ثُمَّ تَتَنَاوَلُ حَمَامَةٌ مَنْ ذَهَبٍ وَاقِفَةٌ عَلَى عَمُودٍ مِنْ جَوْهَرٍ التوراةَ فَتَجْعَلُهَا فِي يَدِهِ فَيَقْرَؤُهَا سُلَيْمَانُ عَلَى النَّاسِ.

وَذَكَرَ تَمَامَ الْخَبَرِ وَهُوَ غَرِيبٌ جِدًّا.

﴿قَالَ رَبِّ اغْفِرْ لِي وَهَبْ لِي مُلْكًا لَا يَنْبَغِي لأحَدٍ مِنْ بَعْدِي إِنَّكَ أَنْتَ الْوَهَّابُ﴾ قَالَ بَعْضُهُمْ: مَعْنَاهُ: لَا يَنْبَغِي لِأَحَدٍ مِنْ بَعْدِي أَيْ: لَا يَصْلُحُ لِأَحَدٍ أَنْ يَسْلُبَنِيهِ كَمَا كَانَ مِنْ قَضِيَّةِ الْجَسَدِ الَّذِي أُلْقِيَ عَلَى كُرْسِيِّهِ لَا أَنَّهُ يَحْجُرُ عَلَى مَنْ بَعْدَهُ مِنَ النَّاسِ. وَالصَّحِيحُ أَنَّهُ سَأَلَ مِنَ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى مُلْكًا لَا يَكُونُ لِأَحَدٍ مِنْ بَعْدِهِ مِنَ الْبَشَرِ مِثْلُهُ، وَهَذَا هُوَ ظَاهِرُ السِّيَاقِ مِنَ الْآيَةِ وَبِهِ وَرَدَتِ الْأَحَادِيثُ الصَّحِيحَةُ مِنْ طُرُقٍ عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ.

قَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ عِنْدَ تَفْسِيرِ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: حَدَّثَنَا إِسْحَاقُ بْنُ إِبْرَاهِيمَ أَخْبَرَنَا رَوْحٌ وَمُحَمَّدُ بْنُ جَعْفَرٍ عَنْ شُعْبَةَ عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ زِيَادٍ عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَ: "إِنَّ عِفْرِيتًا مِنَ الْجِنِّ تَفَلَّت عَلَيَّ الْبَارِحَةَ -أَوْ كَلِمَةً نَحْوَهَا-لِيَقْطَعَ عَلَيَّ الصَّلَاةَ فَأَمْكَنَنِي اللَّهُ مِنْهُ وَأَرَدْتُ أَنْ أَرْبِطَهُ إِلَى سَارِيَةٍ مِنْ سَوَارِي الْمَسْجِدِ حَتَّى تُصبحوا وَتَنْظُرُوا إِلَيْهِ كُلُّكُمْ فَذَكَرْتُ قَوْلَ أَخِي سُلَيْمَانَ: ﴿رَبِّ اغْفِرْ لِي وَهَبْ لِي مُلْكًا لَا يَنْبَغِي لأحَدٍ مِنْ بَعْدِي﴾

قَالَ رَوْحٌ: فَرَدَّهُ خَاسِئًا 

وَكَذَا رَوَاهُ مُسْلِمٌ وَالنَّسَائِيُّ مِنْ حَدِيثِ شُعْبَةَ بِهِ 

وَقَالَ مُسْلِمٌ فِي صَحِيحِهِ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ سَلَمَةَ المُرَادي حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ وَهْبٍ عَنْ مُعَاوِيَةَ بْنِ صَالِحٍ حَدَّثَنِي رَبِيعَةَ بْنِ يَزيد عَنْ أَبِي إِدْرِيسَ الْخَوْلَانِيِّ عَنْ أَبِي الدَّرْدَاءِ قَالَ: قَامَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ يُصَلِّي فَسَمِعْنَاهُ يَقُولُ: "أَعُوذُ بِاللَّهِ مِنْكَ". ثُمَّ قَالَ: "أَلْعَنُكَ بِلَعْنَةِ اللَّهِ" -ثَلَاثًا-وَبَسَطَ يَدَه كَأَنَّهُ يَتَنَاوَلُ شَيْئًا فَلَمَّا فَرَغَ مِنَ الصَّلَاةِ قُلْنَا: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، قَدْ سَمِعْنَاكَ تَقُولُ فِي الصَّلَاةِ شَيْئًا لَمْ نَسْمَعْكَ تَقُولُهُ قَبْلَ ذَلِكَ وَرَأَيْنَاكَ بَسَطَتْ يَدَكَ؟ قَالَ: "إِنَّ عَدُوَّ اللَّهِ إِبْلِيسَ جَاءَ بِشِهَابٍ مِنْ نَارٍ لِيَجْعَلَهُ فِي وَجْهِي فَقُلْتُ: أَعُوذُ بِاللَّهِ مِنْكَ -ثَلَاثَ مَرَّاتٍ-ثُمَّ قُلْتُ: أَلْعَنُكَ بِلَعْنَةِ اللَّهِ التَّامَّةِ. فَلَمْ يَسْتَأْخِرْ ثَلَاثَ مَرَّاتٍ ثُمَّ أَرَدْتُ أخْذَه وَاللَّهِ لَوْلَا دَعْوَةُ أَخِينَا سُلَيْمَانَ لَأَصْبَحَ مُوثَقًا يَلْعَبُ بِهِ صِبْيَانُ أَهْلِ الْمَدِينَةِ" 

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو أَحْمَدَ حَدَّثَنَا مَيْسَرَةُ بْنُ مَعْبَدٍ حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو عُبَيْدٍ حَاجِبُ سُلَيْمَانَ قَالَ: رَأَيْتُ عَطَاءَ بْنَ يَزِيدَ اللَّيْثِيَّ قَائِمًا يُصَلِّي، فَذَهَبْتُ أَمُرُّ بَيْنَ يَدَيْهِ فَرَدَّنِي ثُمَّ قَالَ حَدَّثَنِي أَبُو سَعِيدٍ الْخُدْرِيِّ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَامَ يُصَلِّي صَلَاةَ الصُّبْحِ وَهُوَ خَلْفُهُ فَقَرَأَ فَالْتَبَسَتْ عَلَيْهِ الْقِرَاءَةُ فَلَمَّا فَرَغَ مِنْ صِلَاتِهِ قَالَ: "لَوْ رَأَيْتُمُونِي وَإِبْلِيسَ فَأَهْوَيْتُ بِيَدِي فَمَا زِلْتُ أَخْنُقُهُ حَتَّى وَجَدْتُ بَرْدَ لُعَابِهِ بَيْنَ أُصْبُعَيَّ هَاتَيْنِ -الْإِبْهَامِ وَالَّتِي تَلِيهَا-وَلَوْلَا دَعْوَةُ أَخِي سُلَيْمَانَ لَأَصْبَحَ مَرْبُوطًا بِسَارِيَةٍ مِنْ سَوَارِي الْمَسْجِدِ، يَتَلَاعَبُ بِهِ صِبْيَانُ الْمَدِينَةِ فَمَنِ اسْتَطَاعَ مِنْكُمْ أَلَّا يَحُولَ بَيْنَهُ وَبَيْنَ الْقِبْلَةِ أَحَدٌ فَلْيَفْعَلْ".

وَقَدْ رَوَى أَبُو دَاوُدَ مِنْهُ: "مَنِ اسْتَطَاعَ مِنْكُمْ أَلَّا يَحُولَ بَيْنَهُ وَبَيْنَ الْقِبْلَةِ أَحَدٌ فَلْيَفْعَلْ" عَنْ أَحْمَدَ بْنِ أَبِي سُرَيج عَنْ أَبِي أَحْمَدَ الزُّبَيْرِيِّ بِهِ 

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا مُعَاوِيَةُ بْنُ عَمْرٍو حَدَّثَنَا إِبْرَاهِيمُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ الْفَزَارِيُّ حَدَّثَنَا الْأَوْزَاعِيُّ، حَدَّثَنِي رَبِيعَةُ بْنُ يَزِيدَ عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ الدَّيْلَمِيِّ قَالَ: دَخَلْتُ عَلَى عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمْرٍو، وَهُوَ فِي حَائِطٍ لَهُ بِالطَّائِفِ يُقَالُ لَهُ: "الْوَهْطُ"، وَهُوَ مُخَاصر فَتًى مِنْ قُرَيْشٍ يُزَنّ بشُرْب الْخَمْرِ، فَقُلْتُ: بَلَغَنِي عَنْكَ حَدِيثٌ أَنَّهُ "مِنْ شَرِبِ شَرْبَةَ خَمْر لَمْ يَقْبَلِ اللَّهُ -عَزَّ وَجَلَّ-لَهُ تَوبَةً أَرْبَعِينَ صَبَاحًا، وَإِنَّ الشَّقِيَّ مَنْ شَقِيَ فِي بَطْنِ أُمِّهِ وَإِنَّهُ مَنْ أَتَى بَيْتَ الْمَقْدِسِ لا يَنْهَزه إلا الصلاة فيه، خرج مِنْ خَطِيئَتِهِ مِثْلَ يَوْمِ وَلَدَتْهُ أُمُّهُ، فَلَمَّا سَمِعَ الْفَتَى ذَكْرَ الْخَمْرِ اجْتَذَبَ يَدَهُ مِنْ يَدِهِ ثُمَّ انْطَلَقَ. فَقَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ عَمْرٍو إِنِّي لَا أُحِلُّ لِأَحَدٍ أَنْ يَقُولَ عَلَيّ مَا لَمْ أَقُلْ سَمِعْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ: "مَنْ شَرِبَ مِنَ الْخَمْرِ شَرْبَةً لَمْ تُقْبَلْ لَهُ صَلَاةٌ أَرْبَعِينَ صَبَاحًا فَإِنْ تَابَ تَابَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ فَإِنْ عَادَ لَمْ تُقْبَلْ لَهُ صَلَاةٌ أَرْبَعِينَ صَبَاحًا فَإِنْ تَابَ تَابَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ. فَإِنْ عَادَ -قَالَ فَلَا أَدْرِي فِي الثَّالِثَةِ أَوِ الرَّابِعَةِ-فَإِنْ عَادَ كَانَ حَقًّا عَلَى اللَّهِ أَنْ يَسْقِيَهُ مِنْ رَدْغَة الْخَبَالِ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ" قَالَ: وَسَمِعَتْ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ: "إِنَّ اللَّهَ خَلَقَ خَلْقَهُ فِي ظُلْمَةٍ ثُمَّ أَلْقَى عَلَيْهِمْ مِنْ نُورِهِ فَمَنْ أَصَابَهُ مِنْ نُورِهِ يَوْمَئِذٍ اهْتَدَى وَمَنْ أَخْطَأَهُ ضَلَّ فَلِذَلِكَ أَقُولُ جَفَّ الْقَلَمُ عَلَى عِلْمِ اللَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ" وَسَمِعَتْ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ: "إِنَّ سُلَيْمَانَ سَأَلَ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى ثَلَاثًا فَأَعْطَاهُ اثْنَتَيْنِ وَنَحْنُ نَرْجُو أَنْ تَكُونَ لَنَا الثَّالِثَةُ: سَأَلَهُ حُكْمًا يُصَادِفُ حُكْمَهُ فَأَعْطَاهُ إِيَّاهُ وَسَأَلَهُ مُلْكًا لَا يَنْبَغِي لِأَحَدٍ مِنْ بَعْدِهِ فَأَعْطَاهُ إِيَّاهُ وَسَأَلَهُ أَيُّمَا رَجُلٍ خَرَجَ مَنْ بَيْتِهِ لَا يُرِيدُ إِلَّا الصَّلَاةَ فِي هَذَا الْمَسْجِدِ خَرَجَ مِنْ خَطِيئَتِهِ كَيَوْمِ وَلَدَتْهُ أُمُّهُ فَنَحْنُ نَرْجُو أَنْ يَكُونَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى قَدْ أَعْطَانَا إِيَّاهَا" 

وَقَدْ رَوَى هَذَا الْفَصْلَ الْأَخِيرَ مِنْ هَذَا الْحَدِيثِ النَّسَائِيُّ وَابْنُ مَاجَهْ مِنْ طُرُقٍ عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ فَيْرُوزَ الدَّيْلِمِيِّ عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمْرٍو قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنَّ سُلَيْمَانَ لَمَّا بَنَى بَيْتَ الْمَقْدِسِ سَأَلَ رَبَّهُ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ خِلَالًا ثَلَاثًا ... " وَذَكَرَهُ 

وَقَدْ رُوِيَ مِنْ حَدِيثِ رَافِعِ بْنِ عُمَيْرٍ رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، بِإِسْنَادٍ وَسِيَاقٍ غَرِيبَيْنِ فَقَالَ الطَّبَرَانِيُّ:

حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ الْحَسَنِ بْنِ قُتَيْبة الْعَسْقَلَانِيُّ حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ أَيُّوبَ بْنِ سُوَيْد حَدَّثَنِي أَبِي حَدَّثَنَا إِبْرَاهِيمُ بْنُ أَبِي عَبْلَة عَنْ أَبِي الزَّاهِرِيَّةِ عَنْ رَافِعِ بْنِ عُمَيْرٍ قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ: "قَالَ اللَّهُ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ لِدَاوُدَ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ: ابْنِ لِي بَيْتًا فِي الْأَرْضِ. فَبَنَى دَاوُدُ بَيْتًا لِنَفْسِهِ قَبْلَ الْبَيْتِ الَّذِي أُمِرَ بِهِ فَأَوْحَى اللَّهُ إِلَيْهِ: يَا دَاوُدُ نَصَبْتَ بَيْتَكَ قَبْلَ بَيْتِي؟ قَالَ: يَا رَبِّ هَكَذَا قَضَيْتَ مَنْ مَلَكَ اسْتَأْثَرَ ثُمَّ أَخَذَ فِي بِنَاءِ الْمَسْجِدِ فَلَمَّا تَمَّ السُّورَ سَقَطَ ثَلَاثًا فَشَكَا ذَلِكَ إِلَى اللَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ فَقَالَ: يَا دَاوُدُ إِنَّكَ لَا تَصْلُحُ أَنْ تَبْنِيَ لِي بَيْتًا قَالَ: وَلِمَ يَا رَبِّ؟ قَالَ: لِمَا جَرَى عَلَى يَدَيْكَ مِنَ الدِّمَاءِ. قَالَ: يَا رَبِّ أَوْ مَا كَانَ ذَلِكَ فِي هَوَاكَ وَمَحَبَّتِكَ؟ قَالَ: بَلَى وَلَكِنَّهُمْ عِبَادِي وَأَنَا أَرْحَمُهُمْ فَشَقَّ ذَلِكَ عَلَيْهِ فَأَوْحَى اللَّهُ إِلَيْهِ: لَا تَحْزَنْ فَإِنِّي سَأَقْضِي بِنَاءَهُ عَلَى يَدَيِ ابْنِكَ سُلَيْمَانَ. فَلَمَّا مَاتَ دَاوُدُ أَخْذَ سُلَيْمَانُ فِي بِنَائِهِ فَلَمَّا تَمَّ قَرَّبَ الْقَرَابِينَ وَذَبَحَ الذَّبَائِحَ وَجَمَعَ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ فَأَوْحَى اللَّهُ إِلَيْهِ: قَدْ أَرَى سرورَك بِبُنْيَانِ بَيْتِي فَسَلْنِي أُعْطِكَ. قَالَ: أَسْأَلُكَ ثَلَاثَ خِصَالٍ حُكْمًا يُصَادِفُ حُكْمَكَ وَمُلْكًا لَا يَنْبَغِي لِأَحَدٍ مِنْ بَعْدِي وَمَنْ أَتَى هَذَا الْبَيْتَ لَا يُرِيدُ إلا الصلاة فيه خَرَجَ مِنْ ذُنُوبِهِ كَيَوْمِ وَلَدَتْهُ أُمُّهُ". قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "أما ثِنْتَانِ فَقَدْ أُعْطِيَهُمَا وَأَنَا أَرْجُو أَنْ يَكُونَ قَدْ أُعْطِيَ الثَّالِثَةَ" 

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الصَّمَدِ حَدَّثَنَا عُمَر بْنُ رَاشِدٍ الْيَمَامِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا إِيَاسُ بْنُ سَلَمَةَ بْنِ الْأَكْوَعِ عَنْ أَبِيهِ قَالَ: مَا سَمِعْتَ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ دَعَا دُعَاءً إِلَّا اسْتَفْتَحَهُ بِـ "سُبْحَانَ اللَّهِ رَبِّي الْأَعْلَى الْعَلِيِّ الْوَهَّابِ" 

وَقَدْ قَالَ أَبُو عَبِيدٍ: حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ ثَابِتٍ عَنْ جَعْفَرِ بْنِ بَرْقان عَنْ صَالِحِ بْنِ مِسْمَارٍ قَالَ: لَمَّا مَاتَ نَبِيُّ اللَّهِ دَاوُدُ أَوْحَى اللَّهُ إِلَى ابْنِهِ سُلَيْمَانُ عَلَيْهِمَا السَّلَامُ: أَنْ سَلْنِي حَاجَتَكَ. قَالَ: أَسْأَلُكَ أَنْ تَجْعَلَ لِي قَلْبًا يَخْشَاكَ كَمَا كَانَ قَلْبُ أَبِي وَأَنْ تَجْعَلَ قَلْبِي يُحِبُّكَ كَمَا كَانَ قَلْبُ أَبِي. فَقَالَ اللَّهُ: أَرْسَلْتُ إِلَى عَبْدِي وَسَأَلَتْهُ حَاجَتَهُ فَكَانَتْ [حَاجَتُهُ] أَنْ أَجْعَلَ قَلْبَهُ يَخْشَانِي وَأَنْ أَجْعَلَ قَلْبَهُ يُحِبُّنِي لأهَبَنّ لَهُ مُلْكًا لَا يَنْبَغِي لِأَحَدٍ مِنْ بَعْدِهِ. قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَسَخَّرْنَا لَهُ الرِّيحَ تَجْرِي بِأَمْرِهِ رُخَاءً حَيْثُ أَصَابَ﴾ وَالَّتِي بَعْدَهَا، قَالَ: فَأَعْطَاهُ [اللَّهُ] مَا أَعْطَاهُ وَفِي الْآخِرَةِ لَا حِسَابَ عَلَيْهِ.

هَكَذَا أَوْرَدَهُ أَبُو الْقَاسِمِ بْنُ عَسَاكِرَ فِي تَرْجَمَةِ سُلَيْمَانَ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ فِي تَارِيخِهِ 

وَرُوِيَ عَنْ بَعْضِ السَّلَفِ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: بَلَغَنِي عَنْ دَاوُدَ [عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ] أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "إِلَهِي كُنْ لِسُلَيْمَانَ كَمَا كُنْتَ لِي": فَأَوْحَى اللَّهُ إِلَيْهِ: أَنْ قُلْ لِسُلَيْمَانَ: يَكُونُ لِي كَمَا كُنْتَ لِي، أَكُونُ لَهُ كَمَا كنتُ لَكَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَسَخَّرْنَا لَهُ الرِّيحَ تَجْرِي بِأَمْرِهِ رُخَاءً حَيْثُ أَصَابَ﴾ قَالَ الْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ: لَمَّا عَقَرَ سُلَيْمَانُ الْخَيْلَ غَضَبًا لِلَّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ عَوَّضَهُ اللَّهُ مَا هُوَ خَيْرٌ مِنْهَا وَأَسْرَعُ الرِّيحُ الَّتِي غُدُوُّهَا شَهْرٌ وَرَوَاحُهَا شَهْرٌ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿حَيْثُ أَصَابَ﴾ أَيْ: حَيْثُ أَرَادَ مِنَ الْبِلَادِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَالشَّيَاطِينَ كُلَّ بَنَّاءٍ وَغَوَّاصٍ﴾ أَيْ: مِنْهُمْ مَنْ هُوَ مُسْتَعْمَلٌ فِي الْأَبْنِيَةِ الْهَائِلَةِ مِنْ مَحَارِيبَ وَتَمَاثِيلَ وَجَفَانٍ كَالْجَوَابِ وَقُدُورٍ رَاسِيَاتٍ إِلَى غَيْرِ ذَلِكَ مِنَ الْأَعْمَالِ الشَّاقَّةِ الَّتِي لَا يَقْدِرُ عَلَيْهَا الْبَشَرُ وَطَائِفَةٌ غَوَّاصُونَ فِي الْبِحَارِ يَسْتَخْرِجُونَ مِمَّا فِيهَا مِنَ اللَّآلِئِ وَالْجَوَاهِرِ وَالْأَشْيَاءِ النَّفِيسَةِ الَّتِي لَا تُوجَدُ إِلَّا فِيهَا ﴿وَآخَرِينَ مُقَرَّنِينَ فِي الأصْفَادِ﴾ أَيْ: مُوثَقُونَ فِي الْأَغْلَالِ وَالْأَكْبَالِ مِمَّنْ قَدْ تَمَرّد وَعَصَى وَامْتَنَعَ مِنَ الْعَمَلِ وَأَبَى أَوْ قَدْ أَسَاءَ فِي صنيعه واعتدى.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿هَذَا عَطَاؤُنَا فَامْنُنْ أَوْ أَمْسِكْ بِغَيْرِ حِسَابٍ﴾ أَيْ: هَذَا الَّذِي أَعْطَيْنَاكَ مِنَ الْمُلْكِ التَّامِّ وَالسُّلْطَانِ الْكَامِلِ كَمَا سَأَلْتَنَا فَأَعْطِ مَنْ شِئْتَ وَاحْرِمْ مَنْ شِئْتَ، لَا حِسَابَ عَلَيْكَ، أَيْ: مَهْمَا فعلتَ فَهُوَ جَائِزٌ لَكَ احْكُمْ بِمَا شِئْتَ فَهُوَ صَوَابٌ. وَقَدْ ثَبَتَ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ لَمَّا خُيِّر بَيْنَ أَنْ يَكُونَ عَبْدًا رَسُولًا -وَهُوَ الَّذِي يَفْعَلُ مَا يُؤْمَرُ بِهِ وَإِنَّمَا هُوَ قَاسِمٌ يَقْسِمُ بَيْنَ النَّاسِ مَا أَمَرَهُ اللَّهُ بِهِ-وَبَيْنَ أَنْ يَكُونَ مَلِكًا نَبِيًّا يُعْطِي مَنْ يَشَاءُ وَيَمْنَعُ مَنْ يَشَاءُ بِلَا حِسَابٍ وَلَا جُنَاحٍ، اخْتَارَ الْمَنْزِلَةَ الْأُولَى بَعْدَ مَا اسْتَشَارَ جِبْرِيلَ فَقَالَ لَهُ: تَوَاضَعْ فَاخْتَارَ الْمَنْزِلَةَ الْأُولَى لِأَنَّهَا أَرْفَعُ قَدْرًا عِنْدَ اللَّهِ وَأَعْلَى مَنْزِلَةً فِي الْمَعَادِ وَإِنْ كَانَتِ الْمَنْزِلَةُ الثَّانِيَةُ وَهِيَ النُّبُوَّةُ مَعَ الْمُلْكِ عَظِيمَةً أَيْضًا فِي الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ وَلِهَذَا لَمَّا ذَكَرَ تَبَارَكَ وَتَعَالَى مَا أَعْطَى سُلَيْمَانَ فِي الدُّنْيَا نَبَّهَ عَلَى أَنَّهُ ذُو حَظٍّ عَظِيمٍ عِنْدَ اللَّهِ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ أَيْضًا، فَقَالَ: ﴿وَإِنَّ لَهُ عِنْدَنَا لَزُلْفَى وَحُسْنَ مَآبٍ﴾ أَيْ: فِي الدَّارِ الْآخِرَةِ.

---

## 38:41-44 — verses 41-44 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty mentions His servant and messenger Job (peace be upon him) and the affliction with which He tested him in his body, his wealth, and his children, until there did not remain on his body a needle's prick worth of sound flesh, save his heart, and there remained nothing of his worldly circumstances by which he could help himself against his sickness and what he was suffering, except that his wife preserved her love for him because of her faith in Allah and His Messenger. She used to serve people for wages, and feed him and tend to him, for about eighteen years. Before that he had been possessed of abundant wealth, children, and vast worldly comfort, but all of it was stripped from him, until his condition came to such a state that he was cast upon one of the town's rubbish heaps for this entire period. Near and far abandoned him, except his wife, may Allah be pleased with her, for she did not leave him morning or evening except for the sake of serving people, then she would return to him shortly after.

When the delay grew long and the condition grew severe, and the decreed measure came to its end and the appointed term was completed, he implored the Lord of the worlds and God of the messengers, saying: {Truly affliction has touched me, and You are the Most Merciful of the merciful} [al-Anbiya: 83]. And in this noble verse he said: "My Lord, truly Satan has touched me with distress and torment." It is said: with distress in my body and torment in my wealth and children. At that, the Most Merciful of the merciful answered him and commanded him to rise from his place and to strike the ground with his foot. He did so, and Allah caused a spring to gush forth, and commanded him to wash from it, and it removed all the harm that was in his body. Then He commanded him, and he struck the ground in another place, and a second spring gushed forth for him, and He commanded him to drink from it, and it removed the corruption that was within him, and health was made complete outwardly and inwardly. For this reason the Almighty said: {Strike the ground with your foot; here is a cool bathing place and a drink}.

Ibn Jarir and Ibn Abi Hatim both said: [chain] from Anas ibn Malik, may Allah be pleased with him, that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "The prophet of Allah Job (peace be upon him) remained in his affliction for eighteen years, and near and far abandoned him except two men who were among his closest brothers; they used to come to him morning and evening. One of them said to his companion: 'Know, by Allah, Job has committed a sin that no one among the worlds has ever committed.' His companion said to him: 'What is that?' He said: 'For eighteen years Allah has not shown him mercy so as to remove what afflicts him.' When they went to him, the man could not restrain himself until he mentioned this to him. Job said: 'I do not know what you are saying, except that Allah knows that I used to pass by two men disputing and mentioning the name of Allah, the Mighty and Majestic, wrongfully, and I would return to my house and make atonement on their behalf, out of dislike that they should mention Allah's name except in truth.'" He said: "He used to go out to relieve himself, and when he had finished, his wife would take his hand until he reached home. One day he was delayed in returning to her, and Allah had revealed to Job (peace be upon him): {Strike the ground with your foot; here is a cool bathing place and a drink}. She grew anxious at his delay and went out to look for him, and he came toward her, Allah having removed the affliction that was upon him, and he was in the best state he had ever been. When she saw him she said: 'May Allah bless you, have you seen the prophet of Allah, this afflicted man? By Allah, I have never seen a man more resembling him than you, when he was in health.' He said: 'I am he.'" He said: "He had two threshing floors, one for wheat and one for barley. Allah sent two clouds; when one of them came over the wheat threshing floor it poured gold into it until it overflowed, and the other poured into the barley threshing floor until it overflowed." This is the wording of Ibn Jarir, may Allah have mercy on him.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] from Hammam ibn Munabbih, who said: this is what Abu Hurayrah related to us, saying: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "While Job was bathing naked, locusts of gold fell upon him, and Job began to gather them into his garment. His Lord called out to him: 'O Job, did I not make you rich enough to dispense with what you see?' He said: 'Yes, my Lord, but I cannot dispense with Your blessing.'"

Al-Bukhari alone transmitted this, from the hadith of Abd al-Razzaq, with this wording.

For this reason the Almighty said: {And We granted him his family and the like thereof along with them, as a mercy from Us and a reminder for those of understanding}. Al-Hasan and Qatadah said: Allah brought them back to life for him, the very same persons, and increased them by adding to them their like.

His saying, {a mercy from Us}, means: mercy shown to him for his patience, his steadfastness, his turning back to Allah, his humility, and his submission. {And a reminder for those of understanding} means: for people of intellect, so that they may know that the outcome of patience is relief, a way out, and ease.

His saying, {And take in your hand a bundle of grass and strike with it, and do not break your oath}: this was because Job (peace be upon him) had become angry with his wife and held something against her for a matter she had done. It is said she had sold her braid of hair for bread and fed it to him; he blamed her for this and swore that if Allah healed him he would strike her a hundred lashes. It is also said the reason was something else. When Allah healed him and restored him to health, it was not fitting that her reward, after this complete service, mercy, tenderness, and kindness, should be met with a beating. So Allah, the Mighty and Majestic, gave him the ruling that he should take a bundle, that is, a cluster of palm branches containing a hundred twigs, and strike her with it in a single blow. Thus his oath was fulfilled, he was released from breaking it, and he kept his vow. This was a relief and a way out for one who feared Allah and turned back to Him. For this reason the Almighty said: {Indeed We found him patient, an excellent servant; indeed he was one who often turned back to Allah}. Allah praised him and commended him as {an excellent servant; indeed he was one who often turned back to Allah}, that is, one who returns again and again in repentance. For this reason the Almighty said: {And whoever fears Allah, He will make for him a way out, and will provide for him from where he does not expect} [al-Talaq: 2-3].

Many jurists have used this noble verse as evidence for rulings concerning oaths and other matters, and have taken it according to its apparent implication, while another group of jurists prevented this, saying: it has not been established that expiation was legislated in the law of Job (peace be upon him), and that is why he was granted this dispensation in his case; and Allah has sufficed this nation with expiation instead.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَذْكُرُ تَعَالَى عَبْدَهُ وَرَسُولَهُ أَيُّوبَ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ وَمَا كَانَ ابْتَلَاهُ تَعَالَى بِهِ مِنَ الضُّرِّ فِي جَسَدِهِ وَمَالِهِ وَوَلَدِهِ حَتَّى لَمْ يَبْقَ مَنْ جَسَدِهِ مَغْرز إِبْرَةٍ سَلِيمًا سِوَى قَلْبِهِ وَلَمْ يَبْقَ لَهُ مَنْ حَالِ الدُّنْيَا شَيْءٌ يَسْتَعِينُ بِهِ عَلَى مَرَضِهِ وَمَا هُوَ فِيهِ غَيْرَ أَنَّ زَوْجَتَهُ حَفِظَتْ وِدَّهُ لِإِيمَانِهَا بِاللَّهِ وَرَسُولِهِ فَكَانَتْ تَخْدُمُ النَّاسَ بِالْأُجْرَةِ وَتُطْعِمُهُ وَتَخْدُمُهُ نَحْوًا مِنْ ثَمَانِي عَشْرَةَ سَنَةٍ. وَقَدْ كَانَ قَبْلَ ذَلِكَ فِي مَالٍ جَزِيلٍ وَأَوْلَادٍ وَسَعَةٍ طَائِلَةٍ مِنَ الدُّنْيَا فَسُلبَ جَمِيعَ ذَلِكَ حَتَّى آلَ بِهِ الْحَالُ إِلَى أَنْ أُلْقِيَ عَلَى مَزْبَلَةٍ مِنْ مَزَابِلِ الْبَلْدَةِ هَذِهِ الْمُدَّةَ بِكَمَالِهَا وَرَفَضَهُ الْقَرِيبُ وَالْبَعِيدُ سِوَى زَوْجَتِهِ رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا فَإِنَّهَا كَانَتْ لَا تُفَارِقُهُ صَبَاحًا وَ [لَا] مَسَاءً إِلَّا بِسَبَبِ خِدْمَةِ النَّاسِ ثُمَّ تَعُودُ إِلَيْهِ قَرِيبًا. فَلَمَّا طَالَ الْمَطَالُ وَاشْتَدَّ الْحَالُ وَانْتَهَى الْقَدَرُ الْمَقْدُورُ وَتَمَّ الْأَجَلُ الْمُقَدَّرُ تَضَرَّعَ إِلَى رَبِّ الْعَالَمِينَ وَإِلَهِ الْمُرْسَلِينَ فَقَالَ: ﴿أَنِّي مَسَّنِيَ الضُّرُّ وَأَنْتَ أَرْحَمُ الرَّاحِمِينَ﴾ [الْأَنْبِيَاءِ: ٨٣] وَفِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ الْكَرِيمَةِ قَالَ: رَبِّ إِنِّي مَسَّنِيَ الشَّيْطَانُ بِنُصْبٍ وَعَذَابٍ، قِيلَ: بِنُصْبٍ فِي بَدَنِي وَعَذَابٍ فِي مَالِي وَوَلَدِي. فَعِنْدَ ذَلِكَ اسْتَجَابَ لَهُ أَرْحَمُ الرَّاحِمِينَ وَأَمَرَهُ أَنْ يَقُومَ مِنْ مَقَامِهِ وَأَنْ يَرْكُضَ الْأَرْضَ بِرِجْلِهِ. فَفَعَلَ فَأَنْبَعَ اللَّهُ عَيْنًا وَأَمَرَهُ أَنْ يَغْتَسِلَ مِنْهَا فَأَذْهَبَ جَمِيعَ مَا كَانَ فِي بَدَنِهِ مِنَ الْأَذَى ثُمَّ أَمَرَهُ فَضَرَبَ الْأَرْضَ فِي مَكَانٍ آخَرَ فَأَنْبَعَ لَهُ عَيْنًا أُخْرَى وَأَمَرَهُ أَنْ يَشْرَبَ مِنْهَا فَأَذْهَبَتْ مَا كَانَ فِي بَاطِنِهِ مِنَ السُّوءِ وَتَكَامَلَتِ الْعَافِيَةُ ظَاهِرًا وَبَاطِنًا وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿ارْكُضْ بِرِجْلِكَ هَذَا مُغْتَسَلٌ بَارِدٌ وَشَرَابٌ﴾

قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، وَابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ جَمِيعًا: حَدَّثَنَا يُونُسُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الْأَعْلَى أَخْبَرَنَا ابْنُ وَهْبٍ أَخْبَرَنِي نَافِعُ بْنُ يَزِيدَ عَنْ عُقَيْلٍ عَنِ ابْنِ شِهَابٍ عَنْ أَنَسِ بْنِ مَالِكٍ رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "إِنَّ نَبِيَّ اللَّهِ أَيُّوبَ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ لَبِثَ بِهِ بَلَاؤُهُ ثَمَانِيَ عَشْرَةَ سَنَةً فَرَفَضَهُ الْقَرِيبُ وَالْبَعِيدُ إِلَّا رَجُلَيْنِ كَانَا مِنْ أَخَصِّ إِخْوَانِهِ بِهِ كَانَا يَغْدُوَانِ إِلَيْهِ وَيَرُوحَانِ فَقَالَ أَحَدُهُمَا لِصَاحِبِهِ: تَعَلَّمْ -وَاللَّهِ-لَقَدْ أَذْنَبَ أَيُّوبُ ذَنْبًا مَا أَذْنَبَهُ أَحَدٌ مِنَ الْعَالَمِينَ. قَالَ لَهُ صَاحِبُهُ: وَمَا ذَاكَ؟ قَالَ: مِنْ ثَمَانِيَ عَشْرَةَ سَنَةً لَمْ يَرْحَمْهُ اللَّهُ، فيكشفَ مَا بِهِ فَلَمَّا رَاحَا إِلَيْهِ لَمْ يَصْبِرِ الرَّجُلُ حَتَّى ذَكَرَ ذَلِكَ لَهُ. فَقَالَ أَيُّوبُ: لَا أَدْرِي مَا تَقُولُ غَيْرَ أَنَّ اللَّهَ يَعْلَمُ أَنِّي كُنْتُ أَمُرُّ عَلَى الرَّجُلَيْنِ يَتَنَازَعَانِ فَيَذْكُرَانِ اللَّهَ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، فَأَرْجِعُ إِلَى بَيْتِي فَأُكَفِّرُ عَنْهُمَا، كَرَاهِيَةَ أَنْ يَذْكُرَا اللَّهَ إِلَّا فِي حَقٍّ. قَالَ: وَكَانَ يَخْرُجُ إِلَى حَاجَتِهِ فَإِذَا قَضَاهَا أَمْسَكَتِ امْرَأَتُهُ بِيَدِهِ حَتَّى يَبْلُغَ فَلَمَّا كَانَ ذَاتَ يَوْمٍ أَبْطَأَ عَلَيْهَا وَأَوْحَى اللَّهُ تَعَالَى إِلَى أَيُّوبَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، أَنِ ﴿ارْكُضْ بِرِجْلِكَ هَذَا مُغْتَسَلٌ بَارِدٌ وَشَرَابٌ﴾ فَاسْتَبْطَأَتْهُ فَتَلَقَّتْهُ تَنْظُرُ فَأَقْبَلَ عَلَيْهَا قَدْ أَذْهَبَ اللَّهُ مَا بِهِ مِنَ الْبَلَاءِ وَهُوَ عَلَى أَحْسَنِ مَا كَانَ. فَلَمَّا رَأَتْهُ قَالَتْ: أَيْ بَارَكَ اللَّهُ فِيكَ هَلْ رَأَيْتَ نَبِيَّ اللَّهِ هَذَا الْمُبْتَلَى. فَوَاللَّهِ عَلَى ذَلِكَ مَا رَأَيْتُ رَجُلًا أَشْبَهَ بِهِ مِنْكَ إِذْ كَانَ صَحِيحًا. قَالَ: فَإِنِّي أَنَا هُوَ. قَالَ: وَكَانَ لَهُ أَنْدَرَانِ أَنْدَرُ لِلْقَمْحِ وَأَنْدَرُ لِلشَّعِيرِ فَبَعَثَ اللَّهُ سَحَابَتَيْنِ فَلَمَّا كَانَتْ إِحْدَاهُمَا عَلَى أَنْدَرِ الْقَمْحِ أَفْرَغَتْ فِيهِ الذَّهَبَ حَتَّى فَاضَ وَأَفْرَغَتِ الْأُخْرَى فِي أَنْدَرِ الشَّعِيرِ حَتَّى فَاضَ. هَذَا لَفْظُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ 

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ حَدَّثَنَا مَعْمَر عَنْ هَمَّامِ بْنِ مُنَبِّه قَالَ: هَذَا مَا حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو هُرَيْرَةَ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "بَيْنَمَا أَيُّوبُ يَغْتَسِلُ عُرْيَانًا خَرَّ عَلَيْهِ جَرَادٌ مِنْ ذَهَبٍ فَجَعَلَ أَيُّوبُ يَحْثُو فِي ثَوْبِهِ فَنَادَاهُ رَبُّهُ يَا أَيُّوبُ أَلَمْ أَكُنْ أَغْنَيْتُكَ عَمَّا تَرَى؟ قَالَ: بَلَى يَا رَبِّ وَلَكِنْ لَا غِنَى بِي عَنْ بَرَكَتِكَ".

انْفَرَدَ بِإِخْرَاجِهِ الْبُخَارِيُّ مِنْ حَدِيثِ عَبْدِ الرَّزَّاقِ بِهِ 

وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَوَهَبْنَا لَهُ أَهْلَهُ وَمِثْلَهُمْ مَعَهُمْ رَحْمَةً مِنَّا وَذِكْرَى لأولِي الألْبَابِ﴾ قَالَ الْحَسَنُ وَقَتَادَةُ: أَحْيَاهُمُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى لَهُ بِأَعْيَانِهِمْ وَزَادَهُمْ مِثْلَهُمْ مَعَهُمْ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿رَحْمَةً مِنَّا﴾ أَيْ: بِهِ عَلَى صَبْرِهِ وَثَبَاتِهِ وَإِنَابَتِهِ وَتَوَاضُعِهِ وَاسْتِكَانَتِهِ ﴿وَذِكْرَى لأولِي الألْبَابِ﴾ أَيْ: لِذَوِي الْعُقُولِ لِيَعْلَمُوا أَنَّ عاقبةَ الصَّبْرِ الفرجُ والمخرجُ والراحة.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَخُذْ بِيَدِكَ ضِغْثًا فَاضْرِبْ بِهِ وَلا تَحْنَثْ﴾ وَذَلِكَ أَنَّ أَيُّوبَ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ كَانَ قَدْ غَضِبَ عَلَى زَوْجَتِهِ وَوَجَدَ عَلَيْهَا فِي أَمْرٍ فَعَلَتْهُ. قِيلَ: [إِنَّهَا] بَاعَتْ ضَفِيرَتَهَا بِخُبْزٍ فَأَطْعَمَتْهُ إِيَّاهُ فَلَامَهَا عَلَى ذَلِكَ وَحَلِفَ إِنْ شَفَاهُ اللَّهُ لَيَضْرِبَنَّهَا مِائَةَ جِلْدَةٍ. وَقِيلَ: لِغَيْرِ ذَلِكَ مِنَ الْأَسْبَابِ. فَلَمَّا شَفَاهُ اللَّهُ وَعَافَاهُ مَا كَانَ جَزَاؤُهَا مَعَ هَذِهِ الْخِدْمَةِ التَّامَّةِ وَالرَّحْمَةِ وَالشَّفَقَةِ وَالْإِحْسَانِ أَنْ تُقَابَلَ بِالضَّرْبِ فَأَفْتَاهُ اللَّهُ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ أَنْ يَأْخُذَ ضِغْثًا -وَهُوَ: الشِّمراخ-فِيهِ مِائَةُ قَضِيبٍ فَيَضْرِبُهَا بِهِ ضَرْبَةً وَاحِدَةً وَقَدْ بَرّت يَمِينُهُ وَخَرَجَ مِنْ حِنْثِهِ وَوَفَى بِنَذْرِهِ وَهَذَا مِنَ الْفَرَجِ وَالْمَخْرَجِ لِمَنِ اتَّقَى اللَّهَ وَأَنَابَ إِلَيْهِ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنَّا وَجَدْنَاهُ صَابِرًا نِعْمَ الْعَبْدُ إِنَّهُ أَوَّابٌ﴾ أَثْنَى اللَّهُ تَعَالَى عَلَيْهِ وَمَدَحَهُ بِأَنَّهُ ﴿نِعْمَ الْعَبْدُ إِنَّهُ أَوَّابٌ﴾ أَيْ: رَجَّاع مُنِيبٌ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَنْ يَتَّقِ اللَّهَ يَجْعَلْ لَهُ مَخْرَجًا وَيَرْزُقْهُ مِنْ حَيْثُ لَا يَحْتَسِبُ﴾ [الطَّلَاقِ: ٢، ٣]

وَقَدِ اسْتَدَلَّ كَثِيرٌ مِنَ الْفُقَهَاءِ بِهَذِهِ الْآيَةِ الْكَرِيمَةِ عَلَى مَسَائِلَ فِي الْأَيْمَانِ وَغَيْرِهَا وَأَخَذُوهَا بِمُقْتَضَاهَا [وَمَنَعَتْ طَائِفَةٌ أُخْرَى مِنَ الْفُقَهَاءِ مِنْ ذَلِكَ، وَقَالُوا: لَمْ يَثْبُتْ أَنَّ الْكَفَّارَةَ كَانَتْ مَشْرُوعَةً فِي شَرْعِ أَيُّوبَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، فَلِذَلِكَ رَخَّصَ لَهُ فِي ذَلِكَ، وَقَدْ أَغْنَى اللَّهُ هَذِهِ الْأُمَّةَ بِالْكَفَّارَةِ]

---

## 38:45-48 — verses 45-48 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, informing of the virtues of His messenger servants and His worshipping prophets: {And remember Our servants Ibrahim and Ishaq and Ya'qub, possessors of hands and sight}. He means by that: righteous action, beneficial knowledge, strength in worship, and penetrating insight.

Ali ibn Abi Talhah said, on the authority of Ibn Abbas: {possessors of hands} means possessors of strength, {and sight} means understanding (fiqh) in religion.

Mujahid said: {possessors of hands} means strength in obedience to Allah, {and sight} means sight of the truth.

Qatadah and al-Suddi said: they were given strength in worship and insight in religion.

Concerning His saying {Indeed We purified them with a pure quality, remembrance of the Abode}, Mujahid said: meaning, We made them work for the Hereafter, having no concern besides it. Al-Suddi said likewise: their remembrance was of the Hereafter and their work was for it.

Malik ibn Dinar said: Allah removed from their hearts love of this world and remembrance of it, and He purified them with love of the Hereafter and remembrance of it. Ata al-Khurasani said the same.

Sa'id ibn Jubayr said: he means by "the Abode" the Garden, that is, We made it purely theirs through their remembrance of it. In another report he said: {remembrance of the Abode} means the final outcome of the Abode.

Qatadah said: they used to remind people of the final Abode and of working for it.

Ibn Zayd said: they were given, specially, the finest thing in the final Abode.

Concerning His saying {And indeed, in Our sight, they are among the chosen, the excellent}, that is, among those selected, chosen, and excellent. So they are excellent ones who are chosen.

Concerning His saying {And remember Ismail, and al-Yasa, and Dhul-Kifl, each of them among the excellent}, the discussion of their stories and reports has already been given in full in Surat al-Anbiya, which makes repeating it here unnecessary.

Concerning His saying {This is a remembrance}, that is, this is a passage containing a reminder for whoever takes heed.

Al-Suddi said: he means the Qur'an.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْ فَضَائِلَ عِبَادِهِ الْمُرْسَلِينَ وَأَنْبِيَائِهِ الْعَابِدِينَ: ﴿وَاذْكُرْ عِبَادَنَا إبْرَاهِيمَ وَإِسْحَاقَ وَيَعْقُوبَ أُولِي الأيْدِي وَالأبْصَارِ﴾ يَعْنِي بِذَلِكَ: الْعَمَلَ الصَّالِحَ وَالْعِلْمَ النَّافِعَ وَالْقُوَّةَ فِي الْعِبَادَةِ وَالْبَصِيرَةَ النَّافِذَةَ.

قَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿أُولِي الأيْدِي﴾ يَقُولُ: أُولِي الْقُوَّةِ ﴿وَالأبْصَارِ﴾ يَقُولُ: الْفِقْهِ فِي الدِّينِ.

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: ﴿أُولِي الأيْدِي﴾ يَعْنِي: الْقُوَّةَ فِي طَاعَةِ اللَّهِ ﴿وَالأبْصَارِ﴾ يَعْنِي: الْبَصَرَ فِي الْحَقِّ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ وَالسُّدِّيُّ: أعطُوا قُوَّةً فِي الْعِبَادَةِ وبَصرًا فِي الدِّينِ.

[وَقَوْلُهُ] ﴿إِنَّا أَخْلَصْنَاهُمْ بِخَالِصَةٍ ذِكْرَى الدَّارِ﴾ قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: أَيْ جَعَلْنَاهُمْ يَعْمَلُونَ لِلْآخِرَةِ لَيْسَ لَهُمْ هَمّ غَيْرُهَا. وَكَذَا قَالَ السُّدِّيُّ: ذِكْرُهُمْ لِلْآخِرَةِ وَعَمَلُهُمْ لَهَا.

وَقَالَ مَالِكُ بْنُ دِينَارٍ: نَزَعَ اللَّهُ مِنْ قُلُوبِهِمْ حُبَّ الدُّنْيَا وَذِكْرَهَا وَأَخْلَصَهُمْ بِحُبِّ الْآخِرَةِ وَذَكَرِهَا. وَكَذَا قال عطاء الخراساني.

وَقَالَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْر: يَعْنِي بِالدَّارِ الْجَنَّةَ يَقُولُ: أَخْلَصْنَاهَا لَهُمْ بِذِكْرِهِمْ لَهَا وَقَالَ فِي رِوَايَةٍ أُخْرَى: ﴿ذِكْرَى الدَّارِ﴾ عُقْبَى الدَّارِ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: كَانُوا يذَكّرون النَّاسَ الدَّارَ الْآخِرَةَ وَالْعَمَلَ لَهَا.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ زَيْدٍ: جُعِلَ لَهُمْ خَاصَّةً أَفْضَلُ شَيْءٍ فِي الدَّارِ الْآخِرَةِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَإِنَّهُمْ عِنْدَنَا لَمِنَ الْمُصْطَفَيْنَ الأخْيَارِ﴾ أَيْ: لَمِنَ الْمُخْتَارِينَ الْمُجْتَبِينَ الْأَخْيَارِ فَهُمْ أَخْيَارٌ مُخْتَارُونَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَاذْكُرْ إِسْمَاعِيلَ وَالْيَسَعَ وَذَا الْكِفْلِ وَكُلٌّ مِنَ الأخْيَارِ﴾ قَدْ تَقَدَّمَ الْكَلَامُ عَلَى قَصَصِهِمْ وَأَخْبَارِهِمْ مُسْتَقْصَاةً فِي سُورَةِ "الْأَنْبِيَاءِ" بِمَا أَغْنَى عَنْ إِعَادَتِهِ هَاهُنَا.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿هَذَا ذِكْرٌ﴾ أَيْ: هَذَا فَصْلٌ فِيهِ ذِكْرٌ لِمَنْ يَتَذَكَّرُ.

وَقَالَ السُّدِّيُّ: يَعْنِي الْقُرْآنَ.

---

## 38:49-54 — verses 49-54 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Exalted informs us about His believing, fortunate servants that they will have in the [abode of the] Hereafter {truly a good return}, meaning a place of return and a homecoming. Then He explained this by saying: {gardens of Eden}, meaning gardens of permanent dwelling, with their gates thrown open for them.

The definite article here functions as a possessive construction, as if He were saying "thrown open for them are its gates," meaning: when they come to them, their gates are opened for them.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Muhammad ibn Thawab al-Habbari told us, Abdullah ibn Numayr told us, Abdullah ibn Muslim (that is, ibn Hurmuz) told us, from Ibn Sabit, from Abdullah ibn Amr [may Allah be pleased with them both], who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "In Paradise there is a palace called 'Eden,' surrounded by towers and meadows. It has five thousand gates, and at each gate there are five thousand garments of fine silk (hibarah). None enters it, or none dwells in it, except a prophet, a truthful one (siddiq), a martyr, or a just ruler."

Many hadiths have come down through numerous chains concerning the eight gates of Paradise.

As for His saying: {reclining therein}, it has been said that this means sitting cross legged upon couches beneath canopies. {They call therein for abundant fruit}, meaning: whatever they request, they find it present just as they wished. {And drink}, meaning: of whatever kinds they desire, brought to them by servants, {in vessels, and pitchers, and a cup from a flowing spring} [al-Waqi'ah: 18].

{And with them are those of restrained glances}, meaning: restrained from looking at any but their own husbands, they do not turn their gaze toward anyone other than their spouses, {of equal age}, meaning: equal to one another in age and years.
