This is the meaning given by Ibn Abbas, Mujahid, Sa'id ibn Jubayr, Muhammad ibn Ka'b, and al-Suddi.

{This is what you were promised for the Day of Reckoning}, meaning: this which We have described of the attributes of Paradise, which He promised to His righteous servants, to which they will go after their resurrection and their rising from their graves and their safety from the Fire.

Then He informed us about Paradise that it has no exhaustion, no ending, no passing away, and no termination, saying: {Truly this is Our provision, which will never be exhausted}, just as He said: {What you have will perish, but what is with Allah will remain} [al-Nahl: 96], and just as He said: {a gift never to be cut off} [Hud: 108], and just as He said: {for them is a reward uninterrupted} [Fussilat: 8], meaning: never cut off, and just as He said: {its fruit is everlasting, and so is its shade. Such is the end of those who feared Allah, while the end of the disbelievers is the Fire} [al-Ra'd: 35]. The verses on this matter are very numerous indeed.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنْ عِبَادِهِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ السُّعَدَاءِ أَنَّ لَهُمْ فِي [الدَّارِ] الْآخِرَةِ ﴿لَحُسْنَ مَآبٍ﴾ وَهُوَ: الْمُرْجِعُ وَالْمُنْقَلَبُ. ثُمَّ فَسَّرَهُ بِقَوْلِهِ: ﴿جَنَّاتِ عَدْنٍ﴾ أَيْ: جَنَّاتِ إِقَامَةٍ مُفَتَّحَةً لَهُمُ الْأَبْوَابُ.

وَالْأَلِفُ وَاللَّامُ هُنَا بِمَعْنَى الْإِضَافَةِ كَأَنَّهُ يَقُولُ: "مُفَتَّحَةً لَهُمْ أَبْوَابُهَا" أَيْ: إِذَا جَاءُوهَا فُتِحَتْ لَهُمْ أَبْوَابُهَا.

قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ ثَوَابٍ الهَبَّاري حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ نُمَيْر، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ مُسْلِمٍ -يَعْنِي: ابْنَ هُرْمُزَ-عَنِ ابْنِ سَابِطٍ عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمْرٍو [رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا] قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عليه وسلم: "إِنَّ فِي الْجَنَّةِ قَصْرًا يُقَالُ لَهُ: "عَدْنٌ" حَوْلَهُ الْبُرُوجُ وَالْمُرُوجُ لَهُ خَمْسَةُ آلَافِ بَابٍ عِنْدَ كُلِّ بَابٍ خَمْسَةُ آلَافِ حبَرَة لَا يَدْخُلُهُ -أَوْ: لَا يَسْكُنُهُ-إِلَّا نَبِيٌّ أَوْ صِدِّيقٌ أَوْ شَهِيدٌ أَوْ إِمَامٌ عَدْلٌ". 

وَقَدْ وَرَدَ فِي [ذِكْرِ] أَبْوَابِ الْجَنَّةِ الثَّمَانِيَةِ أَحَادِيثُ كَثِيرَةٌ مِنْ وُجُوهٍ عَدِيدَةٍ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿مُتَّكِئِينَ فِيهَا﴾ قِيلَ: مُتَرَبِّعِينَ فِيهَا عَلَى سُرُرٍ تَحْتَ الْحِجَالِ ﴿يَدْعُونَ فِيهَا بِفَاكِهَةٍ كَثِيرَةٍ﴾

أَيْ: مَهْمَا طَلَبُوا وَجَدُوا وَحَضَرَ كَمَا أَرَادُوا. ﴿وَشَرَابٍ﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ أَيِّ أَنْوَاعِهِ شَاءُوا أَتَتْهُمْ بِهِ الْخُدَّامُ ﴿بِأَكْوَابٍ وَأَبَارِيقَ وَكَأْسٍ مِنْ مَعِينٍ﴾ [الْوَاقِعَةِ: ١٨]

﴿وَعِنْدَهُمْ قَاصِرَاتُ الطَّرْفِ﴾ أَيْ: عَنْ غَيْرِ أَزْوَاجِهِنَّ فَلَا يَلْتَفِتْنَ إِلَى غَيْرِ بُعُولَتِهِنَّ ﴿أَتْرَابٌ﴾ أَيْ: مُتَسَاوِيَاتٌ فِي السِّنِّ وَالْعُمُرِ. هَذَا مَعْنَى قَوْلِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، وَمُجَاهِدٍ وَسَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ وَمُحَمَّدِ بْنِ كَعْبٍ وَالسُّدِّيِّ.

﴿هَذَا مَا تُوعَدُونَ لِيَوْمِ الْحِسَابِ﴾ أَيْ: هَذَا الَّذِي ذَكَرْنَا مِنْ صِفَةِ الْجَنَّةِ الَّتِي وَعَدَهَا لِعِبَادِهِ الْمُتَّقِينَ الَّتِي يَصِيرُونَ إِلَيْهَا بَعْدَ نُشُورِهِمْ وَقِيَامِهِمْ مِنْ قُبُورِهِمْ وَسَلَامَتِهِمْ مِنَ النَّارِ.

ثُمَّ أَخْبَرَ عَنِ الْجَنَّةِ أَنَّهُ لَا فَرَاغَ لَهَا وَلَا انْقِضَاءَ وَلَا زَوَالَ وَلَا انْتِهَاءَ فَقَالَ: ﴿إِنَّ هَذَا لَرِزْقُنَا مَا لَهُ مِنْ نَفَادٍ﴾ كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿مَا عِنْدَكُمْ يَنْفَدُ وَمَا عِنْدَ اللَّهِ بَاقٍ﴾ [النَّحْلِ: ٩٦] وَكَقَوْلِهِ ﴿عَطَاءً غَيْرَ مَجْذُوذٍ﴾ [هُودٍ: ١٠٨] وَكَقَوْلِهِ ﴿لَهُمْ أَجْرٌ غَيْرُ مَمْنُونٍ﴾ [فُصِّلَتْ: ٨] أَيْ: غَيْرُ مَقْطُوعٍ وَكَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿أُكُلُهَا دَائِمٌ وَظِلُّهَا تِلْكَ عُقْبَى الَّذِينَ اتَّقَوْا وَعُقْبَى الْكَافِرِينَ النَّارُ﴾ [الرَّعْدِ: ٣٥] وَالْآيَاتُ فِي هَذَا كَثِيرَةٌ جِدًّا.

---

## 38:55-64 — verses 55-64 (shared commentary)

### Translation

When the Exalted mentioned the destination of the fortunate ones, He followed it by mentioning the state of the wretched ones, their return and their place of coming back in the abode of their resurrection and their reckoning. He said: {This, and indeed for the transgressors} that is, those who go out from obedience to Allah and oppose the messengers of Allah, {is the worst place of return}, meaning the worst outcome and return. Then He explained it by His saying: {Hell, they will enter it to burn}, that is, they will enter it and it will engulf them from all their sides, {and how wretched is the resting place. This, then let them taste it: scalding water and dark, foul liquid}. As for al-hamim, it is the extremely hot liquid whose heat has reached its utmost limit. As for al-ghassaq, it is its opposite, the intensely cold substance whose cold is unbearable due to its painful severity. This is why He said: {and other things of its kind, in pairs}, meaning things of this same category, a thing and its opposite, by which they are punished.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] from Abu Sa'id, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, that he said: "If a single bucketful of ghassaq were poured out into this world, it would make the people of this world stink." Al-Tirmidhi narrated it from Suwayd ibn Nasr, from Ibn al-Mubarak, from Rishdin ibn Sa'd, from Amr ibn al-Harith, from Darraj, with the same chain. Then he said: "We know it only through the hadith of Rishdin." This is what he said, though it has already been narrated through a chain other than his. Ibn Jarir also narrated it from Yunus ibn Abd al-A'la, from Ibn Wahb, from Amr ibn al-Harith, with the same chain.

Ka'b al-Ahbar said: Ghassaq is a spring in Hell into which the venom of every venomous creature flows, of snakes and scorpions and other such things, and it collects there in a pool. A human being is brought and dipped into it a single dip, and he comes out with his skin and flesh having fallen off his bones, his skin and flesh hanging only at his ankles and heels, and he drags his flesh behind him as a man drags his garment. Ibn Abi Hatim narrated this.

Al-Hasan al-Basri said regarding His saying, {and other things of its kind, in pairs}: various kinds of torment.

Others said: such as intense cold, scorching wind, drinking scalding water, eating from the tree of Zaqqum, being forced to climb, and being cast down, and other such varied and opposite things, all of which are means by which they are tormented and by which they are humiliated.

His saying: {This is a company rushing in headlong with you. No welcome for them. Indeed, they will burn in the Fire} is a report of what the people of the Fire say to one another, just as the Exalted said: {Every time a nation enters, it curses its sister nation} [al-A'raf: 38], meaning that instead of greeting one another with peace, they curse one another, accuse one another of lying, and disbelieve in one another. The group that enters before another group will say, when the group that comes after it is brought in along with the guardian angels of the Fire: {This is a company rushing in}, meaning entering along with you, {no welcome for them, indeed they will burn in the Fire}, that is, because they are among the people of Hell. {They said: Rather, you, no welcome for you}, meaning the ones entering will say to them: {Rather, you, no welcome for you, you brought this upon us}, meaning: you called us to what led us to this destination, {and how wretched is this settled abode}, meaning how wretched is this dwelling place, resting place, and destination. {They said: Our Lord, whoever brought this upon us, increase for him a double punishment in the Fire}, just as He, Mighty and Majestic, said: {The last of them will say about the first of them: Our Lord, these led us astray, so give them a double punishment of the Fire. He said: For each is a double, but you do not know} [al-A'raf: 38], meaning: each of you has a punishment according to what he deserves.

{And they said: What is with us, that we do not see men whom we used to count among the wicked? Did we take them in mockery, or have our eyes missed them?} This is a report about the disbelievers in the Fire, that they will miss certain men whom they had believed to be misguided, these being the believers according to their false claim. They will say: what is with us that we do not see them with us in the Fire?

Mujahid said: this is the statement of Abu Jahl, who used to say: what is with me that I do not see Bilal, Ammar, Suhayb, and so and so and so and so. This is an example given, but otherwise every disbeliever is in this same state: they believe that the believers will enter the Fire. So when the disbelievers entered the Fire, they looked for them and did not find them, and said: {What is with us, that we do not see men whom we used to count among the wicked? Did we take them in mockery} in this world, {or have our eyes missed them?} They console themselves with an impossibility, saying: perhaps they are with us in Hell but our eyes have simply not fallen upon them. At that point they come to know that those men are in the elevated ranks, and this is His saying: {And the companions of Paradise will call out to the companions of the Fire: We have found what our Lord promised us to be true, so have you found what your Lord promised to be true? They will say: Yes. Then a caller will announce among them that the curse of Allah is upon the wrongdoers} up to His saying: {And the companions of al-A'raf will call out to men whom they recognize by their mark, saying: Of no benefit to you was your gathering of wealth and your arrogance. Are these the ones about whom you swore that Allah would not grant them any mercy? Enter Paradise, no fear will be upon you nor will you grieve} [al-A'raf: 44-49].

His saying: {Indeed that is true, the mutual dispute of the people of the Fire}, meaning: this which We have informed you of, O Muhammad, concerning the mutual disputing of the people of the Fire with one another, and their cursing one another, is indeed true, with no doubt or uncertainty in it whatsoever.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

لَمَّا ذَكَرَ تَعَالَى مَآلَ السُّعَدَاءِ ثَنّى بِذِكْرِ حَالِ الْأَشْقِيَاءِ وَمَرْجِعِهِمْ وَمَآبِهِمْ فِي دَارِ مَعَادِهِمْ وَحِسَابِهِمْ فَقَالَ: ﴿هَذَا وَإِنَّ لِلطَّاغِينَ﴾ وَهُمُ: الْخَارِجُونَ عَنْ طَاعَةِ اللَّهِ الْمُخَالِفُونَ لِرُسُلِ اللَّهِ ﴿لَشَرَّ مَآبٍ﴾ أَيْ: لَسُوءَ مُنْقَلَبٍ وَمَرْجِعٍ. ثُمَّ فَسَّرَهُ بِقَوْلِهِ: ﴿جَهَنَّمَ يَصْلَوْنَهَا﴾ أَيْ: يَدْخُلُونَهَا فَتَغْمُرُهُمْ مِنْ جَمِيعِ جَوَانِبِهِمْ ﴿فَبِئْسَ الْمِهَادُ. هَذَا فَلْيَذُوقُوهُ حَمِيمٌ وَغَسَّاقٌ﴾ أَمَّا الْحَمِيمُ فَهُوَ: الْحَارُّ الَّذِي قَدِ انْتَهَى حَرُّهُ وَأَمَّا الغَسَّاق فَهُوَ: ضِدُّهُ، وَهُوَ الْبَارِدُ الَّذِي لَا يُسْتَطَاعُ مِنْ شِدَّةِ بَرْدِهِ الْمُؤْلِمِ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَآخَرُ مِنْ شَكْلِهِ أَزْوَاجٌ﴾ أَيْ: وَأَشْيَاءُ مِنْ هَذَا الْقَبِيلِ، الشَّيْءُ وَضِدُّهُ يُعَاقَبُونَ بِهَا.

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا حَسَنُ بْنُ مُوسَى حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ لَهِيعة حَدَّثَنَا دَرّاج عَنْ أَبِي الْهَيْثَمِ عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "لَوْ أَنَّ دَلْوًا مِنْ غَسَّاق يُهَرَاقُ فِي الدُّنْيَا لأنتن أهل الدنيا" وَرَوَاهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ عَنْ سُوَيْد بْنِ نَصْرٍ عَنِ ابْنِ الْمُبَارَكِ عَنْ رِشْدين بْنِ سَعْدٍ عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ الْحَارِثِ عَنْ دَرّاج بِهِ. ثُمَّ قَالَ: "لَا نَعْرِفُهُ إِلَّا مِنْ حَدِيثِ رِشْدِينَ" كَذَا قَالَ: وَقَدْ تَقَدَّمَ مِنْ غَيْرِ حَدِيثِهِ وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ عَنْ يُونُسَ بْنِ عَبْدِ الْأَعْلَى عَنِ ابْنِ وَهْبٍ عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ الْحَارِثِ بِهِ 

وَقَالَ كَعْبُ الْأَحْبَارِ: غَسَّاقٌ: عَيْنٌ فِي جَهَنَّمَ يَسِيلُ إِلَيْهَا حُمَة كُلِّ ذَاتِ حُمَة مِنْ حَيَّةٍ وَعَقْرَبٍ وَغَيْرِ ذَلِكَ فَيَسْتَنْقِعُ فَيُؤْتَى بِالْآدَمِيِّ فَيُغْمَسُ فِيهَا غَمْسَةً وَاحِدَةً فَيَخْرُجُ وَقَدْ سَقَطَ جِلْدُهُ وَلَحْمُهُ عَنِ الْعِظَامِ وَيَتَعَلَّقُ جِلْدُهُ وَلَحْمُهُ فِي كَعْبَيْهِ وَعَقِبَيْهِ ويُجَر لَحْمَهُ كَمَا يَجُر الرَّجُلُ ثَوْبَهُ. رَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ.

وَقَالَ الْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَآخَرُ مِنْ شَكْلِهِ أَزْوَاجٌ﴾ أَلْوَانٌ مِنَ الْعَذَابِ.

وَقَالَ غَيْرُهُ: كَالزَّمْهَرِيرِ وَالسَّمُومِ وَشُرْبِ الْحَمِيمِ وَأَكْلِ الزَّقُّومِ وَالصُّعُودِ وَالْهُوِيُّ إِلَى غَيْرِ ذَلِكَ مِنَ الْأَشْيَاءِ الْمُخْتَلِفَةِ وَالْمُتَضَادَّةِ وَالْجَمِيعُ مِمَّا يُعَذَّبُونَ بِهِ وَيُهَانُونَ بِسَبَبِهِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿هَذَا فَوْجٌ مُقْتَحِمٌ مَعَكُمْ لَا مَرْحَبًا بِهِمْ إِنَّهُمْ صَالُوا النَّارِ﴾ هَذَا إِخْبَارٌ عَنْ قِيلِ أَهْلِ النَّارِ بَعْضُهُمْ لِبَعْضٍ كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿كُلَّمَا دَخَلَتْ أُمَّةٌ لَعَنَتْ أُخْتَهَا﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ٣٨] يَعْنِي بَدَلَ السَّلَامِ يَتَلَاعَنُونَ وَيَتَكَاذَبُونَ وَيَكْفُرُ بَعْضُهُمْ بِبَعْضٍ فَتَقُولُ الطَّائِفَةُ الَّتِي تَدْخُلُ قَبْلَ الْأُخْرَى إِذَا أَقْبَلَتِ الَّتِي بَعْدَهَا مَعَ الْخَزَنَةِ مِنَ الزَّبَانِيَةِ: ﴿هَذَا فَوْجٌ مُقْتَحِمٌ﴾ أَيْ: دَاخِلٌ مَعَكُمْ ﴿لَا مَرْحَبًا بِهِمْ إِنَّهُمْ صَالُوا النَّارِ﴾ [أَيْ] لِأَنَّهُمْ مِنْ أَهْلِ جَهَنَّمَ ﴿قَالُوا بَلْ أَنْتُمْ لَا مَرْحَبًا بِكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: فَيَقُولُ لَهُمُ الدَّاخِلُونَ: ﴿بَلْ أَنْتُمْ لَا مَرْحَبًا بِكُمْ أَنْتُمْ قَدَّمْتُمُوهُ لَنَا﴾ أَيْ: أَنْتُمْ دَعَوْتُمُونَا إِلَى مَا أَفْضَى بِنَا إِلَى هَذَا الْمَصِيرِ ﴿فَبِئْسَ الْقَرَارُ﴾ أَيْ: فَبِئْسَ الْمَنْزِلُ وَالْمُسْتَقَرُّ وَالْمَصِيرُ. ﴿قَالُوا رَبَّنَا مَنْ قَدَّمَ لَنَا هَذَا فَزِدْهُ عَذَابًا ضِعْفًا فِي النَّارِ﴾ كَمَا قَالَ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ ﴿قَالَتْ أُخْرَاهُمْ لأولاهُمْ رَبَّنَا هَؤُلاءِ أَضَلُّونَا فَآتِهِمْ عَذَابًا ضِعْفًا مِنَ النَّارِ قَالَ لِكُلٍّ ضِعْفٌ وَلَكِنْ لَا تَعْلَمُونَ﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ٣٨] أَيْ: لِكُلٍّ مِنْكُمْ عَذَابٌ بِحَسَبِهِ ﴿وَقَالُوا مَا لَنَا لَا نَرَى رِجَالا كُنَّا نَعُدُّهُمْ مِنَ الأشْرَارِ أَتَّخَذْنَاهُمْ سِخْرِيًّا أَمْ زَاغَتْ عَنْهُمُ الأبْصَارُ﴾ هَذَا إِخْبَارٌ عَنِ الْكُفَّارِ فِي النَّارِ أَنَّهُمْ يَفْقِدُونَ رِجَالًا كَانُوا يَعْتَقِدُونَ أَنَّهُمْ عَلَى الضَّلَالَةِ وَهُمُ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ فِي زَعْمِهِمْ قَالُوا: مَا لَنَا لَا نَرَاهُمْ مَعَنَا فِي النَّارِ؟.

قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: هَذَا قَوْلُ أَبِي جَهْلٍ يَقُولُ: مَا لِي لَا أَرَى بِلَالًا وَعَمَّارًا وَصُهَيْبًا وَفُلَانًا وَفُلَانًا. وَهَذَا مَثَلٌ ضُرِبَ، وَإِلَّا فَكُلُّ الْكُفَّارِ هَذَا حَالُهُمْ: يَعْتَقِدُونَ أَنَّ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ يَدْخُلُونَ النَّارَ فَلَمَّا دَخَلَ الْكُفَّارُ النَّارَ افْتَقَدُوهُمْ فَلَمْ يَجِدُوهُمْ فَقَالُوا: ﴿مَا لَنَا لَا نَرَى رِجَالا كُنَّا نَعُدُّهُمْ مِنَ الأشْرَارِ أَتَّخَذْنَاهُمْ سِخْرِيًّا أَمْ زَاغَتْ عَنْهُمُ الأبْصَارُ﴾ أَيْ: فِي الدُّنْيَا ﴿أَمْ زَاغَتْ عَنْهُمُ الأبْصَارُ﴾ يُسَلُّونَ أَنْفُسَهُمْ بِالْمُحَالِ يقولون: أو لعلهم مَعَنَا فِي جَهَنَّمَ وَلَكِنْ لَمْ يَقَعْ بَصَرُنَا عَلَيْهِمْ. فَعِنْدَ ذَلِكَ يَعْرِفُونَ أَنَّهُمْ فِي الدَّرَجَاتِ الْعَالِيَاتِ وَهُوَ قَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَنَادَى أَصْحَابُ الْجَنَّةِ أَصْحَابَ النَّارِ أَنْ قَدْ وَجَدْنَا مَا وَعَدَنَا رَبُّنَا حَقًّا فَهَلْ وَجَدْتُمْ مَا وَعَدَ رَبُّكُمْ حَقًّا قَالُوا نَعَمْ فَأَذَّنَ مُؤَذِّنٌ بَيْنَهُمْ أَنْ لَعْنَةُ اللَّهِ عَلَى الظَّالِمِينَ﴾ إِلَى قَوْلِهِ: ﴿ [وَنَادَى أَصْحَابُ الأعْرَافِ رِجَالا يَعْرِفُونَهُمْ بِسِيمَاهُمْ قَالُوا مَا أَغْنَى عَنْكُمْ جَمْعُكُمْ وَمَا كُنْتُمْ تَسْتَكْبِرُونَ. أَهَؤُلاءِ الَّذِينَ أَقْسَمْتُمْ لَا يَنَالُهُمُ اللَّهُ بِرَحْمَةٍ] ادْخُلُوا الْجَنَّةَ لَا خَوْفٌ عَلَيْكُمْ وَلا أَنْتُمْ تَحْزَنُونَ﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ٤٤ -٤٩] 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِنَّ ذَلِكَ لَحَقٌّ تَخَاصُمُ أَهْلِ النَّارِ﴾ أَيْ: إِنَّ هَذَا الَّذِي أَخْبَرْنَاكَ بِهِ يَا مُحَمَّدُ مِنْ تَخَاصُمِ أَهْلِ النَّارِ بَعْضُهُمْ فِي بَعْضٍ وَلَعْنِ بَعْضِهِمْ لِبَعْضٍ لَحَقٌّ لَا مِرْيَةَ فِيهِ وَلَا شَكَّ.

---

## 38:65-70 — verses 65-70 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, commanding His Messenger ﷺ to say to those who disbelieve in Allah, associate partners with Him, and reject His Messenger: I am only a warner, I am not as you claim. {And there is no god except Allah, the One, the Overpowering.} That is: He alone has overpowered everything and prevailed over it. {Lord of the heavens and the earth and whatever is between them, the Almighty, the Ever-Forgiving.} That is: He is the possessor of all of that and the one who disposes of it as He wills. {The Almighty, the Ever-Forgiving} that is, He is ever-forgiving despite His might and His greatness.

{Say: It is a great tiding} that is, a great piece of news and a weighty matter, namely Allah's sending of me to you. {From which you turn away} that is, in heedlessness.

Mujahid, Shurayh the judge, and al-Suddi said regarding His statement {Say: It is a great tiding}: it refers to the Qur'an.

His statement: {I had no knowledge of the highest assembly when they were disputing} means: were it not for revelation, how would I have known of the dispute of the highest assembly? That is, concerning the affair of Adam (peace be upon him) and Iblis's refusal to prostrate to him, and his arguing with his Lord about Adam's being preferred over him.

As for the hadith which Imam Ahmad narrated, where he said: [chain] Abu Sa'id, the freedman of the Banu Hashim, told us, Jahdam al-Yamami told us, from Yahya ibn Abi Kathir, from Zayd ibn Abi Sallam, from Abu Sallam, from Abd al-Rahman ibn A'ish, from Malik ibn Yukhamir, from Mu'adh, may Allah be pleased with him, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ was delayed from us one morning from the dawn prayer until we almost thought we could see the edge of the sun's rays. Then the Messenger of Allah ﷺ came out quickly and had the call to gather for prayer given, and he prayed and made his prayer brief. When he gave the closing greeting, he said: "Remain as you are in your rows." Then he turned to face us and said: "I will tell you what kept me from you this morning. I got up in the night and prayed as much as was decreed for me, and I dozed in my prayer until I woke up and found myself before my Lord in the most beautiful form. He said: O Muhammad, do you know about what the highest assembly is disputing? I said: I do not know, my Lord, and he repeated it three times. Then I saw him place his palm between my shoulders until I felt the coolness of his fingertips between my chest, and everything became clear to me and I came to know. He said: O Muhammad, about what does the highest assembly dispute? I said: About the expiations. He said: And what are the expiations? I said: Moving the feet toward the Friday prayers, sitting in the mosques after the prayers, and performing ablution fully even in unpleasant circumstances. He said: And what are the elevations in rank? I said: Feeding food, gentle speech, and prayer while people are asleep. He said: Ask. I said: O Allah, I ask You for the doing of good deeds, the abandonment of forbidden deeds, love of the poor, and that You forgive me and have mercy on me, and if You intend a trial for a people, then take me to You without being subjected to trial, and I ask You for Your love and the love of those who love You, and the love of deeds that draw me nearer to Your love." The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "It is true, so study it and learn it." This is the well-known hadith of the dream (al-manam), and whoever takes it to be a waking event has erred. It is found in the Sunan through several routes.

This very hadith was narrated by al-Tirmidhi from the hadith of "Jahdam ibn Abd Allah al-Yamami," with the same chain, and he said: "hasan sahih (sound and authentic)." This dispute, however, is not the same dispute mentioned in the Qur'an, for this one has already been explained, while the dispute mentioned in the Qur'an is explained further on, in His statement, the Almighty:

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى آمِرًا رَسُولَهُ ﷺ أَنْ يَقُولَ لِلْكَفَّارِ بِاللَّهِ الْمُشْرِكِينَ بِهِ الْمُكَذِّبِينَ لِرَسُولِهِ: إِنَّمَا أَنَا مُنْذِرٌ لَسْتُ كَمَا تَزْعُمُونَ ﴿وَمَا مِنْ إِلَهٍ إِلا اللَّهُ الْوَاحِدُ الْقَهَّارُ﴾ أَيْ: هُوَ وَحْدَهُ قَدْ قَهَرَ كل شيء وغلبه. ﴿رَبُّ السَّمَوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ وَمَا بَيْنَهُمَا الْعَزِيزُ الْغَفَّارُ﴾ أَيْ: هُوَ مَالِكٌ جَمِيعَ ذَلِكَ وَمُتَصَرِّفٌ فِيهِ ﴿الْعَزِيزُ الْغَفَّارُ﴾ أَيْ: غَفَّارٌ مَعَ عِزَّتِهِ وَعَظَمَتِهِ.

﴿قُلْ هُوَ نَبَأٌ عَظِيمٌ﴾ أَيْ: خَبَرٌ عَظِيمٌ وَشَأْنٌ بَلِيغٌ وَهُوَ إِرْسَالُ اللَّهِ إِيَّايَ إِلَيْكُمْ ﴿أَنْتُمْ عَنْهُ مُعْرِضُونَ﴾ أَيْ: غَافِلُونَ.

قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ وَشُرَيْحٌ الْقَاضِي وَالسُّدِّيُّ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿قُلْ هُوَ نَبَأٌ عَظِيمٌ﴾ يَعْنِي: الْقُرْآنَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿مَا كَانَ لِيَ مِنْ عِلْمٍ بِالْمَلإ الأعْلَى إِذْ يَخْتَصِمُونَ﴾ أَيْ: لَوْلَا الْوَحْيُ مِنْ أَيْنَ كُنْتُ أَدْرِي بِاخْتِلَافِ الْمَلَأِ الْأَعْلَى؟ يَعْنِي: فِي شَأْنِ آدَمَ وَامْتِنَاعِ إِبْلِيسَ مِنَ السُّجُودِ لَهُ، وَمُحَاجَّتِهِ رَبَّهُ فِي تَفْضِيلِهِ عَلَيْهِ.

فَأَمَّا الْحَدِيثُ الذِي رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ حَيْثُ قَالَ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو سَعِيدٍ مَوْلَى بَنِي هَاشِمٍ حَدَّثَنَا جَهْضَمٌ الْيَمَامِيُّ عَنْ يَحْيَى بْنُ أَبِي كَثِيرٍ، عَنْ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَبِي سَلَّامٍ عَنْ أَبِي سَلَّامٍ عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ عَائِشٍ عَنْ مَالِكِ بْنِ يُخَامِرَ عَنْ مُعَاذٍ رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: احْتَبَسَ عَلَيْنَا رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ ذَاتَ غَدَاةٍ عَنْ صَلَاةِ الصُّبْحِ حَتَّى كِدْنَا نَتَرَاءَى قَرْنَ الشَّمْسِ. فَخَرَجَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ سَرِيعًا فَثَوّب بِالصَّلَاةِ فَصَلَّى وتَجَوّز فِي صَلَاتِهِ فَلَمَّا سَلَّمَ قَالَ: "كَمَا أَنْتُمْ عَلَى مَصَافِّكُمْ". ثُمَّ أَقْبَلُ إِلَيْنَا فَقَالَ: "إِنِّي سَأُحَدِّثُكُمْ مَا حَبَسَنِي عَنْكُمُ الْغَدَاةَ، إِنِّي قُمْتُ مِنَ اللَّيْلِ فَصَلَّيْتُ مَا قُدّر لِي فَنَعَسْتُ فِي صَلَاتِي حَتَّى اسْتَيْقَظْتُ فَإِذَا أَنَا بِرَبِّي فِي أَحْسَنِ صُورَةٍ فَقَالَ: يَا مُحَمَّدُ أَتَدْرِي فِيمَ يختصم الملأ الأعلى؟ قُلْتُ لَا أَدْرِي رَبِّ -أَعَادَهَا ثَلَاثًا-فَرَأَيْتُهُ وَضَعَ كَفَّهُ بَيْنَ كَتِفِي حَتَّى وَجَدْتُ بَرْدَ أَنَامِلِهِ بَيْنَ صَدْرِي فَتَجَلَّى لِي كُلُّ شَيْءٍ وَعَرَفْتُ فَقَالَ: يَا مُحَمَّدُ فِيمَ يَخْتَصِمُ الْمَلَأُ الْأَعْلَى؟ قُلْتُ: فِي الْكَفَّارَاتِ. قَالَ: وَمَا الْكَفَّارَاتُ؟ قُلْتُ نَقْلُ الْأَقْدَامِ إِلَى الْجُمُعَاتِ وَالْجُلُوسُ فِي الْمَسَاجِدِ بَعْدَ الصَّلَوَاتِ وَإِسْبَاغُ الْوُضُوءِ عِنْدَ الْكَرِيهَاتِ. قَالَ: وَمَا الدَّرَجَاتُ؟ قُلْتُ: إِطْعَامُ الطَّعَامِ وَلِينُ الْكَلَامِ وَالصَّلَاةُ وَالنَّاسُ نِيَامٌ. قَالَ: سَلْ. قُلْتُ اللَّهُمَّ إِنِّي أَسْأَلُكَ فِعْلَ الْخَيْرَاتِ، وَتَرْكَ الْمُنْكَرَاتِ، وَحُبَّ الْمَسَاكِينِ، وَأَنْ تَغْفِرَ لِي وَتَرْحَمَنِي، وَإِذَا أَرَدْتَ فِتْنَةً بِقَوْمٍ فَتَوَفَّنِي غَيْرَ مَفْتُونٍ، وَأَسْأَلُكَ حُبَّكَ وَحُبَّ مَنْ يُحِبُّكَ، وَحُبَّ عَمَلٍ يُقَرِّبُنِي إِلَى حُبِّكَ". وَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنَّهَا حَقٌّ فَادْرُسُوهَا وَتَعَلَّمُوهَا" فَهُوَ حَدِيثُ الْمَنَامِ الْمَشْهُورُ وَمَنْ جَعَلَهُ يَقَظَةً فَقَدْ غَلِطَ وَهُوَ فِي السُّنَنِ مِنْ طُرُقٍ.

وَهَذَا الْحَدِيثُ بِعَيْنِهِ قَدْ رَوَاهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ مِنْ حَدِيثِ "جَهْضَمِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ الْيَمَامِيِّ" بِهِ. وَقَالَ: "حَسَنٌ صَحِيحٌ" وَلَيْسَ هَذَا الِاخْتِصَامُ هُوَ الِاخْتِصَامُ الْمَذْكُورُ فِي الْقُرْآنِ فَإِنَّ هَذَا قَدْ فُسِّرَ وَأَمَّا الِاخْتِصَامُ الَّذِي فِي الْقُرْآنِ فَقَدْ فُسِّرَ بَعْدَ هَذَا وَهُوَ قَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى:

---

## 38:71-85 — verses 71-85 (shared commentary)

### Translation

This story God, exalted is He, has mentioned in Surat al-Baqarah, at the beginning of al-A'raf, in Surat al-Hijr, in [Surat] Subhan (al-Isra'), in al-Kahf, and here. It is that God, glory be to Him, informed the angels before the creation of Adam (peace be upon him) that He would create a human being from clay taken from altered black mud, and He gave them the command in advance that when He had finished creating him and fashioning him in due proportion, they should prostrate to him, out of honor, veneration, and respect, and in compliance with the command of God, mighty and majestic is He. All the angels complied with this except Iblis, who was not of their kind at all but was of the jinn. His nature and inborn disposition betrayed him at the very moment he most needed to master it, so he refused to prostrate to Adam and disputed with his Lord, mighty and majestic is He, concerning him, claiming that he was better than Adam, since he was created from fire while Adam was created from clay, and fire, in his reckoning, is better than clay.

He erred in this, opposed the command of God, and thereby disbelieved. So God cast him far away, humiliated him, and expelled him from the gate of His mercy, from the abode of His intimacy, and from the presence of His holiness. He named him "Iblis" as a sign that he had become despairing (ablasa) of mercy, and He sent him down from heaven, condemned and driven out, to the earth. Iblis then asked God for respite until the Day of Resurrection, and the Forbearing One, who does not hasten against those who disobey Him, granted him respite. When he thus felt secure from destruction until the Day of Judgment, he grew defiant and rebellious, and said: {I will surely mislead them all together, except Your chosen servants among them}, just as He said: {Do You see this one whom You have honored above me? If You give me respite until the Day of Resurrection, I will surely bring his descendants under my sway, except for a few} [al-Isra': 62]. These are the very ones excepted in the other verse, which is His saying, exalted is He: {Indeed, over My servants you have no authority, and sufficient is your Lord as a Guardian} [al-Isra': 65].

Concerning His saying: {He said: Then the truth, and the truth I speak, is that I will surely fill Hell with you and with all of those among them who follow you}, a group of reciters, among them Mujahid, read the first occurrence of "al-haqq" (the truth) in the nominative case, and Mujahid explained its meaning as: "I am the truth, and the truth I speak." In another report from him: "The truth is from Me, and I speak the truth."

Others read both occurrences in the accusative case.

Al-Suddi said: it is an oath by which God swore.

I (Ibn Kathir) say: this noble verse is like His saying, exalted is He: {But the word from Me has come true: I will surely fill Hell with jinn and men, all together} [al-Sajdah: 13], and like His saying, exalted is He: {He said: Go, and whoever among them follows you, indeed Hell is your recompense, an ample recompense} [al-Isra': 63].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

هَذِهِ الْقِصَّةُ ذَكَرَهَا اللَّهُ، تَعَالَى فِي سُورَةِ "الْبَقَرَةِ" وَفِي أَوَّلِ "الْأَعْرَافِ" وَفِي سُورَةِ "الْحِجْرِ" وَ [فِي] سُبْحَانَ" وَ "الْكَهْفِ"، وَهَاهُنَا وَهِيَ أَنَّ اللَّهَ سُبْحَانَهُ أَعْلَمَ الْمَلَائِكَةَ قَبْلَ خَلْقِ آدَمَ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ بِأَنَّهُ سَيَخْلُقُ بَشَرًا مِنْ صَلْصَالٍ مِنْ حَمَأٍ مَسْنُونٍ وَتَقَدَّمَ إِلَيْهِمْ بِالْأَمْرِ مَتَى فَرَغَ مِنْ خَلْقِهِ وَتَسْوِيَتِهِ فَلْيَسْجُدُوا لَهُ إِكْرَامًا وَإِعْظَامًا وَاحْتِرَامًا وَامْتِثَالًا لِأَمْرِ اللَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ. فَامْتَثَلَ الْمَلَائِكَةُ كُلُّهُمْ ذَلِكَ سِوَى إِبْلِيسَ وَلَمْ يَكُنْ مِنْهُمْ جِنْسًا كَانَ مِنَ الْجِنِّ فَخَانَهُ طَبْعُهُ وَجِبِلَّتُهُ أَحْوَجَ مَا كَانَ إِلَيْهِ فَاسْتَنْكَفَ عَنِ السُّجُودِ لِآدَمَ وَخَاصَمَ رَبَّهُ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ فِيهِ وَادَّعَى أنه خير من آدم فإنه مخلوق مِنْ نَارٍ وَآدَمُ خُلِقَ مِنْ طِينٍ وَالنَّارُ خَيْرٌ مِنَ الطِّينِ فِي زَعْمِهِ. وَقَدْ أَخْطَأَ فِي ذَلِكَ وَخَالَفَ أَمْرَ اللَّهِ، وَكَفَرَ بِذَلِكَ فَأَبْعَدَهُ اللَّهُ وَأَرْغَمَ أَنْفَهُ وَطَرَدَهَ عَنْ بَابِ رَحْمَتِهِ وَمَحَلِّ أُنْسِهِ وَحَضْرَةِ قُدْسِهِ وَسَمَّاهُ "إِبْلِيسَ" إِعْلَامًا لَهُ بِأَنَّهُ قَدْ أبْلَس مِنَ الرَّحْمَةِ وَأَنْزَلَهُ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ مَذْمُومًا مَدْحُورًا إِلَى الْأَرْضِ فَسَأَلَ اللَّهَ النَّظِرَةَ إِلَى يَوْمِ الْبَعْثِ فَأَنْظَرَهُ الْحَلِيمُ الَّذِي لَا يَعْجَل عَلَى مَنْ عَصَاهُ. فَلَمَّا أَمِنَ الْهَلَاكَ إِلَى يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ تَمَرَّدَ وَطَغَى وَقَالَ: ﴿لأغْوِيَنَّهُمْ أَجْمَعِينَ. إِلا عِبَادَكَ مِنْهُمُ الْمُخْلَصِينَ﴾ كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿أَرَأَيْتَكَ هَذَا الَّذِي كَرَّمْتَ عَلَيَّ لَئِنْ أَخَّرْتَنِي إِلَى يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ لأحْتَنِكَنَّ ذُرِّيَّتَهُ إِلا قَلِيلا﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ: ٦٢] وَهَؤُلَاءِ هُمُ الْمُسْتَثْنَوْنَ فِي الْآيَةِ الْأُخْرَى وَهِيَ قَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنَّ عِبَادِي لَيْسَ لَكَ عَلَيْهِمْ سُلْطَانٌ وَكَفَى بِرَبِّكَ وَكِيلا﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ: ٦٥]

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿قَالَ فَالْحَقُّ وَالْحَقَّ. أَقُولُ لأمْلأنَّ جَهَنَّمَ مِنْكَ وَمِمَّنْ تَبِعَكَ مِنْهُمْ أَجْمَعِينَ﴾ قَرَأَ ذَلِكَ جَمَاعَةٌ مِنْهُمْ مُجَاهِدٌ بِرَفْعِ "الْحَقُّ" الْأَوْلَى وَفَسَّرَهُ مُجَاهِدٌ بِأَنَّ مَعْنَاهُ: أَنَا الْحَقُّ، وَالْحَقُّ أَقُولُ وَفِي رِوَايَةٍ عَنْهُ: الْحَقُّ مِنِّي، وَأَقُولُ الْحَقَّ.

وَقَرَأَ آخَرُونَ بِنَصْبِهِمَا.

قَالَ السُّدِّيُّ: هُوَ قَسَمٌ أَقْسَمَ اللَّهُ بِهِ.

قُلْتُ: وَهَذِهِ الْآيَةُ الْكَرِيمَةُ كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَكِنْ حَقَّ الْقَوْلُ مِنِّي لأمْلأنَّ جَهَنَّمَ مِنَ الْجِنَّةِ وَالنَّاسِ أَجْمَعِينَ﴾ [السَّجْدَةِ: ١٣] وَكَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿قَالَ اذْهَبْ فَمَنْ تَبِعَكَ مِنْهُمْ فَإِنَّ جَهَنَّمَ جَزَاؤُكُمْ جَزَاءً مَوْفُورًا﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ: ٦٣]

---

## 38:86-88 — verses 86-88 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says: Say, O Muhammad, to these polytheists: I do not ask you for any reward for this conveyance and this sincere counsel that you would give me from the goods of worldly life. {Nor am I of those who take things upon themselves that are not required of them (al-mutakallifin)}, meaning: I do not add anything to what Allah sent me with, nor do I seek any addition to it. Rather, whatever I have been commanded I have delivered, neither adding to it nor subtracting from it. I only seek by that the face of Allah, Mighty and Majestic, and the abode of the Hereafter.

Sufyan al-Thawri said, from al-A'mash and Mansur, from Abu al-Duha, from Masruq, who said: We came to Abdullah ibn Mas'ud, and he said: O people, whoever knows something, let him speak it, and whoever does not know, let him say: Allah knows best. For it is part of knowledge that a man says, regarding what he does not know: Allah knows best. For Allah said to your Prophet ﷺ: {Say, I do not ask you for any reward for it, nor am I of those who take things upon themselves.} Both of them [al-Bukhari and Muslim] narrated this from the hadith of al-A'mash with this chain.

His saying: {It is nothing but a reminder to the worlds} means: the Qur'an is a reminder for all the responsible beings (mukallafin) among mankind and jinn. This was said by Ibn Abbas. Ibn Abi Hatim narrated it from his father, from Abu Ghassan Malik ibn Isma'il: [chain] Qays told us, from Ata' ibn al-Sa'ib, from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, from Ibn Abbas, concerning His saying: {to the worlds}, he said: the jinn and mankind.

This verse is like His saying, the Almighty: {that I may warn you thereby, and whomever it reaches} [al-An'am: 19], and like His saying: {And whoever disbelieves in it among the confederates, then the Fire is his promised place} [Hud: 17].

And His saying: {And you will surely know its tidings} meaning: its report and its truth, {after a time}, meaning: soon. Qatadah said: after death. Ikrimah said: it means the Day of Resurrection. There is no contradiction between the two sayings, for whoever dies has already entered into the ruling of the Resurrection.

Qatadah said concerning His saying, the Almighty: {And you will surely know its tidings after a time}, al-Hasan said: O son of Adam, at death the certain news comes to you.

The end of the tafsir of Surat Sad. To Allah belongs all praise and grace.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: قُلْ يَا مُحَمَّدُ لِهَؤُلَاءِ الْمُشْرِكِينَ: مَا أَسْأَلُكُمْ عَلَى هَذَا الْبَلَاغِ وَهَذَا النُّصْحِ أَجْرًا تُعْطُونِيهِ مِنْ عَرَضِ الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا ﴿وَمَا أَنَا مِنَ الْمُتَكَلِّفِينَ﴾ أَيْ: وَمَا أَزِيدُ عَلَى مَا أَرْسَلَنِي اللَّهُ بِهِ، وَلَا أَبْتَغِي زِيَادَةً عَلَيْهِ بَلْ مَا أُمِرْتُ بِهِ أَدَّيْتُهُ لَا أَزْيَدُ عَلَيْهِ وَلَا أَنْقَصُ مِنْهُ وَإِنَّمَا أَبْتَغِي بِذَلِكَ وَجْهَ اللَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ وَالدَّارَ الْآخِرَةَ.

قَالَ سُفْيَانَ الثَّوْرِيِّ عَنِ الْأَعْمَشِ وَمَنْصُورٍ عَنْ أَبِي الضُّحَى عَنْ مَسْرُوقٍ قَالَ: أَتَيْنَا عَبْدَ اللَّهِ بْنَ مَسْعُودٍ قَالَ: يَا أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ مَنْ عَلِمَ شَيْئًا فَلْيَقُلْ بِهِ وَمَنْ لَا يَعْلَمُ فَلْيَقُلْ: اللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ فَإِنَّ من العلم أن يقول الرجل لما لا يَعْلَمُ: اللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ قَالَ لِنَبِيِّكُمْ ﷺ: ﴿قُلْ مَا أَسْأَلُكُمْ عَلَيْهِ مِنْ أَجْرٍ وَمَا أَنَا مِنَ الْمُتَكَلِّفِينَ﴾ أخرجاه من حديث الأعمش به وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِنْ هُوَ إِلا ذِكْرٌ لِلْعَالَمِينَ﴾ يَعْنِي: الْقُرْآنُ ذِكْرٌ لِجَمِيعِ الْمُكَلَّفِينَ مِنَ الْإِنْسِ وَالْجِنِّ، قَالَهُ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ. وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ أَبِي غَسَّانَ مَالِكُ بْنُ إِسْمَاعِيلَ: حَدَّثَنَا قَيْسُ، عَنْ عَطَاءِ بْنِ السَّائِبِ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جبير ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿لِلْعَالَمِينَ﴾ قَالَ: الْجِنُّ وَالْإِنْسُ.

وَهَذِهِ الْآيَةُ كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿لأنْذِرَكُمْ بِهِ وَمَنْ بَلَغَ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ: ١٩] ، [وَكَقَوْلِهِ] ﴿وَمَنْ يَكْفُرْ بِهِ مِنَ الأحْزَابِ فَالنَّارُ مَوْعِدُهُ﴾ [هُودٍ: ١٧] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلَتَعْلَمُنَّ نَبَأَهُ﴾ أَيْ: خَبَرَهُ وَصِدْقَهُ ﴿بَعْدَ حِينٍ﴾ أَيْ: عَنْ قَرِيبٍ. قَالَ قَتَادَةُ: بَعْدَ الْمَوْتِ. وَقَالَ عِكْرِمَةُ: يَعْنِي يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ وَلَا مُنَافَاةَ بَيْنَ الْقَوْلَيْنِ؛ فَإِنَّ مَنْ مَاتَ فَقَدْ دَخَلَ فِي حُكْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَتَعْلَمُنَّ نَبَأَهُ بَعْدَ حِينٍ﴾ قَالَ الْحَسَنُ: يَا ابْنَ آدَمَ، عِنْدَ الْمَوْتِ يَأْتِيكَ الْخَبَرُ الْيَقِينُ.

آخَرُ تَفْسِيرِ سورة "ص"، ولله الحمد والمنة.

---
